25b1: btad lani/ / bar na mi yi sgra las bya// drang khrod nyid dam khang stong ngam// gnas dben par ni yongs su bri// las mkhan ldan pa 'gas bags te// khrag gas gdong dag thugs byas la// sngags 'dra/
25b2: yis ni rtag tu bzlas// oM tsaN+Da Da ma ha roSha Na kar yaM// sarba sa twA raHhUM hUM// gtor madrag po gang yin pa// bri ba'i dus su gzhag par bya// zin nas de nyid gtang bar bya// dang por chen rtsi thams cad
25b3: la/ / rin chen sna lngar byin gyis brlab// rdo rje rtse gcig phyag rgya yis// yang dag pa ru bri bya ste// skyed byed dang ni yon bdag gi/ bsam pas yongs su bri bar bya// dkyil du pad ma bcu drug la// snying
25b4: po ze 'bru yang dag ldan/ / dkyil du gtso bo 'bar ba nyid// rgod ma'i gzugs kyis bri bar bya// 'khor la sogs pa thams cad kyang // snga ma lta bur yang dag bri// phyi rol shing la sogs pa dang // dur khrod
25b5: brgyad kyis rnam par brgyan/ / 'jigs par byed pa'i ro langs dang // lce spyad drag po'i sgra yang sgrogs// de ltar rim pa ji bzhin pas// gong ma lta bus yang dag bri// dbang bskur nas skabs gang yin
25b6: pas/ / mtshan ma'i dkyil 'khor yongs su bri// de yi bar du mi gzhan la// bris sku bstan par mi bya'o// brkyang shing ngus pa nyid la ni// byas pas thang ka yongs su brkyangs// gur dag sngon po phub byas la/
25b7: mkha' la yongs su bstan mi bya// gal te bstan par byas pa na// dngos grub 'grub par 'gyur ba med// de bas mnyam par bzhag pa yis// sbyor ba legs par brtsam par bya// glegs bam nges par bri
25b8: bar bya/ / grog dag la sor dag ni// dkyus su bcu gnyis zheng du bzhi// de yi tshad du bya ba la// khrag dang bdud rtsi lnga rnams kyis// yongs su byug par byas pa la// me long ur gyis gnan byas te/

26a1: mthing shun nyid kyis legs par bri// 'dra mkhan sbyor bar ba ldan pas/ sU gu lcags las byas pa yi// snod ni thod par yang dag sngar// gter ma yang dag pa shams byas la// hUM ga~M dge
26a2: rtag tu brjod/ / gos dag sngon po bgos byas nas// rgyan cha lnga yis rnam par brgyan// mau gzhan la ni mi bstan cing // glegs shing ngus pa'am glang chen gyi// bso dag la nges par bya// theg pa bram ze
26a3: mo yi ni/ / sgra yis yongasu bsdam par bya// yang na yang chen lpags pa la// mnyen par bya bas yongs su bsdam/ der ni lag g.yon ston gyi bar// de nyid dag gi yongs su smra// sangs rgyas lnga yi bdag po
26a4: mchog/ nges par rdo rje don po nyid// sdang ba thams cad 'dul byed cing // dngos su dpa'abor ba 'bar ba// chen pa yon chen po nyid// kur la mkha' 'gro che po ste// sku chen rab dag 'jigs
26a5: ba'i gzugs/ / mkha' ltar mnyam la phyag 'tshal bstod// las la 'jug par snang ba nyid// kun bsdus pas ni de brjod bya// lag na rdo rje do rngon po can rdo rje me lce'i rgyud las bris sku dang glegs pa ma
26a6: gyi le'u ste bcu bzhi pa'o/ / / lag na rdo rje gos sngon gyis bcom ldan mgon la 'di skad gsol// gang shig rgyud 'di las sbyor bas// thabs kyi yan lag sna tshogs pa// yang dag rgyas pa
26a7: gsung du gsol/ / bde gshegs mchog gis bka' stsal pa// rang ba'i rang bzhin can gyi mis// 'di nyid la ni mngon par bsgrub// klu gdug 'bar bas zin pa ni// nub mon par gyur pa dang // yan lag drag
26a8: bar na ba dang / / smin ma la sogs byi ba dang // lus la sha ro khol par gnas// tshigs sun zhing chags par ldan// snying mi dga' dang da// ral dga'// klu yi nad du shes par bya// bkla

26b1: dmar ba mthong ba dang / / bral ba na sags mtshan marba// bum gzhan du thong ba dang // skyes pa snga ser mi bdag/ klu ma mtshan smra bstan pa yin// khrub la dga' gang skud pa 'khal// rang la yongs/
26b2: su dang che ba// tshangs pa'i nang du shes par bya// sA log yang dang lag sbyar dang // tho rangs na pa gang yin pa// zas ma za dang snying 'phar ba// tshangs pa'i gdon du rig par bya// rkang pa brkyad dang nyal la
26b3: dga'/ / sen mo bye dor byed pa dag/ tshangs pa'i nang du shes par bya// ru mo srur ba rmi ba dang // we 'u byi la mthong gyur na// tshangs pa'i mtshan mar bstar ba yid// merga ra ba mthong ba dang // shar
26b4: phyogs ri la 'dzeg pa dag/ tshangs pa'i rtags su bstan pa yin// dbugs dag mang du 'dren pa dang // bral zhing spyi bor lag pa 'dung // sdug par byed cing shal dga'// gshin rje yin gdon tu bstan//
26b5: rkang pa sa la brdebs pa dang // mkhal sogs g.yas pa'am g.yon pa na// gshin rje'i nang du rig par bya'o// tshig pa za dang gzhan la rgol// mi gzhan can mngon par sdang // sdung rag rab tu mi bde dang //
26b6: thag pa dag las 'dud pa 'dor// gshin rje'i gdon du shes par bya// glang dang sha ba mis pa dang // gos dag sngon bo lus la gyon// gshin rje yin mtshan ma yin// shing la 'dzegs pas phyir lhung dang /
26b7: g+han zhugs pa gang sleb// de ni gshin rje'i mtshar ma yin// mig ca rgod cing lngalbu ba skyug/ 'khrur ba 'bud cing brang la rdung // gnod sbyin gdon du shes par bya// yang yang ldang zhing rngam bzod// kha nas
26b8: lce ni rkyong ba dang / / lus la bsku brug byed pa dang // gnod sbyin gdon du shes par bya'o// lto ba na zhing bas la dga'// rgyab du gzer ba gang yin pa// gnod sbyin nang du shes par bya// rta sngon dag la zhon pa dang /

27a1: bong bu la zhon rmib rnams// gnod sbyin mtshan ma yin par bshad// bya rog lag par thogs pa dang // thag pas lus 'khyud nyal bar rmis// gnod spyan mtshan mar rig par bya'o// spos tshul
27a2: ni sngags btab nas/ / byin na len par mi byed pa// tshangs pa'i gdan du shes par bya// yungs dkar nyid la rab sngags nas// lag par byin pas mig ma lta// gshin rje'i gdan du shes par bya// sha
27a3: lasngags kyis rab bsngags nas/ / kha ru byin pas sna 'gags pa// de klagadodangs par gsal// skud pa sngon po nyid la de// rab sngags mdud pa bdun pong ba// mgul du bcings pas ga ngan 'dod/
27a4: gnod sbyin gdon du yin par bshad// chos po dag ni phrad pa na// sbyor ba 'di yis yang dag sbyor// dur khrod mi gang bsregs pa yi// sna tshogs thal ba blang byas la// chang dang nges par spras byas te// sbrul
27a5: kyigyi lpags pas btums byas la/ / til gyi gang bu grags pa la// 'bum du yang dag bzlas pa ste// bdag nyid gos la yang dag btum// de nas de dang phrad pa na// drag po las kyi sbyor ba yis// de nyid lan
27a6: phog par gtor/ / de yis de la gtor ba yi// de ni rengs dang rmongs par 'gyur// oM ma nu Sha duSh+Ta staM b+ha na hAM// sgyu ma dbang du sdud byed na// sbyor ba 'di nyid brtsam par bya// ngos 'jam rdul dang zla ba dang /
27a7: bgegs kyi gnyen po'i khu ba dang // sgog chen las kyi khu bas su// byed pa gnyis ka bar spras la// de la 'thun pa nyid la ni// yongs su bskul bas sbyin par bya// de nas nges pa dus btab la// kha sbyor
27a8: ba yis yang dag bsngags/ / oM na ma kA mde pa ya ya ya ka ya ka ka la sin tsa b+ha g+ha bi pa ra ta na swA hA// a mu kaM/ 'bum du dang por bsnyen pa yis// sbyor ba nges par spyad par bya// nor dag bsgrub par 'ad

27b1: pan/ / nor 'dzin lha mo yongs su bri// kha dog ser po nyid la ni// phyag bzhi par ni bri bar bya// zhal gcig nu ma 'bur ba la// g.yas kyi dang po ting 'dzin pa// gnyis pa 'bras kyi snyem 'dzin// g.yon gyi
27b2: dang po nyid na ni/ / rin chen 'bar ba yang dag bsnams// gnyis pa ne le'i rgyal pa bsdams// de lta bu yi gzugs byas la// sna tshogs dri yis yang dag mchod// mchod pa rnam pa lnga dag dang // na bza'
27b3: dang la sogs pa yis/ / yang dag pa ru mchod par bya// zhag grangs brgya rtsa brgyad pa ru// yongs su bsnyen pas sngags bzlas bya// de nas grub par gyur pa'i rtags// de nyid g.yo bar gyur pa yin//
27b4: de grub rten ni rnyed par ni// de yis lung ni ston par 'gyur// de nas dbyig ni mi bzad pa'i// bdag por mi de nges par 'gyur// ma rungs pa dag spror gzhug na// sbyor ba 'di dag nges par brtsam// de yis kun grags//
27b5: nyid dang ne// khu chen sa la sogs pa la// sngags 'di yis ni 'bum du bzlas// de nas bsnyen pa yongs rdzogs pas// yid ches dung la spu gucan// sor bdun dag la dug zugs te// skud pa sngon pos rab bcing
27b6: la/ / nub phyogs dag tu nges par bdags// de na 'byung bas bskyod pa ni// mi de nges par spro bar 'gyur// oM ma hA kA la ya sta~M b+ha u na ma ta ya// a mu kaM san tsa la swA hA// mi rnams nges par mi gsal bas//
27b7: rdo rje mo ni yongs su bsgrub// sa la phyogs bzhi mtshams brgyad du// re mig bcu gnyis bris byas la// ma rig la sogs rtags kyi ni// dngos po yang dag bri bar bya// de nas sngags pas rab bsngags
27b8: la/ / bsam pa rab tu rdzogs byas la// de nyid dngos po gang yin pas// bsam pa sbyar bas me tog bor// gang du bab pa der gnas la// shes rab can gyis rnam par dpyod// bzang ngan bltas rnams yongs

28a1: su bshad/ / rig pa legs par sbas pa yis// ba yi lAbs rab ba tums la// dang por gnyis su shes par bya// ring du bye brag med pa yis// bcom ldan sngon du bzhag byas te// dang por
28a2: mchod pas yang dag mchod/ / smod dag yongs su btsugs pa yis// shes rab bcu gsum bdag nyid can// dmar be gos kyis brgyan byas te// khrus dag legs par byas pa dang // dri yis legs
28a3: par byug byas la/ / dpral bar thig le dmar po gdab// me tog dri zhim dmar po nyid// de yi lag tu sbyin par bya// de yis de la blang bar bya// de nyid dngos po gsal bya ste// bza' ngan bltas su nges
28a4: par ston/ / spyir na sna tshogs gdon la ni// 'bad pa chen po'i sngags bzlas bya// gu gul nag po'i dud pa dag/ de yi sna ru bdug byas la// yungs kar gu gul me tog dang // de yi snying pos bsreg par
28a5: bya/ / de yis nad pa gang yin pa// bgegs dang nges par bral bar 'gyur// srin lag nyid la skud pa ni// sngon pos yang dag bsdam par bya// spyi bo'i skra las srad bu gang // bcings pas sngags na
28a6: nges par bzlas/ / 'khrug pa'i sde dag rgyal 'dod na// khams gsum rnam rgyal snying po yis// 'bum du bzlas pas bsnyen pa bya// de nas a mra'i lo ma las// yung bas yongs su bri byas la//
28a7: 'gi wang gis ni rab tu bsku// cod pan spyi bor btums byas la// rang nyid sku ru bsgoms byas la// lag pa g.yas pas yungs kar dang // ske tshe thal bar sbyar byas la/ sngags bzlas sdig 'dzub
28a8: phyar ba yis/ / yongs su bris par sde rgyal 'gyur// rnal 'byor pa yis bdag nyid la// 'chi ba slu ba yang dag bya// bdag gi rgyud la 'chi bltas ni// phyi nang bcu gnyis yang dag ldan// bdag gi zang /

28b1: la sha mtshan dag/ dmar por byung bar gyur pa na// sum bcu gnyis zhag 'chi 'gyur bas// rig pa'i rgyal po'i sngags kyis su// til la bsregs thugs stong du ni// tshang bar byas pas de bzlog 'gyur// de dang
28b2: cha mthur gang yin pa/ / rkan la 'bru ba gsum pa dang // lce yi rtse mor sme ba dang // rdo rje lam nas khrag 'dzag dang // 'dzag gnyis dbugs dag gsum pa dang // ri yi rtse mor shub byung // nang gi 'chi bltas nges pa ste//
28b3: stag dang byi ba 'brug dag dang // rtsangs pa bya gag nag po ru// yongs su sbyor bas rig pa bzlas// 'gi wang 'ug pa ru sbal dang // tsam pa ka dang ud pal dang // seng ldeng phur bu gang yin dang // 'ag pa'i sgrol sbyor
28b4: ba dang / / bya rog mkha' la 'phur ba yi// dkar pos bdag la phog pa na// phyi yi 'chi bltas yin pas na// gong du grags pa'i sar song la// rig pa la sogs sbyor ba yis// yongs su bzlog par bya ba yin// mkha'/
28b5: la sna lnga mthong ba dang // tshu la mig gzugs mthong gyur na// shin tu sdig pa'i bltas su bstan// rmi lam la ni stag zhon la// mchod rten nyid la 'dzeg pa dang // seng ge'i khar ni bzhugs rmis pa// yongs su
28b6: sdig pa'i bltas yin pas/ / logs shig sor mo rtse gsum dang // bse ru'i phyogs dang kun da'i 'dab// yon tan rgya mtsho'i mtshan bzang dang // skye mched 'phags lam chu srin sod// lo gsum zhag bzhi
28b7: zla ba lngar/ / ri de nges par 'chi bas na// rig pa'i rgyal mo bdud rtsi 'khyil// rten 'brel yige brgya pa yi// sngags kyis sman la bsrung bar bya/ khams gsum rnam rgyal 'jig rten mgon// de dag gi'ini snying po
28b8: yis/ / stag sogs gsol nges par bzlas// rma bya chen mo'i sngags dag gis// 'ug pa'i sgo sogs nges par sngags// phyag na rdo rje 'jam dbyangs dang // stobs chen khro bo gang dag gis// sngags kyis seng

29a1: ldeng 'ag sgo dang / / ku sha byil la sogs dang // gsob la sngags pa yongs su bzlog/ gtor ma sbyin bsreg las kyis ni// yongs su bzlog par bya ba yin// shin tu dpa' dang dad par ldan// shes
29a2: rab che dang thos pa bsags/ / bla ma la gus gtong bar pod// ltung ba mgos gtsang ma la// rim pa bzhin du dbang bskur nas// tshogs kyi 'khor lo lnga byas la// shes rab ldan la bstan bya ba'i// gsang ba
29a3: drag po'i rgyud rgyal 'di/ / gzhan la bshad par bya ba min// gsang ba bdag po khyod kyis ni// phan dang gnod bya gang yin la// rim pa bzhin du shes pa yis// legs par spa dang bshad pa ni// gnas skabs
29a4: du ma dang ldan zhing / / kun la nges par zhugs pa yis// rgyud 'di la ni nges par brtag/ rgud 'di gang na gnas pa na// sa phyogs de yi gdug pa rnams// ring du bsrings pas gnas mi byed// gal te gnas
29a5: par byed pa na/ / de rnams kun gyi rgyud tshig 'gyur// drag po rgyud kyi rgyal po la// gang zhig zhugs par gyur pa la// dug gsum sku la rab brgyan nas// btsun mo'i b+ha ga la gnas te// nyon mongs 'khor gyis rab
29a6: bskor nas/ / bde ba chen po'i rol pas gnas// lag na rdo rjes de nyid du// skad cig tsam gyis bskor ba ni// 'bum phrag gsum du rab bskor nas// bde bar gshegs la 'di skad gsol// bdag gis
29a7: rgud kyi rgyal po 'di/ / nges pa'i don dang rab sbyar nas// gsang ba nyid du sba bar bgyi// lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gnod sbyin drag po'i rdo rje me lce'i rgyud las las sna tshogs kyi le'u ste bcwa lnga pa'o//
29a8: phyag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gnod sbyin drag po chen po rdo rje me lce'i rgyud kyi rgyal po rdzogs s+ho// // rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen da na kI ra ti dang // bod kyi lo ts+tsha ba dge tshul khyud grags kyis bka' drin gnos nas rgya

29b1: mang su / / na sum 'as rdzu sa sum sa sams de su nas shi mi su sa laso// / rdza sa rje ldan ga gags dang /
29b2: sa sa na/ sa y-i pa ma su ma can ba zang ma/ khanam lan 'das dpal na bal/ gzugs kyi tshogs sa bldanas sa//
29b3: dad pa dpa' ra yang thugapas 'das sus m+b+hal ta// sa maldan 'das gas pa'i dag pa bsgrub pan la ltar ba rdza ga lags// tsam ldan das kyis pag 'phrul ba/ nga rje lan
29b4: rab / / bzod dang ldan zhing brtson 'grus te// byenang gsang ba'i dbang thob cing // bsgrub pa gsum la rab tu gnas// das ni dnga' ba yang dag 'grub// gsang ba bstan pa'i rgyud las bsgrub pa gang zag bstan pa
29b5: la'u ze dang po'o/ / yang dpa' mos gsal pa/ bcom ldan 'das dpa' ba 'di bsgrub pa'i gnas jel bu lags// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal ba/ dben la nyams dga' ying 'ab// bkra
29b6: sa dpal 'bal dbang yang 'dzan/ / drar khrong pan pa 'jigs gnas pa// rig sum ze'i ma tha ngas/ khro ba'i na byang 'draba'i gnas// dedo ni 'ab bsgrubal shis// gsang babastan
29b7: byung las sgru pa'i gnas brtan pa'i lal ste gnyis par/ / yang da' bas gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das dpa' 'a 'di bltud pa'i migs pa 'i thalags// btsam lan das
29b8: kyis ba 'phrul ga/ dang po gang shing bdag med// nang zhing srid pa'i chos rnams kun// ra ba nyid byas rnam par dag/ del bu mchos nyid pa// sangs rgyas sems can gnyis med pas// ma skam mi tog sdang la

30a1: gsal/ / nam mkha' mtha' med mkha' mnyam dbum 'ad// sems kyi rang bzhin de lta bu// de ltar ma rtogs sems can la/ sdug bsngal kun dang bral bas// thugs na phyogs med pasgom par
30a2: sangs rgyas thams cad 'byung ba'i chu/ / rang gi sems ni yig hUM// yaM ge hUMgi 'phro 'dra las// gzhal yas khang dang lha yi gdan// lha yi sa bon yig las// rim pa bzhin du bskyed par bya// gas
30a3: bstan pa'i rgyud las bskyed pa'i dmigs pa bstan pa'i le'u ste gsum pa'o/ / / yang dpa' mos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das rigs sngags kyi bdag po 'di'i bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dmigs
30a4: pa ji lta bu lags/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa// skyed pa'i dmigs pa thob nas ni// rang gi snying khar ye shes sems dpa' bsgom// ye shes sems dpa'i thugs khar ni// pad ma 'dab bzhi rgya sran tsam//
30a5: dbus su nyi zla'i gzhal yas khang // gzhal yas khang gi nang du ni// a shad mar me'i rtse ltar bsgom// de la dmigs pa thob nas ni// ci yang bsam par mi bya ste// bsam gyis maM khyab de bsams nas// de la
30a6: shes thob par 'gyur/ / gsal la rtog med rig pa'i sku// ye shes zhes ni de la bya'o// gsang ba bstan pa'i rgyud las bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dmigs pa bstan pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o//
30a7: yang dpa' mos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gsang ba'i bdag po 'di'i 'khor ji lta bu lags// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ dpa' bo chen po 'di'i 'khor ni// thugs kyi 'khor ni bzhi'o// gsung
30a8: gi 'khor ni brgyad do/ / sku'i 'khor lnga brgyad nges so// gsang ba bstan pa'i rgyud las 'khor bstan pa'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// // yang dpa' mos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das dpal chen po 'di'i ri/

30b1: pa ji lta bu lags// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ oM badz+ra pA Ni hU~M hUM phaT phaT swA hA/ oM badz+rA kro d+ha nI lA~M ba ra d+ha ra badz+ra pA Ni hUM hUM phaT phaT swA hA// oM badz+ra pA Ni kro d+ha ma hA tsa Na Da ma hA ro Sha/ hUM hUM
30b2: phaT phaT swA hA/ / 'khor bzhi'i rig pa bral ba ni// oM badz+ra kro d+ha ma hA ka lA ya hUM hU~M phaT phaT/ tsin po ci dun dza/ oM badz+ra kro d+ha tri lo kr-i bi dza~M ya hUM hU~M phaT phaT/ ma ra ya tsit+ta rbang chad/ oM badz+ra kro d+ha nA ga s+phu
30b3: hUM phaT phaT/ mar ma rag ta rngubs rngubs rbad/ oM badz+ra kro d+ha kra bai ra hU~M hU~M phaT phaT/ mar ya tsho tsha tshad// dpa' bo'i 'khor lha srin sde brgyad kyi rig pa phul ba/ ma bre mar ya sod sod/ ma hA
30b4: gamar mdzod na / dzadza// ma hA da bi ma ra ya ha na ha na// ma hA ma ni ma ra ya nubs rngubs// ma hA sidaH/ ma ra ya tiSh+Tha tiSh+Tha/ ma hA yak+Sha mar ya b+hin d+ha b+hin d+ha/ ma hA dri za ma ra ya khas khas// ma hA ma ni bon d+ha ma ra/
30b5: btsun/ ma hA badz+ra hUM phaT// ma ra ya ru d+ha ruHhUM hUM phaT/ gsang ba bstan pa'i rgyud las rig pa phul ba'i le'u ste drug pa'o// / yang dpa' mos gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das dpa' bo 'di'i
30b6: phrin las kyi 'jug sbyin bsreg gis bsdu 'tshal lam mi 'tshal ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ sbyin pasreg ni rnam pa gsum ste/ da na dang gsang ba gsum/ ra ral na bzhi
30b7: bzhang bstan/ zhib dang ni rgyas par bstan// bang dang drag po'i sbyin pasreg go/ gsang ba bstan pa'i rgyud las sbyin bsreg gi le'u sa bdun pa'o// / bcom ldan 'das dpal chen pos/
30b8: de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / dpa' mo'i dbang phyug ma dang / rigs kyi lha tshogs rnams dga' mgu yid rangs te/ dpal chen pos gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// dpal phyag na rdo rje gtum po shas ba

31a1: bstan pa'i rmad rdzogs sos+ho/ / // rgya gar gyi pa Na Ni ti wal tsan dra dang / lo ts+tsha ba glan chung dang ma tshul khrims kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o// zhus dag
31a2: rgya gar skad du/ b+ha ga bAn badz+ra pA Ni gu h+ya a b+hi de sha tan tra rA dza na ma/ bod skad du/ bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gsang ba mngon par bstan pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po zhes bya ba/ dpal gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje
31a3: la phyag 'tshal lo/ / 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na// bcom ldan 'das lcang lo can gyi pho brang na/ sangs rgyas gang gA'i klu gi bye ma dang mnyam pa'i tshogs dang // byams pa la sogs pa byang chub sems
31a4: dpa'i tshogs dang / reg pa'i khro bo'i tshogs dpag tu med pa dang / lha ma yin gyi tshogs dang / gnod sbyin lnga brgya dang bcas te thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das bdud thams cad 'joms pa zhes bya
31a5: ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs so/ / de nas byang chub sems dpa' lag na rdo rjes bla gos phrag pa gcig la gzar te/ phyag 'tshal nas 'di skad ces gsol to// kye ma gsang ba'i rdo rje 'dzin// ting 'dzin
31a6: rgyal po mi g.yo las/ / cig car bzhengs te gsang ba'i mchog/ ye shes lnga yi spyod yul gyi// sku gsung thugs kyi gsang ba mchog/ ji ltar bsgrub pa'i rim pa dang // las kyi bya ba mdor bsdus te// gang
31a7: zag ji lta bus sgrub cing / / rig pa'i rgyal po mchog gyur pa// bcom ldan 'das kyis legs par gsungs zhes zhus pa dang / bcom ldan 'das mnyam par bzhag pa las langs ste/ thugs khar ye shes lnga mi phyed
31a8: ba'i rdo rje lan gsum du gsor bas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'gul ba dang / ldeg pa la sogs pa kun tu 'khrugs te/ gdug pa can 'dul ba zhes bya ba'i 'od zer bkye nas slar thugs par thim pa las rdo rje'i//

31b1: lte ba nas yum dpal mo rdo rje bde ma zhes bya ba byung ste/ rang gi ston pa la g.yas phyogs su bskor ba lan gsum byas nas/ phyag byas thal mo sbyar te 'di skad ces gsol to// khyod kyi sku gsung thugs kyi ni// gsang ba dam
31b2: pa gang yin pa/ / rdo rje 'dzin pas legs par gsungs// 'di ni rnyeng dka' rgyang chen te// rin chen lta bur 'dod 'byung ba/ grangs med tshogs las 'byung ba 'di// thugs rje'i rang bzhin stong pa las// bcom ldan khyod kyis
31b3: bshad du gsol/ / zhes zhus pa dang / zhal 'dzum pa mdzad nas byams pa rnam par 'phrul ba zhes bya ba'i 'od zer gyis 'jig rten khyab par byas te// tshur 'dus nas rang gi zhal du thim pa dang / dpa' bo rdo rje bde ma khyod// stong
31b4: pa'i rang bzhin bdag med mas/ / ji ltar zhus bzhin bshad par bya// gus par nyon la legs par zung // rdo rje 'chang gi sku gsung thugs// mi phyed stong pa'i rang bzhin las// thugs rje sna tshogs thabs tshul te/ 'di ni rab
31b5: tu rtogs dka' bas/ / 'das pa da ltar bzhugs pa dang / ma 'ongs sangs rgyas spyod yul yin// bsam gyis mi khyab rnam par dag/ brjod med mi g.yo 'dus ma byas// nam mkha' dri med chos kyi sku// dus gsum dus
31b6: med rtogs pa'i mchog/ 'di la ji ltar bstan du yod// 'on kyang snying rje'i rang bzhin pas/ thabs dang shes rab rang bzhin ni// gnyis med gnyis kyi thabs tshul rig/ 'di ni gsang ba dam pa ste// de nyid gzhan la
31b7: mngon bstan pas/ / gdul bya tshim 'gyur rgyal po bzhin// rang 'dod 'bras bu 'byung 'gyur bas// gsang ba mngon par bstan pa yi// na po na pa / ye to/ byed rdzog bi'i ma mo/ yem to// thabs dang shes rab gnyis
31b8: med pa'i/ / sna tshogs nor bu rgyud chen 'di// rang gi gsang ba dam pa yin// bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gsang ba mngon par bstan pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po las rab tu dga' ba'i gleng bzhi'i le'u ste dang po'o//

32a1: ra ma rje pa dems gsol pa// bcom ldan das rdorje 'chang chen pa byed zla ba'i gang gagis thulags// bamam ldan nas kyis bka'aphrul pa// mangs ma kyang kyis nus pa legs/ gas
32a2: bde ba'i rgyu 'byung ma/ / bdag med shes rapas yimachog/ khyod la ba shad kyis legs par rtson// nyid sgru ba'i gang ga ni// bI rje ldan ni shes pa che// bdod ldan yon 'grus bran sa mchogs/ @
32a3: gsum ldan dad pas brgyan/ / dpa' zhing gsang ba'i spyod pa shes// gus shing g.yo med skyabs gnas gsum// rtag tu mchod cing yangs pa med// lhag pa'i lhal yid ches shing // phyi nang gsang ba'i dbang thob la//
32a4: dam tshig brjodo na nges par 'dzin// de ltas sgrub pa byas gyur na// yun mi ring ba rang nyid kyi// gsang gsum la ni mkhas 'gyur te// 'bad pas thob pa'i 'bras bu ni// skal ldan de yi snying la gnas// zhes gsungs
32a5: so/ / bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gsang ba mngon par bstan pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po las sgrub pa po'i gang zag bstan pa'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o// / dpa' mo rdo rje bde mas gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das
32a6: rdo rje 'chang khyod sgrub pa'i gnas ji lta bu lags/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa// mdzes ma khyod kyis zhus pa legs// zag med bde ba'i rgyu 'byung ma// bdag med shes rab ma yi mchog/ khyod la
32a7: bshad kyis legs par nyon/ / nga nyid sgrub pa'i gnas mchog ni// dur khrod brgyad dmanye ba'i gnas// dur khrod nags kyi nang du ni// ri rtse brag ri sngon po'i mdog/ khros pa'i gzugs 'dra byad lta ba/
32a8: me tog sngon pos mdzes pa dang / ne'u sing dang ud pal nags// dben zhing yid 'ong nyams dga' ba// bkra shis dpal 'phel dbang yang 'dzin// lcang lo can dang ming 'thun pa// sna tshogs sgrub pa'i

32b1: gnas su shis/ / tshwam chu med / uma'i gnas// rgyal po'i po zung tshong 'dus dang // nyan thos la sogs 'dug gnas sa// nga nyed bsgrub par mi bya'o// smin pa'i gang bag rnams la ni// gnas sogs btags papa
32b2: ci zhig / / thams cad pad chen sangs rgyas kyi// zhing khams rol pas gnas pa yin// bde bas rigs kyis brtag par bya// bcom ldan 'das phyug na rdo rje gsang ba mngon par bstan pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po lang
32b3: sgrub pa'i gnas bstan pa zhes bya ba'i le'u ste gsum pa'o/ / / dpa' mo rdo rje bdems gsol pa// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang khyod// sgrub pa'i thabs ji lta bu lags// bcom ldan 'das
32b4: kyis bka' stsal pa/ mdzes ma khyod kyis zhus pa legs// zag med bde ba'i rgyu 'byung ma// bdag med shes rab ma yi mchog/ khyod la bshad kyis legs par nyon// nga nyid sgrub pa'i rim pa ni// snying rje chen pos
32b5: sngon 'gro zhing / / gzhan gyi don la bslab par bya// nam mkhar rdo rje can dmigs la// bde ba chen pos rnam par mchod// rgyud sbyangs sangs rgyas tshogs dag la// 'gyod pa spangs te rjes yid rang // mya ngan 'da'
32b6: la gsol bar bya/ / dam pa'i don la bskul bya zhing // rigs kyi sa bon cher bskyed la// kun la khyab bya gzhan don bsgrub// bdag gi sdug bsngal mi blta zhing // gzhan dag bde la dgod par bya// me 'obs lta bur
32b7: gnas pa yi/ / sems can kun la snying rje bsgom// spos bral gnyis 'dzin spangs pa yi// tshul la yang dag bslab par bya// sangs rgyas sems can gnyis med cing // dang po stong zhing bdag dang bral// snang
32b8: zhing srid pa'i chos rnams kun/ / ngo bo nyid kyis rnam par dag/ mtha' bral mkha' 'dra dbu ma'i don// de lta bu yi chos nyid la// sems kyi rang bzhin gnyis su med// ma rtogs log pa'i sems can la// sdug

33a1: bsngal ban dpral ba'i phyir/ / snying rje chen po bsgom par bya// rang gi sems nyid yi ge hUM// sangs rgyas thams cad skyed pa'i ma// chu skyes thabs dang shes rab ldan// mtha' gnyis spangs pa gangan dang
33a2: bcas/ / gnyis med rdo rje'i rang bzhin te// snying rjes sbyangs nas gsum pa rdzogs// sku mdog nag po zhal cig pa// phyag gnyis g.yas pa rdo rje 'dzin// snun pa'i stobs can rdo rje 'bar// g.yon pas dril bu dkur
33a3: bsten te/ / sgeg pa'i tshul can nam mkhar gdengs// rin chen chu 'dzin rgyan dang ldan// stag lpags dar gyis skul brgyan// g.yas bskum g.yon brkyang bdud la rdzis// spyan gsum gsum pa'i mche ba gtsigs
33a4: bskal pa'i me 'od nang du bzhugs/ / yi ge gsum gyi gnas gsum po// ltar byas skye mched byin gyis brlab/ gnas su khro ba'i yig 'bru bskyed// sprul pa dpag med phyogs bcur 'gyed// yi ge bzhi yis ye shes
33a5: rab/ / rigs bdag la sogs sangs rgyas kyis// dbang bskar byin brlabs cod pa nabs pa// de yi ting 'dzin 'byung ba'i d+ha/ cho ga gsum pa'i sems dpa' yis// gzhan de d+ha/
33a6: mi 'chang bar bsgom// yang na gsung gi yig 'brus mtshan// 'phrin las thogs med rnal 'byor bzlas// 'di ni rnam dag rig pa ste// rtag tu ma nyams 'bras bur ldan// bcom ldan 'das phyag na rje
33a7: gsang ba mngon par bstan pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po las dpa' bo gcig pa bsgrub pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o/ / dpa' mo rdo rje bde mas gsol pa// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang gi dkyil
33a8: 'khor bsgom pa'i thabs ji lta bu lags/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa// mdzes ma khyod kyis zhus pa legs// zag med bde ba'i rgyu 'byung ma// bdag med shes rab ma yi mchog/ khyod la

33b1: bshad kyis lags par nyad/ / gang cag sa yis ltung bsams nas// snying khar nya ma'i rig pacu// 'ad kyis rang gzhan stong bcud nams// stangs te sangs rgyas sa la bzhugs/ 'ad zang gnyis pas sa
33b2: rgyas dang / / byangasems dkyil la'o sa ste// phyag bya hA las lham bsam// me tog la sogs pas mchod la// tha dad pa yi mchod pa che// de 'od dpag med lha ma yis// reg byab mi dad pas mchod/
33b3: sdig bshags rjes su yi rang dang // gsol zhing skyabs 'gro bdag lus dbul// sems bskyed dge ba bsngo bar bya// de rjes dang po byams pa ste// gnyis pa snying rje gsum pa dgal// kun gyi mtha' la btang
33b4: sems so/ / byung bani sngags kyis byi nang kun// seng bar byas te rang lus kyang // dbang po'i gzhu 'dra srid 'dzin gyi// gnas su rngubs med 'od bcas// tsa ma las byung ba'i 'khor lo te// rtsibs bcum ni
33b5: nyi ma bsapa/ / dbus su hUM las gnod mdzes bskyed// de las hUM 'phros khro bcu yang // rang rangs la gsal bar skyed// sngags pas bgegs med kyis shig par/ de la bka' lung bsgo bar bya// zhal bzhin
33b6: gsang sngags dran pa yis/ / mthe bong sdig 'dzub sbyar nas ni// phyogs bcur brda ni bstan par bya// oM su~M b+ha ni suM b+ha hUM hUM phaT/ oM grih+Na gri h+Na hUM hUM phaT/ oM grih+NA pa ya grih+NA pa ya hUM hUM phaT/ oM a na ya
33b7: b+hag bAn bid+ha rA dzA ya hUM hUM phaT/ sngags kyi rgyal po 'di brjod pas// lus ngag sems las byung ba yis// bgegs kun gyen mgo stengs su// rdo rje phur bu gzugs par bya/ oM b+haka u0f7f ta pa~Mma~M b+ha ta yas rba Sh+Tha na badzin
33b8: hUM hUM phaT/ kI la ya kI la~M ya sarba pA be A dz+nyA ba ya ti/ kA ya bA ga tsi ta badz+ra ki la ya hU~M phaT/ rdo rje thobs brdung bya ste// oM badz+ra mu dag ra badz+ra kI la ya A ko Ta ya hU~M phaT/ spyi bor btab pas nges par rlag/ sla

34a1: 'dus byags ma thams sa lus par/ / sagan dang // bu sa pa dang tha dang // da nam 'du ya nas/ sa parna ma ya tatanan rdza/ mas gra
34a2: oM brdab tsar rdum hUM/ / oM badz+rab rten rmumahUM/ oM sha ra dz+wa la tras tra/ oM badz+ra dz+wa la a na lan hU~M ma pas brjod la snying rnga yi// bdag nyid gzhan la phan 'dod pa// smon lam las byung rngu 'phrul mchog
34a3: las byung bga'u 'dra ba/ / sngon po bdan ldan pa bsam// de steng du byung rgod ma'i la// grug sum dmar po 'da'ab rab// ba las skyes pa zlum po ste// dkar po 'khyil ba'i tshul du bas ma// de las skyes pa dbang chen
34a4: lam skyes ser po rdo rje'i rgyu/ / grub zhi 'od thar 'bar ba bsam// de steng tsam las chos 'khor lo// lte bar brum las gzhal yas khang // gru bzhi sgo dang rta babs bcas// drab byed dang drabs brgyan// phre
34a5: ba rin chen rdo rje dang / / mdzes pa'i ba dan bcas pa bsam// de nang baM las chu skyes ni// ge sar 'dab mar bcas pa'i ste// nyi ma kA li 'od 'bar che// steng du zla ba A li ba sil// kha sbyar bar dud+hU dang a// nag cing
34a6: dmar ba'i rnam pa la/ / de las pad ma rdo rje bsam// slar yang yi ges 'gro ba sbyangs// hUM gis mi bskyod thugs rnams bsdu// a yis 'od dpag gsung bsdus la// gnyis med zhu bas sprul pa bsdu// rdo rje las
34a7: ni khro bo ste/ / pad mas khro mo'i rnam par bskyed// khro bo mthing ka zhal gcig pa// rang 'od las byung phyag gnyis 'khyud// rdo rje dril bu thabs shes rab// g.yas dang g.yon du bsam par bya// dbu rgyan la sogs rin
34a8: chen ldan/ / dbu skra kham ser gyen du 'bar// nag po sbrul lus klu chen brgyad// sku smad stag gi lpags pas dkris// chos gos sngon pos stod dkris te// mche ba gtsigs shing spyan gsum dmar// 'dod

34b1: dgur sbyar zhing brkyang bskum zhabs/ / mtha' gnyis spangs pa'i steng du bzhugs// de lum rdo rje bde ma gro// dmar ldang nal gces bya gnyis ma// g.yas pa gri gug lab la 'khyud// g.yon pa zod pa ba de bster/
34b2: gnyis med g.yon gyi phyogs nas 'khril// rdo rjes sbyor ba'i sgras bskul te// shar phyogs pad mar tizla las// dz+wa las khams gsum rnam par rgyal// dkar po nal gcig phyag bzhi pa// g.yas pa rdo rje
34b3: gsum 'dzin/ / g.yon ba rji du po / 'i can na kyang // 'byung ba'i nus pa 'joms par byed// go phyogs nyi ma do stengs su// hUM las rlung ba'i legs ldan gan// g.yas pa gri gug g.yon thong pa// zhabs
34b4: gnyis kya nas yod cing ldar/ / dgra thogasod pa'i las la brtson// nub tuklu 'dul bdud rtsi 'khyil// ljang zhun la gcig phyag zin no// gams pa rdo rje bya zhung dang // gson pa dbyug to bur ba bsngams//
34b5: thon tu mags pas su gsol// byang du thalas namathos bu// nal gcig phyagaganyis tham nyis su// mag ser gsas pargyam mtshan rnams// g.yon pas nod byin zung ba ste// dngum bas
34b6: don la brtson/ / sgomatshams lha yi rang bzhin la// ye shes spyan drangs mchod pa gam// ngan yig pa ni sbyor yin// lus ngag sems ma yin so// sgra yi mtshan ma gdab par bya// sde mched ltar byas ting 'dzin no//
34b7: nus pa mi shegs par b.las la// ya shes lnga 'dus migabasam// de ma dkyis spyan drangs pa'i// rigs lnga rnams 'jug byin rlabs kyis// mi bstod rdo rje dbang bsku // gsang ba shes rab mi
34b8: rgyas gad pa rigs la can pa'i/ / phyag rgya tshal rigs med do// 'di ni gsang rtson tu sgrub pa// rim gyis gsapa zhing rnam par dag/ rdo rje 'dzin pa'i sku thob pa// tshigacig nyid la 'gyur ba yin/

35a1: rtag tu goms pa'i sbyor ba yis// sa sogs 'jig rten ma lus kun// skad cig nyid la dbang du 'gyur// gtsug na rin chen la sogs pa'i// gdug pa can rnams snying yang 'byin// dga' bo
35a2: la sogs klu chen rnams/ / rtag tu de la 'dud par 'gyur// nad kyi rigs kun ma lus 'joms// gnod sbyin mo yis bka' nyan mi/ lha srin ma lus bran du 'gyur// 'di ni gsang ba dam pa ste// mdzes ma khyod la bsha
35a3: pa yin/ / bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gsang ba mngon par bstan pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po las dkyil 'khor bskyed pa'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// / dpa' mo rdo rje bde mas gsol pa// bcom ldan 'das
35a4: rdo rje 'chang gi rig pa'i gsang sngags kyi don ji lta bu lags/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa// mdzes ma khyod kyis zhus pa legs// zag med bde ba'i rgyu 'byung ma// bdag med shes rab ma yi mchog

35b1: ga d+ha ma ni/ bi si ma d+ha nA ga sha ri ra/ bi s+pho Ta ya rA ga rA ni/ tad ya thA/ oM A hU~M phaT/ nA ga bi dar NA ya hU~M/ nA gad sad rA ya hU~M phaT/ nI lA ba sa nA ya hU~M phaT/ a pra ti ha ta bal par kra ma ya hUM phaT/ kri tAn tA ya phaT/
35b2: kri tAn ta rA bA ya phaT/ ro Sha nA ya phaT/ dA sa nA ya phaT/ kus+sa Na Dod sa da nA ya phaT/ pre ta bi shAtsa bi nA sha ka rA ya phaT/ yak+Sha a ba sma ra bin sha kar ya phaT/ ha sa ha sa/ dA ra dA ra/ mA ra ya mA ra ya/ nA sha ya/

36a1: swAta ra/ / shAhwA hral dril// da mad ma// bab pag// ga ga / dar dar zad zang // khaH// baT/ thus thus/ dar dAr d+ha/ has tas/ te ba tab/ kr-i tata Tha ta/ khrag kyi khrag/ tshal bachal pa// zad yang nad
36a2: ling / / srog tshig nan rbad// lus dul mA ra ya rbad/ raM raM dz+wa la gi gi/ rdul bun rbad sod/ nA ga mA ra ya hU~M phaT/ dzaHhU~M ba~M hoH/ d+harmaka ka ki ti ra/ d+ha te/ nun te/ ta/ pat+ta rme ga tsa ka ra/ d+harma te sha sa ma ya/ bud N+Da
36a3: prata pa/ te pa te pa kha khA ra// te pa te pa ka tsa pa~M/ te ba te ba mun du ri// te pa te pa bustaM ta ra// te ba te pa sa mr-i dza~M/ kang mun du ra khe/ badz+ra tsa man ran dzA drA// te sha ra~M/ mun du nan/ badz+ra dzu ru dz+wa ru // dzur dzu ru sa mr-i dza dzAr+tha/
36a4: badz+ra g+he ne khe dza// badz+ra bur ni khe dza/ badz+ra mun d+ha re khe dza/ kha dza rA dza mun dur khe/ kha dza rA dza mun du ra sa muM khe/ pad ma ra ni kha dza rA dzA mun du ra dza khe/ kha dza rA dza mun du ra sa mun dza ra khe dzu dzu dza dza khA hi dza// oM kA ya/

36a8: gsol pa/ / bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang gi 'khor ji lta bu lags// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ mdzes ma khyod kyis zhus pa legs// zag med bde ba'i rgyu 'byung ma// bdag med shes rab ma yi/

36b1: mchog/ khyod la bshad kyis legs par nyon// nga yi 'khor ni bsam mi khyab// 'di tsam grangs ni sangs rgyas kyis// bskal par bgrangs kyang shes mi 'gyur// de bas nam mkha'i tshad dang mtshungs// mdor bsdus
36b2: nas ni bshad par bya/ / sku yi 'khor ni khro bo bcu// rigs lnga'i ngo bo sku gsung thugs// mi 'gyur gdug pa 'dul ba yin// thugs kyi 'khor ni rigs brgya ste// mdor bsdus sprul pa'i khro bo bzhi// gsung gi
36b3: 'khor ni dpag med kyang / / rigs drug 'dul ba'i khrung chen yin// sna tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab bo// gdul bya'i 'khor ni klu chen brgyad// gsung gis de rigs 'dul ba yin// gnod sbyin lag na rdo rje'i tshogs
36b4: lnga brgya rigs bsdus sku yis 'dul/ / thugs kyis lha srin gdug pa 'dul// byams pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyis 'dul// 'di la 'dis 'dul sprul pa'i tshogs// smon lam dbang gis byung ba ste// bsam gyis mi
36b5: khyab des 'dul ba/ / rigs la brjod par ga la nus// mdor bsdus mdzes ma khyod la bstan// bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gsang ba mngon par bstan pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po las 'khor nges par bstan pa'i

36b8: sprul pa ste/ / mche ba rnod pa'i drag pa gtsigs// pa las rgya mtsho'i ri rab sted/ yige hUM las byung ba yi// dpa' bo klu 'dul sgom par bya// su mchog nag po zhes dgu ldan// 6zhal mthing nag g.yas pa dkar //

37a1: g.yon pa dmar po de steng du// dbus dmar g.yas pa ldang ba ste// g.yon pa bcom gser dang 'dra// de steng dbus dkar g.yas pa gnag/ g.yon pa bai dUr+ya ltar sngo// thams cad spyan gsum rdo rje'i

37a7: rigs ma lus brlag mdzad pa/ / 'og min gnas su sleb par bsam// de rjes gnas gsum yigs brgyan// oM AHhU~M/ dkar dmar zhing gnag/ sprul pa go cha'i sngags bsam pa// oM hUM trA~M tI A// spyi ba

38a1: par gyur na ni/ / klu chen drug gis snying la zin// nges par sos par 'gyur ba yin// gal te mi gtong klu chen gyi// lus dang khang par bcas pa la// me dang rdo rje 'char ba yin// skad cig nyid la

40a1: de/ / 'din nam dag lags pa'i gnas// thob par 'gyur ba smos ci dgos// 'di ltar rnam par dag pa na// nyin mtshan cha yis dbye ba yis// dbyug gu chu tshod dus sbyor sogs// brtsibs rnal
40a2: 'byor dal ba'i chu/ / thams cad gcig tu bsdoms gyur na// mi rtog mnyam nyid nam mkhar dag/ 'bad med ye shes lhun gyis grub// dang po'i sangs rgyas ye shes che// khams gsum thams cad sgrol mdza
40a3: ma/ / shes rab yub la phyag 'tshal lo// mi gnas spros bral 'dus ma byas// legs rtogs bla ma mchog la 'dung // brjod par dka' ba'i rnal 'byor 'di// mdzes ma khyod la bshad pa yin// dpa' bo brtan par

40a5: par dag/ 'di ni gsang ba dam pa ste// gsang ba bla na med pa 'di// bdag med rtogs pa khyod la bshad// gzhan du gang gA'i bye ma dang // mnyam pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyis kyang // brjod par nus par nus pag
40a6: la yod/ / bcom ldan 'das phyag na rnga rdzogasang pa mngon par bstan pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po las bsam gyis ma khyab brdzogs pa'i rim pa bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu pa'o// / dpa' bo rdo rje bdems gas
40a7: ba/ / bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang gi rigs dag pa la dbang bskur ba ji lta bu lags// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ mdzes ma khyod kyis zhus pa legs// zag med bde ba'i chu 'byung ma// bdag med
40a8: shes rab ma yi mchog/ khyod la bshad kyis legs par nyon// dang por slob dpon mtshan nyid kyang // mdzes shing dul la byams sems ldan// sngags dang rgyud kyi de nyid mkhas// snyan par smra zhing gtong la dga'//

40b1: brtan zhing bden sra byams sems ldan// bsam pa shes shing gsong por smra// dam tshig ldan zhing sngags tshul mkhas// phyag rgya dkyil 'khor ba dmas mangs// de nyid bcu shes snying rjer ldan// 'jig rten pa'i
40b2: rnam spangs pa/ / mkhas pas de nyid shes nas kyang // de ni sangs rgyas kun rang bzhin// byang chub sems dang dgra bcom dang // nyan thos rang rgyal gang na med// de lta'i tham srog ltar bsten// gal te slob dpon
40b3: smod pa la/ / dngos grub rmi lam du yang med// de bas bla ma mnyes byas la// bla gos phrag pa la g.yogs te// bus gcugs thal sbyar me tog thogs// dkyil 'khor bri bar gsol bar bya// grong dang tshang 'dus
40b4: dur khrod dang / / tshal dang lha khang grong khyer te// byang shar dngos grub gzhan gnyis spangs// ro ha ta sogs zla ba yi// lto 'phye'i lto bar shes pa yin// gzhan du nyes pa 'byung bar 'gyur// mkhas pas nyes pa med
40b5: par bya/ / sa bslang ba dang brtag pa ni// rim bzhin gtsug lag khang pa dang // tshal dang rdo leb khang bzangs te// kun la brtag pa spang bar bya// slob dpon smin pas slob ma rnams// phung po lnga po dag par bya// sa
40b6: yi nyes pa kun bsal nas/ / laM las byung ba'i lha mo na// rgyan ldan bum pa phyag na bsdams// de la mchod cing gsol bar bya// oM iSh+NI hi ma hA de bi bri thi bi lo ga/ ma ti ra sarba rang na s+yo phur ni// d+hi b+h+ya u lang ka ra bu
40b7: shi te/ ha ra nu su ra nir go she/ badz+ra sad d+ya bra bu dzi te g+hi ti ti hi/ i dam arga a smin sa ni hi to b+ha ba hri hri hi hi sA hA// gnang bas sa la slar thim bsam// slar spang bsrung zhing gtso bo la// dri yi gdan chen
40b8: grub bzhi ste/ / 'khor lo sum cha dor bas zlum// me tog sngon po'i gdan la bsam// rin po che 'am sa yang rung // bum pa nag po'i skyon spangs te// bya kr-i seng kri dbyig pa yi// ud pa la gzhan gyis

41a1: mi thub pa/ / ha sa de bas nad rnams spyod// dngul dang mu tig mu men dang // byi ru gser gyis ye shes 'phel// nas gro til dang sran ma dang // mud ka yis ni lam lnga dag/ ga bur gur gum 'a
41a2: ti dang / / tsan dan a ka ru yis ni// gzhan don phrin las lnga 'grub bo// chu dang snying po lnga yis ni// rnal 'byor phun sum tshogs gyur pas// mgrin pa gos kyis dkris pa dang // 'bras ldan shing gis
41a3: kha yang brgyan/ / ku sha la dag pa mtshan ma can// rang rang phyogs su gzhag par bya// bdug pos thogs la gsol ba gdab// bcom ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa'i rgyal// bdag la dgongs nas gzigs su gsol/
41a4: slob ma rnams kyi don phyir dang // khyed rnams la yang mchod pa'i phyir// bdag ni dkyil 'khor 'dri bar 'tshal// rin po che'i mthu bzhin du// bka' drin rjes su gnang ba yi// sad ni byon par mdzad du gsol// lan
41a5: gsum bar du gsol bar bya/ / slob ma rnams la rjes brtse bas// sdom gzung gsol zhing bsrung ba dang // slob dpon rdo rje can dmigs la// gang yang gsang sngags lnga kun dang // 'jig rten skyong ba ma lus pa/
41a6: rdzogs pa'i byang chub la zhugs dang // sangs rgyas bstan dga' 'byung po dang // gang dag rdo rje'i spyan ldan rnams// rdo rje 'chang gi dkyil 'khor mchog/ deng bdag 'dri bar 'gyur ba la// bdag dang skal ldan sleb ma
41a7: la/ byin gyis brlab phyir bsrung bar mdzod// srad bu ye shes lnga yi dngas// re re'ang rigs lngarnam dag ste// chos kun de ba nyid med pas// phan tshun sngags bzlas bsgril bar bya// dkyus su 'khor lo'i nyis 'gyur
41a8: la/ / sngangs su sgo yis bcu gnyis tshad// hUM brjod bdud rtsi lngas byugs la// dz+dza dz+nyA'i sgra brjod lte bar gzung // slar yang de bzhin ye shes kyi// thig chen nam mkhar gdab par bya// de bzhin cha ldan gnyis pa yis//

41b1: gtsang zhing rdo rje 'dzin bsams ste// tshangs pa'i thig chen gdab par bya// gnyis ba zur thig la sags pa// nub dang ltar ni slab dpon la// byang shar sleb ma'i gnas pa ste// g.yas kyis bskor ba ma gtogs par/
41b2: g.yon du nam yang ma yin no// de ltar cha yis rnam par dbye// thig skud chad na bla ma 'chi// dman dang lhag pas nad du 'gyur// phyogs 'khrul na ni slob ma rmongs// de bas mkhas pas skyon med bya// rin tshon lnga'am
41b3: 'bru yi phye/ / yang na 'byung khungs las byung ba// yi ge bcu yis byin brlabs te// rigs lnga rnam par dag pa las// dkar ser dmar ljang nag po nang // dbang ldan phyogs nas bri bar bya// gal te tshon rtsi mi mnyam
41b4: zhing / / yo dang dma' bar gyur na ni// dngos grub med cing rtsod la gdung // sbom pas nad 'byung phra bas ni// nor nyams gal te chad pas ni// 'chi 'gyur g.yas bskor ma bris na// phur bus btab pa yin zhes bya// shar
41b5: phyogs dkar la lho nub byang / / ser dmar ljang khur bri bar bya// dbus ni bai dUr+ya lta bu// pad ma phyogs kyi rnam pa ste// mtshams ni mdzes tshon bum pas brgyan// sgo la sogs pa'i rgyan nams dang // dur khrod ra ba'i
41b6: nang du bri/ / gtum drag la sogs phyogs mtshams dgod// dbus mthong shar dang byang gzhol zhing // mtho zhing ma 'dres dran par bri// de nas rdo rje 'dzin dmigs la// gus pas me tog dang bcas nas// gsol ba 'di
41b7: ltar gdab par bya/ / dpal ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa che// byang chub chen po'i tshul bstan pa// mgon po chen po bdag 'tshal lo// dam tshig de nyid bdag la gsol// byang chub sems mchog bdag la gsol// sangs
41b8: rgyas chos dang dge 'dun te/ / skyabs gsum dag kyang bdag la gsol// bar pa chen po'i grong mchog tu// mgon pos bdag ni gzhug par mdzod// ces pa lan gsum bar du bya// bu chur theg pa chen po yi/

42a1: tshul can ldad da khyad man te// gsang sngags spyod tshul chog mchog/ khyod la yang dag shad par bya// rdo rje mi byed pa cu yis de// banas med pa'i sa shes 'thob// de bas kun ma khyen thob 'dod pas//
42a2: bu lis blo gros 'di gyis shig/ bla ma sangs rgyas kun mchod cing // rtsa ba yan la gnyis pa spong // mgrol ba'i sems can la// snying rje chen por rababaskyed nas// bsgral zhing grol ba'i lam la dgod// bde bar dbugs na
42a3: dbyung bar bya/ / de dag ri ma dang rim min pa// slob ma'i ris pa rnam par btag/ khrus byas shing sbyin par bya// phrin la pa phyogs dang dngos grub kyi// rim par rnam par btag par bya// bsrung srud ba dgas dang kug
42a4: sbyin/ rmi lam brtags la ngan pa ni// zhi ba'i me yis bzlog par bya// gdong g.yogs bcings la ye shes dbab// dkyil 'khor dam par gzhug pa'i phyir// sngon bsags sdig pa ma lus las// dkyil 'khor
42a5: mthong ba tsam gyis 'byang / / bu khyod su yin ci dga' ba// bdag ni skal bzang rigs yin pas// rdo rje 'dzin pa khyod la dga'// mig dbye dkyil 'khor lha yang bstan// dam tshig chu sbyin mna' yang bsgrub// me tog
42a6: dor la lta ro bstan/ / gang dang gang du ba 'gyur ba'i// rigs kyis de la spro bar bya// chu dang cod pan rdo rje de// dril bu ming gi dbang bskur te// rigs lnga'i bdag nyid ye shes lnga// brtul zhugs lung bstan rjes gnang
42a7: sbyin/ / dbugs dbyung rdo rje slob dpon bsgrub// gsang ba shes rab ye shes dang // bzhi pa brjod med dbang bskur ba// gas rab mchog gi dkyil 'khor d+ha// mchog tu rabazhugs mthong bas na// deng khyod sdig pa
42a8: ma lus las/ / rnam grol rigs su skyes pas na// sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam gsungs pa'i// rjes su gnang bas dbugs phyin 'gyur// dngos grub rgyu yi dam tshig ni// bu yis rtag tu bsrung bar gyis// slob mas

42b1: da pa/ / / dag sa// 15/ sapa@// tsa ldananas kyis pagad pa sar// rgyan nas dadang// rgyal phred da chu pa da // ragal
42b2: bla ma dang / / bsnyen bkur tshim pa med par bya// deng du bdag tshe 'bras bu yod// bdag ni gson pa 'bras bu che// de ring sangs rgyas rigs su skyes// sangs rgyas sras su bdag gyur pas// sems can dan ni mnyam
42b3: med bya/ / zhi ba'i sbyin pasreg dngos grub grogs// tshogs kyi 'khor lo dge 'dun mchod// na pa' ma mgon med phongs pa kun// kha zas kyis ni tshim par bya// zhing skyong gtor mas mnyes byas la// rang 'dod 'bras
42b4: bu gsol ba gdab/ / rjes su dam tshig spyod pa dang // skyed pa la sogs rgyun mi 'chad// rnal 'byor pas ni bsam par bya// 'di ni rig mchog dbang bskur bla na med// mdzes ma khyod la skal ldan pasgrub phyir bstan//
42b5: gzhan du rigs par drug la de yis slar zhing gnod// de phyir 'di ni dam tshig rdo rje bkod pa yin// bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gsang ba mngon par bstan pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po las slob ma dbang bskur
42b6: ba ri le'u ste bcu gcig pa'o/ / / dpa' ma rdo rje bde mas gsol pa// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang gi 'khor klu sgrub pa'i thabs ji lta bu lags// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa// mdzes
42b7: mkhyod kyis zhus pa legs/ / zag med bde ba'i rgyu 'byungam// bdag med shes rab ma yi mchog/ khyod la bshad kyis legs par nyon// gdul bya'i rigs su skyes pa yi// gdug pa'i klu tshan rnam pa brgyad//
42b8: rigs bsdus chu bdag bdun// dam tshig la gnas sog ma med// 'di dag bsgrub par 'dod pa ni// mdzes pa'i dkyil 'khor rnam lngas byug/ pad ma lha sngam sgom dang bcas// sgo rgyan ltos 'gros rab tu mdzes//

43a1: lte bar rdo rje 'dzin pa bsam// mdun du las kyi bka'anyan bskyed// pad ma brgyad la khru chen brgyad// gdeng ga bdun ldan pal sbyong bsas// lha sngam rigs bzhi'i sa bdag ste// sgo dang gra tshad rigs
43a2: kyi rim/ / mchod rdzas klu yi rtsi sman bas ma// de rjes rdo rje 'dzin pasams la// klu chen gnas nas spyan drang ste// e h+ye nA ga rA dzas pa ri b.ras ma yadza dzaH// rang rang san la bzhugs par bya// pad ma' lte bar chu ba dag
43a3: dang / dam tshigasog med dkar dang ser// thal sbyang sbrul gyi nabs su 'khyil// gtso dzAH'chang la 'dud// shar phyogs mtha' yas sngon po ste// rtswa phyags nor rgyas ser po che// nub phyogs 'jig po la dog dam pa/
43a4: byang phyogs spobs rgyu nag po ste// shar lhor ba dem dud dang 'dra// lho nub pad chen mar po ste// nub byang dung stong btsod dang 'angadra// byang shar rigs ldan dung ba'i mdog/ mjug pa 'khyil bas gtsel 'dud// sacog
43a5: gzugs ni rigs pazhi dang / / sa bdag snga tshogs gzugs kyis bskor// de dag sngags kyi ma pa ni// oM badz+ra nan ma hA do Na badz+ra pA Ni hri da yaM// nAg yas nA ti kA ma u0f7f ud sa t+yad+ha b+ha bi shra ti swA hA// rdo rje 'chang
43a6: gis grang ma tshig la gzhag pa'o/ / oM ba drA Na ye hU~M pra swA hA// oM s+'u m+b+ha ba tA ga rA dza kro d+ha dz+dza/ sid d+hi si da N+Di s+pho Ta ya hU~M pra lAH// oM anan ta trUM pra sA hA/ oM ba su ki hU~M pra swA hA/ oM tak+Sha ka trUM pra swA hA/ oM ka /
43a7: thAd+ha// sa bdas hU~M rbak+Sha// oM ma pa das ng+ge naH/ oM ga la shAm hrA~M Ta swA u0f7f// oM g+na sa ka rmAr+thak+Sha hA// 'di dgra klu'i rgyal ba rnams kyi sngags sa// rim pas mchod ci gas pa/
43a8: pa'i rgya mtsho'i gtor ma yis// klu rnams tshim pas gdug sems ni// re rjes bstod pa brjod par bya// hUM chu bdag sprul pa'i dam tshig can// mtha' yas nor rgyas la sogs klu dbang rnams// rgya mtsho chu ga ter zab

43b1: ba'i 'jing chen gnas/ / rin chen sna tshogs yid 'ong spras pa yi// gzhan yas 'byor pa phun sum gnas na bzhugs// sbrul mgo'i gdengs ka rab 'bar rin chen gas la// yid 'ong nor bu 'dod pa kun sgrub pa/
43b2: rang bzhin phun sum tshogs don rnams ster ba'i dpal// 'od 'bangs 'og mun pa ma lus sel// du ma'i bskal bar yon tan sbyangs pa yis// klu rgyal 'byor pa mchog la mnga' brnyes pa// bsam gyis
43b3: mi khyab rdzu 'phrul mchog brnyes pa'i/ / yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab khyed la bstod// sangs rgyas bka' thob dang pa'i stobs 'phel ba// sangs rgyas sar gnas sgrub la nan tan byed// thabs dang shes rab 'brel
43b4: bas gzhan don mdzad/ / bdag gzhan don sgrub khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// bde gshegs spyan sngar khas blangs dam bcas te// bstan pa bsrung zhing 'gro rnams bskyang ba'i phyir// khas blangs mna' phral dam tshig
43b5: dran gyis la/ / phrin las don gyis bdag gzhan don sgrub mdzod// gzhan yang 'jig rten pa rnams la// oM mtha' yas dang ni 'jog po dang // stobs kyi chu dang rigs ldan dang // nor rgyas bu dang drang skyong dang /
43b6: pad ma dang ni chu lha dang // rgya mtsho rgya mtsho chen po dang // dpal gyi 'od dang 'od po che// gzugs che lto 'phye sprul chen po// klu chen 'khor dang bcas pa la// mthun pa'i dam rdzas yid 'ong ba// dkar gsum mngar
43b7: gsum gso ba'i sman/ / rin chen dang dang za 'og dang // dpag bsam shing dang 'dod 'jo'i pa// sna tshogs khyed la phul ba yis// klu'i nang nam med par mdzod// phyis kyang mi byed dam chos la// so so'i gnas
43b8: su 'gro bar gyis/ / 'di ni rdo rje 'chang gi bka'// 'di las 'das na klu rgyal rnams// snying 'tshig mgo bo 'gas 'gyur te// lus la bskal pa'i me 'bar nas// sdug bsngal gyur na pa legs pas// dam

44a1: las 'da' bar ma byed cig/ nA ga rA dza sa ma ya a b+he shi nu badz+ra na nar ma hA ra Sha Na badz+ra pA Ni hU~M phaT// smanams dam tshig sgrub pa'o// de bzhin byas na kund rnams// skad cig nyid la byang 'gyur
44a2: te/ / sgrub po bde bar 'gyur ba yin// de bas 'di la brtson par gyis// mdzes ma khyod kyis zhus pa bzhin// gtan la phab pas rab tu bshad// bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gsang pa mngon par bstan pa'i rgyud
44a3: kyi rgyal po las klu bsgrub pa'i le'u ste bcu gnyis pa'o/ / dpa' mo rdo rje bdems gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang gi 'khor klu gdug pa can rnams kyi nad 'byung ba'i rtags ji lta bu lags// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka'
44a4: stsal pa/ / mdzes ma khyod kyis zhus pa legs// zag med bde ba'i rgyu 'byung ma// bdag med shes rab ma yi mchog/ khyod la bshad kyis legs par nyon// klul rigs drug la sogs pa// sna tshogs
44a5: rigs su yod gyur kyang / / 'byung ba lnga yi rang bzhin te// nor rgyas drang skyong rgyal rigs yin te// mthong ba'i dug/ ser po sa la dbang ste lci 'thibs lus po lbo// sha babs rab bzhi la khyad par na ba yin//
44a6: bcwa lnga nyin gung rgyu ba'i dus la ni// nad kyi gnas ni spyi bar nges par 'bab// rlung rtsa babs la sha rus bar du na// sgra 'byi ba rlang thabs byas napa na sten pad/ thob/ 'brel pas sha ro glo lu srung ba yin/ gar po rigs ldan
44a7: bram ze yin te bltags pa'i dug/ dmar po ma la dbang ste tsha zhing gdung // lus dmar skye chung thang la mig rtsa lus po skam// 'bring po babs sa nyi nub dgongs mon// gnam stong bcwa lnga rgyu ba'i dus te de lan/
44a8: snyiste khar babs pas snying mi dga' zhing dran pa nyams// mjug tu mgo dang lus la bab sten cha che// sharo snying la 'ong bas lce yis ro mi tshor// pad ma 'jog po rje rigs yin te kha rlangs drug/ dkar po tshul

44b1: dbang bas zang zhid bsel bar na/ / lus mdag dkar la lpags pa'i thams 'chags// brdungs babs pa yan tams brgyad bcwa brgyad na// snga dro tho rangs ma bde sbe dang dpung ba g.yas// brang na tham mchin
44b2: par babs pa'i sa yin no/ / pho bas zas mi 'ju zhing mig gis gzugs mi 'dzin// sha brul tshor ba med de cung zad sha lpags dar ra// pad chen stobs rgyu dmang rigs pa tog pa dug/ nag po rlung la dbang
44b3: pas yang zhing g.yo/ / lus 'dar sems rgod sha' phar bu shus 'debs// yan lag tshigs bzhin zhing po la dang bdakan rtse// glegs dang ro stong na ning lda ga dag kya chung // 'byung zhing yul ngal dgongs dang srod lan
44b4: tha chung zhag la 'bab ste tshes gsum bcu gsum na/ / 'di ni 'gong rigs rtsub pas skyo 'bog btsan thabs gsod// tha ma mkhal mar 'bab ste rnabs sgra mi thos// khu chu nyams pas chu sri sor mo pra// chu lha
44b5: dam tshig nam mkha' yin pas kun la khyab/ gong ma ci rigs 'byung zhing dus med shes pa zhum// lus kyi shed nyams bral te sna tshogs ston// 'di ni bcos par bka' ste gtan la phabs par bya// khyad par mcher
44b6: pan zhing gdong la sme ba 'byung / / lus la shig mang ko dri rwa gzho ba mnam pa dang / thur sel rlung la rul ba'i dri ma bro gyur la/ 'di ni mtsher bar 'bab ste chu la khrag kyang 'byung // so so'i rtags su mkhas pas shes par gyis//
44b7: spyir ni lngag gang zhugs kyang // rim pas 'di ltar 'byung bar 'gyur// me dang grog po phugs rdugs dang // ri phug dog pa'i sgo dang dod // lha khang 'dam rdzab mi sdug gzugs// dud 'gro'i tshogs dang mtsho ri gzar//
44b8: snying mi dga' zhing 'tshig pa ni// dang po 'byung bar shes par bya// glu len nub mo na dang shes pa lci// yan lag mi bde shu ba g.yan pa dang // pas ljags 'brum chung dmar sib 'od// 'khrug cing za 'phrug sha mdog

45a1: nyams/ / me ris chu drang blugs ltar grang // grang si ba tsha thig sha bkra che chung byed// sha 'phrig bem dang sbrid cing 'khol// mig zlus tsha zhing sprin ma 'bye// lag sor sen mo nyams pas pra// lus la dring
45a2: chu bur dang / / nya skangs gnag chu dul dri mnam// stod gzer slad du 'khru bar byed// phyi yi sha skams mdog nyams dri ma bral// brag pa'i sgo yo bdud rtsi dus med pa// yang cig mdor bsdus bshad pa ni// dbang po
45a3: gsal ba'i 'bras bu ni/ / mchin pa'i sgo yin mig la brtag/ rgyal mo 'khor lo g.yang ra yin// gnas pa rus pa'i 'bras bu ni// mdzes pa so yi mkhar yin pas// kha dog rkang bu nus pa blta// nus pa chu ba'i
45a4: 'bras bu ni/ / zangs mdog sen mo'i tshigs yin pas// skye lugs la dog rtsab brtag/ mdangs dang sha ye 'bras bu ni// khyab badreg pa yin pas na// chags lugs kha dog 'gyur bar blta// drod rten khrag gi 'bras
45a5: brani/ / bud med gsang sgo'i chu yin pas// kha dog ku la gzugs la brtag/ rkang dmar bcud kyi 'bras bu ni// rba ba gnas lugs skyes brtag/ de rnams thams cad rtags ldan na// ngas kyang gso bar gal nus//

45a8: ji lta bu lags/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa// mdzes ma khyod kyis nus pa legs// zag med bde ba'i rgyu 'byung ma// bdag med shes rab ma ya mchog/ khyod la bshad kyis legs par nyon// byol song

45b1: klu yis zin pa la/ / 'tshe dang mi 'tsho gnyis yin te// nges pa'i rtags chen drug tshang na// de la mkhas pas ci byar yod// rnam smin las las byung ba yin// gzhan rnams gso par 'dod pa la// dka' dang slab
45b2: gnyis yin te/ / dang po sngags kyi rim pa yin// gnyis pa rdzas dang 'brel ba yin// dang po sngags kyi sbyor ba ni// dbang bskur tshogs bcags rgyud stangs pa/ jig pa gsum gyi bsnyen pa bya// kha cig de tsam gyis kyang ni/
45b3: gal te nus pa che ba na// gsang ba drag po'i sham bu gdags// kha cig de yis 'tsho ba yin// gal te gnod tshabs che ba na// klu yi rang gi shed bzlas pa tsam// nam mkha'i klu yis snying nas gzir// rig pa
45b4: gnyis pa gsham du sbrel/ / rdo rje lte bar 'khor lo bri// de la dmigs te bsgrub par bya// dug rigs gsal bar gyur na ni// sa dug ngos zin rdo rje'i nang // dga' bo rigs ldan me'i sngags// bram ze'i 'khrul 'khor shes
45b5: pa yin/ / me la chu yi 'khrul 'khor te// de yi sngags kyis gsang bar bya// pad chen stobs rgyu rlung yin pas// sa yi 'khrul 'khor lte bar bca'// pad ma 'jog po chu yin pas// rlung gi 'khor los bsad par bya//
45b6: rang rang kha dog gshed du sbyar // gzhi snying sngags rnams dril la bzlas// gnyen po mi mthun rdzas dang sbyar// gnyen po gang yin lha yi gshed// man ngag bzhin du shes par bya// 'khrul 'khor tshar nas se ma bden/
45b7: rgyal po'i sdong zla dbye bar bya// dus tshod zhag grangs rim pa ni// rtags dang sbyar la shes par bya// rtags rjes rjes su log pa na// sbyin sreg ci rigs mkhas pas bya// phyi rjes drag pos gcod pa dang // lha
45b8: ngang rdzas kyi gegs kyis gcod/ / mnan pas las mtha' brtul bar bya// zhi ba drag po'i rim pa ni// mkhas pas rtags la bsten par bya// bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gsang ba mngon par bstan pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal

46a1: po las klu'i nad gsal ba'i le'u ste bcu bzhi pa'o/ / / dpa' mardarje bdems gsol pa// rdo rje 'chang gi gtor ma bya ba'i rim pa ji lta bu lags// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka'
46a2: stsal pa/ / mdzes ma khyod kyis zhus pa legs// zag med bde ba'i rgyu 'byung ma// bdag med shes rab ma yi mchog/ khyod la bshad kyis legs par nyon// dkyil 'khor bri dang sbyin sreg dang // bzlas pa thun
46a3: 'tshams rab gnas dang / / dbang bskur bskrad cing gsang pa dang // 'byung po khyud dang gnod sbyin dang // klu da gas spyod mchod pan// gtor ma med par gang spyad pa// las de 'bras bu med pa 'am// bar chad
46a4: nyebar skye 'gyur bas/ gtor ma'i cho ga bstan par bya// lha yi rnal 'byor ldan pa yis// phun sum tshogs pa'i 'byor pa bsag/ gtor ma'i 'og tu rlung lha yis// sa bon las skye kha dog sngon//
46a5: g.yo ba'i rlung yob dang bcas pa// de stengs rgod ma'i kha bsams te// dmar po rlung las skyes pa bsam// gru gsum hUM las rdo rje gsum// sku gsung thugs kyis brtan por bya// de steng a las pad ma che//
46a6: yangs la dkar zhing cung zad dmar// chos dbyings snod kyi gzhal yas yin// de nas sbyang ba'i sa bon las// bruM aM dz+riM khaM hUM bas te// slar yang sha lnga sbyangs pa las// me kI bA tAM baM bsams te// yum lnga'i
46a7: ye shes rnam par dag/ bdud rtsi ye shes rnam dag 'di// spyad dang spar rtogs sbyor ba yis// yi ge gsum gyi sna ldan pa// bde ba'i ro cher nyi mar gsal// 'char ba'i bdog 'dra bar 'gyur// rdo rje las

46b1: ma sbya / / mthe thong rdo rje bstan par gnas// rang 'dod dngas grub sang bzhag la// sgra ldan pas sngags 'das sbyin// a and/ sa mjal/ dzak+Sha ThA ta pan+d+ha/ ba su/ rak+Sha/ tsan da su dzA ma dpa ga/ ta
46b2: la pa ta la a dza sa ba swA hA/ i dam pa lid b+hU dze dzi g+ha phuwa/ d+hU pa mas pig/ am+b+ha kadza/ pap+pa sA ha khan ti khu Ni pheMT ga da sA hA// oM a kA ro mu khaM sarba d+harmA Ne/ A d+ya rud ba nan trad tA oM AHhUM phaTas

46b4: kyis so/ / klul dkar gsum mngar gsum dang // ci sman dang zab sna tshogs mchod// rang gi rig pa dril byas la// bstod cing gsal ba gang yin bya// d+hU khyod kyis sems can don kun mdzad// rjes su

47a1: rgyas rnams kyis bshad/ / da ltar byung ba'ang de 'chang de// ma 'ongs rnams kyang 'chad 'gyur la// nga yis kyang ni 'dir bshad de// byang chub sems ldan gang zag gis// rab dben pa yis yi char//
47a2: mchod cing bstan dga' bsnyen byas la// sangs rgyas rdo rje can mchod bya// rim pas tshangs pa'i gnas bzhi bsgom// oM swa b+hA ba shud d+ha sarba d+harma swa b+hA ba shud d+ho haM// rang bzhin rnam par dag pa bsgom// oM shUH
47a3: tAdAn dz+ra swa b+hA ba Ad ma ko ha/ / brjod med ye shes dag par bsgom// bsrung zhing gzhal yas khang pa der// mdzes ma'i pad ma la gnas pa// chos 'byung rnam dag pho brang du// nyi ma zla ba rnam dag dpal/

47a5: zhal cig phyag gnyis ma/ / g.yas pa rdo rje g.yon thod pa// g.yas su sangs rgyas spyan ser te// zhal cig phyag gnyis g.yas pa na// rin chen g.yon pas thod pa 'dzin// g.yon du dam tshig sgrol ma ldang /
47a6: g.yas pa ud pal thod pa 'dzin// rgyab tu gos dkar dmar ser te// pad ma thod pa bsnams pa'i phyag/ kun kyang khro zhing gar thabs bzhugs// rus pa rin chen rgyan dang ldan// mchog sgrub nad rnams

47a8: sha ka re shAn ting ka re/ puHk+Shur+tha/ k+ShAN+Ti ni k+ShA ta ya/ g+hA ta ya/ gAts+tshin swA twA// oM ru ru su ru dz+wal tiSha siN+Da lo tsa ni sarba ar+tha sAd+ha ni sAhA/ oM a ga te bi ka Te ni ka Te/ ka Ta ka Ta~M ka ro Ta bin+yA swA tAM/ oM tA

47b1: tu ma ma mA yu At+ma/ / rang rang las dang 'bral ba ni// 'bus 'gyur sngags kyis 'grub par 'gyur// las gzhan dngos grubs bsgrub par// lbal khyad kyis byed pa yan// 'din gsang bdam pas//
47b2: ches gsad pas kyang mchog yin no// de bas mdzes ma khyod la bshad// bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gsang ba mngon par bstan pa'i chud kyi rgyal po las yum bsgrub pa rnam par bye ba'i le'u ste bcu drug pa'o//

47b5: spyod ming dang spel bris nas/ / dgug la bcug la sngags 'di bzlas// oM tsaN Da ma hA ro Sha Na// tad ya thA/ oM tsa le pra tsa le// la lA lu te yA// de ba kam hA kA la// an tsar ya bi s+t+wa~M swA hA// khri bzlas
47b6: bas rang ci 'dod pa 'ong bar 'gyur te/ / gong bu dgug pa'o// rang nyid rdo rje 'dzin du bsams la ta la'i lo ma la ri rab kyi 'khor lo byas te// zur du hUM dang hri'i bar du bsgrub bya'i ming bri'o// lte bar sngags bri/

47b8: ma hA ro Sha Na ga ga a ra ga ka bi ta ri swA hA/ / sngags 'di bzlas la kha bkrus la// khyu mchog gi lci ba dang // lding ros bsres la rdo rje'i gzugs byas te// lte bar 'khrul 'khor bcug la dgra'i sgor sbas na

48a1: 'chi bar 'gyur ro/ / bklags pas 'grub 'gyur nus pa 'di// rdo rje 'dzin par rabazhugs nas// rdza mkhan lag pa'i 'dag pa la// rdo rje'i rnam par 'khrul 'khor bca'// oM tsa tar ma hA ro
48a2: Na che ge mo mu kha ti thAn tas/ / sa b+ha tsha na ting / b+han ting / laM g+haM laM g+haM/ mu tra mu rI she ni che ge mo b+h+yan d+ha mi swA hA// sngags 'di khri bzlas khang pa mnan// nges par shags las rgyal bar 'gyur// oM badz+ra tsaN ra ma hA

48a4: na tun ti si ra sa re/ / khaM laM khi la~M swA hA// stag ga lpags pa la bris te// gang la btegs pa'i skyang gi bsrung // oM tsata Da ma dA ro Sha Na ma rak+Sha to// na sha ka rA ya swA hA// shing thog la bzlas rabar sbas// snre
48a5: gnod pa bzlog par 'gyur/ / oM tsaN De ma hA ra Sha Na sarba staM b+hA ya dum b+he swA hA// sbrang rtsi bu ram khu ba la// 'di bzlas byugs pas dom 'bros so// oM tsaN ra ma hA roSha Na ba ra hA d+hin dr-i dr-i d+he swA hA// dug dang lan

48b1: btums la/ / oM badz+ra tsaN+Da ra ma hA ro Sha Na ga run tsa le tsa le bdud tra mA ra ya/ badz+ra b+ha ti ga ru na Da be ge hUM ri dza pri dzan bA ra dzA hUM phaT/ sngags khri bzlas te lus la bcangs na// klu thams cad 'bros par 'gyur ro// so bdag/

49a1: mar na gnang du gtso/ / stobs chen sngags bris ras mas btums// khyim sgor sbas na 'chi bar 'gyur// oM badz+ra kro d+ha ma ha ba la ha na da ha ba tsa/ bi d+h+wa na sa ya ud sa mA ra ya hU~M phaT// sbrul mgo

50b1: pa'i thabs su shes par bya/ / dun pasum ga te kha khyer brgyad ma po// rig pa bzhin byed rdo rjes mtshan// dkar ser dmar nas ldang khu ste// las dang 'brel bar shes par bya// mchod pa'i rdzas dang lam shing /

50b7: bu thams cad 'dzin/ / rtse bzhi mnyam nyid brtan pa ste// rgyas pa'i lam la 'bras bu yod// zla 'dra snum la dri ma med// du ba med cing bai dUr 'dra // nad med rigs rnams rgyas par byed// chu shel nor bu
50b8: srungs pa dang / / pad ma rA ga gsal ba ni// sdig pa ma lus zad par 'gyur// dmar ser bu Na Da rig dang // ban du kha dog gsal ba na// rgyal srid dpal 'byor thob pa yin// ud pal ma la~M u sha dri//

51a1: tsam pa ka dang srig ka ri dri// gzungs garu'i dris// dgage zhing tshe ring dpal gyi gnas// zab pa'i skang dang drung dang ni// rdza bi wa nam ru// de yi sgras ni bde ba 'phel// dpal be 'ubag shis gzugs sa
51a2: 'char/ / rgyal mtshan rnga yab phyag mtshan rnams// rin chen gdugs kyi dbyings su 'char// dge ba me yi dbyibs su bstan// ngan pa de las ci rigs bzlog/ de rjes rdzas kyi rim pa ni// oM a ga ne ye a muH
51a3: s+ya shAn ting ku ru ye swA hA/ / bsreg lugs so// oM bo d+hi prik+Shi ya swA hA// a shwad tha'i 'o// oM badz+ra ta lA ya swA hA// p+lag sha'i'o// oM badz+ra ku be ru ye swA hA// 'o ma can gyi shing gi'o// oM badz+ra sha ma dz+wa la ya swA hA/
51a4: u dum 'bar ba'i'o// oM sarba pA paM da ha na badz+ra swA hA/ til gyi'o// oM badz+ra puSh+Ta ye swA hA// 'bras so ba'i'o// oM badz+ra sa~M b+he de swA hA// zho dang zan gyi'o// oM badz+ra A yeShe swA hA// dUng ba'i'o// oM badz+ra pra ta
51a5: ha ta badz+ra ya swA hA/ ku sha'i'o// rdzas rnams rang sngags ci rigs dbul// stod cing gsol ba'i las bya ste// me yi snying khar dkyil 'khor mchod// gsang la sogs pa rim pa bzhin// sngar bstan pa las shes par bya/
51a6: dere rjes lhag mas ci rigs mchod// zhu ba la sogs rdzas rnams ni// lha yi zhal du mchod par bya// yam shing ku sha la sogs pa// 'od la mchod par bya ba yin// phyag du zhal zas 'thor 'thung dbul// me tog gdug
51a7: padabu dang 'od/ / thig le snying khags gtor yang // skul phul te zhabs bsil zhabs// mar me la sogs rim bzhin gnas// dkyil 'khor bsdu gshegs rim pa rnams// mkhas pas nye bar brtags teH/
51a8: dkyil 'khor lhas ni mchog ster la// me yis 'dod pa'i don sgrub byed// lag pan gyis ni bde ba 'byin// 'o ma sbrang rtsis rig pa 'phel// gro dang sran mas nad kun sel// du rabs srog ni 'dzin par byed// nas

51b1: kyis brtson 'grus la dbang ste/ / skabs 'phel ma shaka yin no// 'bru 'phelas pa'i las yin te// sdig pa'i dag pa til yin no// 'bras kyis nus pa 'phel byed pa// zhi la yungs dkar ku shas srung // dpal skyed/
51b2: pani bud shing ste// yam shing gzi byin ster bar byed// 'byor pa 'phel ba mar yin no// sbyin bdag bkra shis thab yin te// dngos grub kun star mchod pa'i rdzas// thabs dang shes rab gzar bu ste// bdud rtsi
51b3: mar gyis tshim byed pa/ / mchod pa gzhan gyis ci zhig bya// 'di ni mdzes ma'i yul yin gyis// gzhan gyis rtogs par ga la 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gsang ba mngon par bstan pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po las
51b4: sbyin bsreg gi cho ga bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu dgu pa'o/ / / dpa' mo rdo rje bdems gsol pa// rdo rje 'chang khyod kyis gsang ba'i mtshan nyi shu rtsa gcig bstod pa ji lta bu lags// bcom ldan 'das
51b5: kyis bka' stsal pa/ mdzes ma khyod kyis zhus pa legs// zag med bde ba'i rgyu 'byung ma// bdag med shes rab ma yi mchog/ khyod la bshad kyis legs par nyon// nga yi ming ni nyi shu gcig/ dus gsums pa
51b6: rgyas rnams kyis gsung / / mi 'gyur g.yung drung dbang bskur te// 'di dag mdzes ma khyod la bstan// na mo nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badz+ra pA Ni tsaN Da badz+ra// na mo g+ha dza ka ra ne b+ho tsaN Da badz+ra na maHsu b+hu sha ni sa b+h+yo tsaN Da badz+ra/
51b7: namo rang Na kur Na kar si tsaN Da badz+ra// na mo b+ha kran pa nye d+ha si ra tsaN Da badz+ra/ na maHad+ya g+ho shi sin tsaN Da badz+ra/ na maHsa pras rA yi to sI tsaN Da badz+ra// na mo badz+ra la ar tsi shi sI tsaN Da badz+ra/ na maHsa su ru pano pa/
51b8: la tsaN Da badz+ra// na mo dur d+han tad ma ka ma pa raHtsaN Da badz+ra// na mo b+ha ra bi b+ha sa ta ru bi b+hi tsaN Da badz+ra// na mo dro me kro d+ha bi gra ha ru bI b+hi tsaN Da badz+ra// na maHtsa tur smA dA rI sha sa Na tsaN Da badz+ra/ na mo ma hA ba la ba rakra

52a1: pa tsaN Da badz+ra/ na mo nair rma sid ha nir nad tsaN Da badz+ra// na maHa mo b+ha dza g+ha tad thA kri tsaN Da badz+ra/ na mo shA dig bi shwa nir maN tsata Da badz+ra/ na mo ha hA satwa so nir g+ho go tsata Da badz+ra/ na maHa tsa lo haH
52a2: dzad to Na Da badz+ra/ na maHpany+tsa bud d+ha ta ma mu kraT tsata Da badz+ra/ na mo badz+ra ma hA b+he sha yud d+ha rod tsa tsaN Da badz+ra// rdo rje gtum po'i mtshan nyi shu rtsa gcig po 'di 'dzin pa dang // 'chang ba dang / klog pa dang / yid la byed pa dang /
52a3: 'dri ba dang / 'drir 'jug pa dang / glegs pam dra byas te 'chang ba la ni phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyis rjes su skyong bar 'gyur ro// srung bar 'gyur ro// sred par 'gyur ro// skyob par 'gyur ro// mtshan
52a4: 'di rnams 'dzin pa de/ 'tshams med pa lnga byas pa'i sdig pa yang byang bar 'gyur ro// lan gcig tsam brjod pas kyang bskal pa bye ba phrag dgu bcu'i bar du sems can dmyal ba rnams su mi skye'o// ngan 'gro gzhan
52a5: yang spangs pa yin no/ / tshe rabs thams cad du skye ba dran par 'gyur ro// rdo rje 'chang lnga brgya yang rtag tu mtshan 'di 'dzin pa'i phyi bzhin rjes su 'brang ngo // gdug pa can gyi klu rnams kyis me 'tshe zhing slar longs
52a6: spyo sna tshogs sbyin no/ / 'chi ba'i dus su yang bai dUr+ya lta bu'i klu lus bstan te rang gi gnas su khrid par 'gyur ro// mtshan 'di gnas pa'i sa de ni lcang lo can dang mtshungs pa yin no// mi dang mi ma yin pa gdug
52a7: pa can rnams kyis nam yang gnod pa byed par mi 'gyur ro/ / grub pa brgyad dang sangs rgyas kyang ster bar byed na// gzhan lta yang ci smos te// mtshan 'di dag rin po che dang 'dra bar lta bar bya'o// 'di ni dus gsum
52a8: sangs rgyas kyis/ / tshe du brjod pa rin po che// gdug pa thams cad 'joms par byed// dpal dang gzi brjid 'phel ba yin// phrin las skornams thogs pa med// 'di ni rdo rje 'chang yin pas// nyin pa

52b1: dus gsum klog pa yi/ / phyi bzhin rtag tu srung bar byed// nad dang gdon rnams kun las thar// sman chen nyes pa thams cad 'joms// 'thung po kun gyis bkur ba ste// mdzes ma khyod la bstan pa yin// 'di
52b2: ni rnam dag legs pa'i lam/ / su 'chang lag na dpal gnas te// rtag tu mtshan 'di brjod par gyis// bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gsang ba mngon par bstan pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po las mtshan nyi shu rtsa gcig gi
52b3: bstod pa'i le'u ste nyi shu pa'o/ / / dpa' mo rdo rje bde mas gsol pa// rdo rje 'chang gi rgyud 'di bshad pa dang // sba ba dang / ji ltar gzung ba'i cho ga ji la bu lags// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka'
52b4: stsal pa/ mdzes ma khyod kyis zhus pa legs// zag med bde ba'i rgyu 'byung ma// bdag med shes rab ma yi mchog/ khyod la bshad kyis legs par nyon// phyi ma'i dus su nga yi rgyud// gsang ba sku gsung thugs
52b5: kyi gter/ / bla med rgyud rgyal rin chen 'di// byang chub sems ldan snying rje che// thos mang shes rab mchog tu gsal// dad pa che zhing lha la gus// bla ma bsten cing dbang bskur thob// dam tshig sdom pa ma lus ldan//
52b6: brtson 'grus che la gzhan don dpa'// 'jig rten bde la ma chags pas// rgyud 'di mnyan dang bshad par bya// de las bzlog pa'i gang zag la// ming tsam bstan par mi bya'o// gal te bstan par gyur pa na// sngags
52b7: pa dam tshig nyams gyur te/ / nad gdon 'byung po ma lus pas// nyes par gtses te 'chi bar 'gyur// de nas mnar med sdug bsngal ni// grangs med 'das kyang thar mi 'gyur// de bas gsang ba sku gsung
52b8: thugs/ / snying po dam pa 'di dag la// rgya yis btab ste mchod pa dang // bstod cing sba ba byas gyur na// yid la re ba kun rdzogs shing // 'jig rten thams cad bde bar 'gyur// glegs bam sor ni bcu drug la//

53a1: rim bdun rgya yis btab nas kyang // rtag tu smra ba'i gtsug tu gzung // 'di dang bral bar mgyur na// bsnyen pa de yin bsgrub pa de// sgrub pa chen po'ang de yin te// sngags kyang de yin lha yang /
53a2: de// bla ma de yin slob dpon yang // sangs rgyas chos dang dge 'dun yang // de yin bskyed dang rdzogs pa de// ma lus dbang yang de yin te// 'jig rten bya ba kun spangs nas// 'di la mchod par gyur pa ni// chos
53a3: gzhan ci yod rmongs pa'i rgyu/ / ci phyir 'di la 'bad mi byed// ces bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs te// yum la rjes su gtang ba'i don bstan pa ni// sangs rgyas kun gyi yum chen mo// rdo rje bde ma bde ster ma//
53a4: rtog pa gcod mdzad yum khyod la// rgyud 'di gtad kyis legs par zung // gzungs ma yid 'ong rgyal ba'is// rnam dag mchod cing sdug bsngal 'joms// ma lus 'gro ba 'dren pa'i dpal// rdo rje bdem phyag
53a5: 'tshal lo/ / zhes pa stod nas rgud gtad ngo // de nas yum gyis rjes bzung ste// dus gsum bde gshegs ma lus pa'i// thugs kyi sras po sde dpon che// 'jig rten thams cad 'dul mdzad pa// dpa' bo myod
53a6: la phyag 'tshal lo/ / gtum po dpa' bo 'jigs par byed// klu 'dul gzhan gyis mi thub pa// drag po 'jigs par byed pa'i lha// rdo rje gtum po khyod phyag 'tshal// zhes bstod nas phyag dang bskor bas mnyes
53a7: par byas nas slar yab kyi thugs ka'i rdo rje'i lte bar thim par gyur to/ / de nas 'khor thams cad kyis mchod pas mchod cing bstod pas bstod de// gsang ba mngon par bstan pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po gsungs pa leg
53a8: so legs so zhes mngon par mgrin gcig tu chad du brjod pa ched du brjod de/ / rdo rje 'chang chen pos gsungs pa la mngon par dga' nas yid rangs te mngon par bstod par gyur to// bcom ldan 'das phyag na

53b1: dzirjegs pa mngon par bstan pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po las rgyud ji ltar bstan cing sla da rjes su yi nga ba'i le'u ste nyi shu rtsa gcig pa'o/ / / bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gsang ba mngon par bstan pa'i hung
53b2: gyi rgyal po zhes bya ba rdzogs s+ho/ / / rgya gar byi mkhan po wal can dgu du can po dang // bong kyilo rgyub gran d+hang dang ma tshul khrims kyis byang phyogs sham tha la'i ba dang bkun te bskung bag//
53b3: slad kyis yul dbus kyi dpe dang / kha chenas byung ba dang bsun nas legs par gtan la bab pa'o// rgyag gang du/ badz+ra tha~Md yabadzadzi mam nam dAr NI/ bod ska dang / rdo rje snyid brje
53b4: lde dbab pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na// bcom ldan 'das dur khrod chen po bsil ba'i cha
53b5: na bzhugs te/ / de na 'khor nye ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas dang // lha dang / mi dang / lha ma yin dang // klu rnams dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das
53b6: kyis rdo rje snying po zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ / thugs kha nas 'od zer rab tu bkye bar gyur te// 'od zer des stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad khya ba bya nas ma
53b7: can thams cad kyi nad dang mi bde ba dang sdug bsngal thams cad dang bral bar byas nas slar bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs su zhugs so/ / de nas drang srong chen po nye 'dor langs te phyag 'tshal nas bcom ldan
53b8: 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to/ / bcom ldan 'das 'jig rten gyi khams 'di na sems can thams cad la nad dang / dug dang / rims dang / dgra dang / gdon dang / byad stems dang / srod gtong dang / chang ches

54a1: pa dang / char mi 'bab pa dang / la tag ma drangs par byed pa rnams kyis sems can thams cad sdug bsngal zhing nyam thag par gyur nade la gang bsrung ba dang / bskyab pa dang / spa bar brtse/ ba/

54a3: bshad kyis legs par rab tu nyon la yid la zung shig/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis badz+ra badz+ra hU~M zhes gsungs pas rdo rje snying po khro zhing gtum gdug pa'i cha lugs can 'thod nas bcom ldan 'das kyis
54a4: snam logs na 'khod par gyur to/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis mgrin gcig tu gzungs 'di bka' stsal to// nyi ma sa zla na na/ klad pa nan/ kun zhi/ tsi ta ku li na na/ yag sha zlog byen/ de nas gzungs
54a5: 'di gsungs ma thag tu bgegs dang log 'dren thams cad 'jigs skrag nas kha srub tu 'gyel te lbu bar skyug cing brgyal bar gyur to/ / de nas klu'i rgyal po mtha' yas kyang 'jigs skrag nas lus 'dar zhing

54a7: gyis brlab tu gsol/ na mo bud d+ha ya/ tsa tra mu drA yag sha zlog byer/ de nas gzungs 'di smras ma thag tu sa chen po g.yos par gyur te/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kha srub tu 'gyel te// gdor dang
54a8: log 'dren thams cad kha sbub tu 'gyel te/ / khrag tu skyug cing dbugs dang bral bar gyur to// de nas yang klu mtha' yas kyis 'di skad ces brjod do// bcom ldan 'das bdag gis sems can thams cad la bsrung

54b1: ba dang / / bsgrub pa dang // sba bar bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bstan pa bsrung bar bgyi'o// sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa yun ring du gnas par bgyi'o// char dus su dbab cing lo tog thams cad bsrung bar
54b2: bgyi'o/ / nad dang dgra dang gdon thams cad gzhom par bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis ji ltar bka' stsal pa ltar bgyi dpa las zlog par mi bgyid do// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa// legs
54b3: so legs so/ / klu'i rgyal po mtha' yas khyod kyis ji ltar dam bcas pa ltar gyis shig/ dam tshig rjes su srungs shig/ ji ltar nga'i bka' bcag na ngan song du smra gyud de// nga'i ji ltar bsgo ba thams cad
54b4: kyis shig/ de nas gsad pa'i bdag pos rdo rje lce dbab pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs klags pas 'grub pa drag po rab tu mi bzad pa'i da smras so// nA ga shig/ nA ga byer/ nA ga nAn/ nA ga go la nAn/ nA ga ha na ha na mA ra ya rba
54b5: nAn/ / sa gdon nag po song// sa gdon nag po sod/ sa gdon nag po/ nAn/ phyug tsi phaT/ cig pU phaT/ lce ba ti phaT/ e ba ga re tse 'di na dag por ma ma hA b.las ta ye go ra mad te nAn/ thum ril rbad che ge
54b6: mo mA ra ya dza rbad nAn/ nA ga hri la hri la/ nA ga phroM phreM/ nA ga phro ba badz+ra pra pe sha yas 'di srungs shig byer ya/ b+h+yor ma ma hA a hUM hUM phaT swA hA/ de nas gzungs 'di gsungs ma thag tu nam mkha' la gnam
54b7: lcags drag po'i rdo rje'i thog pab nas dgra dang / gdon dang / lo tog ma rungs par byed pa thams cad kyi lus dum bur dum bur gtubs nas rdul phra rab bzhin du brlag par byas so// de nas bcom ldan
54b8: 'das kyis chog bka' stsal pa/ drang srong chen posa'i dkyil 'khor gru bzhi pa byid byas nas pa'i rnam lngas byug par bya'o// tsan dan dang rgya spos dri zhim pos thug par bya'o// me tog sil ma dgram sa/ khrim pa

55a1: gang ba bzhag go/ mar me bud do// gtor ma bzang po gzhag go// lcags sam seng ldeng gi phur pa gzugs so// dbus su rdo rje snying po gzhag par bya'o// de'i mdun du klu mtha' yas bzhag
55a2: go/ / de nas mchod par 'dod na me tog la sogs pa mchod pa lnga bya'o// klu mchod par 'dod na khar ba'i snod du 'o ma dang / klu sman sna tshogs dang / rtsi sman sna tshogs kyis bya'o// nad dang dug bsrung bar 'dod na
55a3: tshil chen dang / gla rtsi dang / skud pa sngon po dang // rma bya'i spros bya'o// kun chen po la ni tshil chen dang / gla rtsi dang / tshon skud sna lnga dang / seng ldeng gi phur pas bya'o// 'byung po thams cad la ni phur pa dang / yungs
55a4: dkar gyis bya'o/ / skya rengs 'char ka'i gdon la ni phur pa dang / yungs dkar dang / yungs nag dang / ske/ tshe dang / thal chen gyis bya'o// 'byung po kun tu rgyu ba la ni phur ba lnga dang / thod pas bya'o// gzhan dag gas
55a5: bar 'dod na phur pa dang / gzugs dang / thod pas bya'o// gnan par 'dod na thod pa dang / drug dang / yungs dkar gyis bya'o// lo tog gzhom par 'dod na thod pa dang / dug dang / yungs dkar dang / tshil chen dang / khrag

55b1: dang / / che dang / til dang mar nag dang / tshil chen dang / ming byang spel te/ sbyin bsreg bya zhing / che ge mo ra sha sAr ya zad ces bzlas na dgra dang / gdon thams cad rlag par 'gyur ro// bdag dang gzhan bsrung /

55b3: rtsis bya'o/ / mchog tu bsrung bar 'dod na 'bras bu gsum dang / bu chung gi rang byung dang / dri chus bya'o// khyad par dam pa bsrung ba chen po na a ru ra rnam par rgyal ba bcang zhing gzungs 'di brjod par bya'o//
55b4: shig byer nAn// 'gonAn/ han tan mA ra ya rbad nAn/ drang srong chen po nyes 'dir gzungs 'di yid la rab tu zung shig/ sems can thams cad la bsrung ba dang / bskyab pa dang / sba bar gyis shig/ de'i bstan
