98a7: dang / / 'khyil pa'i mtshan ma mkhas pas brtag/ de nas myur du 'grub 'gyur bas// bsgom dang bzlas la 'bad par bya// zhi dang rgyas dang dbang la ni// oM zhes pa dang swA hA mthar// dbyangs kyi rgyun ni
98a8: bsring pa dang / / bar chad med pa'i dbyangs kyis sbyar// zhi ba'i sems kyis zhib mo// 'byor pa rgyas pa mngon par spel// dregs gdong stabs tshul bcas pa dang // dbang du gyur pas dbang bya'o// drag

98b1: shul spyod tshul la gnas pas/ / hU~M zhes pa dang phaT dang bcas/ lus ni me lce 'bar ba dang // 'jig rten gsum po bzang bsams nas// bskul ba'i tshig dang spel ba yi// gsang sngags yi ge nges par
98b2: sbyar/ / sngags grub chog shes pa yis// sbyin pa sreg cho ga thams cad la// sna tshogs las dang ldan pa'i lha// gang dag yin pa mthong bar bya// sbyin pa sreg de nyid kyis bskul cing // dang po dgang blugs
98b3: bsreg cing dbul/ / phyis ni rim bzhin rnam par spel// zhi dang rgyas dang dbang rnams la// dge ba rdzas rnams sbyin pasreg bya// gshang gci khrag rkang rus pa dang // sha chen dag kyang sbyin pasreg bya// ci ste ye
98b4: shes sems pa'i zhal/ / mi gtsang ba yis bkang nago/ ji ltar sdig pa mi skye 'gyur// gal te sdig 'gyur 'bras bu gang // sems can mi shes pas rmongs te// thams cad shes rab rnam spangs shing phyi rol
98b5: dngos la mngon zhen pas/ / rnam rtog dra bas blan byas gang // de dag gis ni dge sdig gi/ phung po gnyis su rnam par brtags// chos 'di rang bzhin gyis dag ste// skye ba med cing gnas pa med// sems
98b6: can shes pa spel ba'i phyir/ / sangs rgyas rnams kyi thabs kyis bstan// dam pa'i don du dge spang na// bsod nams med pa ci zhig spos// dper na chus gang chu klung gi// pha rol 'gro ba'i sems can dag/
98b7: dang shing la sogs bsdus te// chu las rgal ba'i gzings byas na// de la 'dzus te legs rgal na// bor te bde bar 'gro bltar// de bzhin 'khor ba'i pha rol gyi// chos kyi lam ni bskyed byas kyang / chos
98b8: dang chos min rnam spangs nas/ / byang chub bde ba thob pa bzhin// de phyir rnam rtog drang spongs la// zab mo yi ni chos spel te// de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs lam la// sngags rig rnam rtogs byed cig

99a1: rnam rtog rmongs pa chen po sde/ / 'khor ba'i brgya mtshor ltung byed pas// nam mkha' lta bur dri med pa'i// rnam par mi rtog ting 'dzin mnos// dbang po gnyis ni mnyam sbyar te// lus dang
99a2: ngag dang sems bsdams nas/ / nga'o snyam pa'i gzi bskyed gzugs// rnam pa kun gyis rnam par brgyan// rnal 'byor ldan pa tshe 'di la// ye shes rdzogs pa nyid du 'gyur// las las byung ba
99a3: rnam bstan pa'i/ / skyes pa bud med gzugs med la// brnyes pa nyid du mi bya 'dis// rdo rje lus can dam tshig yin// ngan rtog bzang rtog dra ba yi// sems kyis sems can rnams la ni// sna tshogs gdung
99a4: bas sun mi dbyung / / rdo rje sems ldan dam tshig yin// sred pas bskyed rngub phra ba yis// tshig dag rnam par mi smra zhing // mnyan na bde bar byed pa 'di// rdo rje dag can dam tshig yin// rnam par snang mdzad
99a5: cher 'khrugs mchog/ sha yi khams la gnas pa yin// rkang la mi 'khrugs rgyal po ste// khrag la rin chen 'byung ba gtso// sems can rnams kyi rus phung gi/ dus gos la ni 'od dpag med// rtsa yi
99a6: cho gas rnams rnam 'dren pa/ / thub pa skyed mchog don yod la// dam tshig shes pa rnams la ni// gsang chen nga yis bsten pa 'di// blo ldan rdo rje sems kyis ni// rtag tu bsten zhing bsgom par bya//
99a7: 'dod chags zhe sdang de bzhin rmongs// sred dang de bzhin rnam spel ba'i// chos ni rnam pa lnga po 'di// thub pa skyes mchog rnams kyis gsungs// bshad gci khu ba mchil ma khrag/ 'dzag pa
99a8: 'byung ba bzhin bsdus pa/ / bsgom pa'i blo gros rdzogs pa yis// dam tshig bsten par bya ba ste// rtag tu bza' zhing btung bar bya// rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po sgyu 'phrul gyi dra ba las 'di ni sbyin bsreg rim

99b1: par bye ba'i le'u ste dgu pa'o/ / / de nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad chen po rdo rje'i de bzhin gshegs pas ting 'dzin thams cad kyi dngos grub dam pa rdor zhes bya ba nga /
99b2: la snyoms par zhugs nas dam tshig thams cad kyi rdo rje chen po'i mchog dngos grub 'di bka' stsal to// lag na rdo rje gsang sngags bsgom pa'i rnal 'byor gyi tshogs yang dag par bskul nas rjes thams
99b3: cad kyi dngos grub sgrub pa'i thabs gsang chen 'di nyon cig/ rnam par snang mdzad ting 'dzin la// gnas shing sku gsung thugs bsgoms te// mdun du 'khor lo legs par bzhag/ sku gsum rdo rje can
99b4: gyi gzugs/ / 'bar ba'i phreng ba 'khrug pa'i 'od// 'khor lo'i nang du zhugs gyur par// bsgo ba zhing 'khor lo bsgrub par bya// me yi 'od ltar 'bar ba'i 'od// 'khor lo chen po 'phags par 'gyug/
99b5: spyan ni bzlas brjod byed bzhin du// bla med 'khor lo blang bar bya// rgyal chen 'khor lo drug pa dag/ 'od ni rnam par snang mdzad bzhin// lan gsum 'jug pa'i sems can la// chos kyi 'khor lo
99b6: bskor bar gyur/ / mi 'khrugs par ni rnam par bsgom zhing // rdo rje mdun du bzhag nas ni// rim pa bzhin du bskul na 'dis// sku gsum rnam par 'phel 'gyur zhing // 'bar ba'i phred chen mnyam pa'i 'od/
99b7: rdo rje chen po 'phags par 'gyur// mA ma kI ni zlos bzhin du// rdo rje bla med blang bar bya// rdo rje rgyal po blangs pa yis// gtso ba rdo rje 'chang gnyis 'gyur// gtso bo chen po sangs rgyas dang // byang chub sems
99b8: dpas yongs bskor nas/ / sems can kun sems la gnas pa'i// lag na rdo rje rdo rje 'chang // 'jig rten khams su rnam rgyu zhing // kun gyi bsam pa yongs rdzogs byed// rin chen 'byung ba bsgoms na

100a1: ni/ / rin po che ni mdun bzhag ste// sbyor ba'i rim pas rnam spel na// rin chen chen po 'phags par 'gyur// rin chen sgrol ma zlos bzhin du// 'od bzangs gzi brjid 'bar ba can//
100a2: phyogs kun snang bar byed pa yi// nor bu'i rgyal po blang bar bya// lha rdzas nor bu blangs pa yis// rin chen 'byung ba gnyis par 'gyur// de ni sems can thams cad kyi// yid bzhin nor bu rin chen bzhin//
100a3: rin chen char ba rab 'bebs shing // sems can kun gyi dbul ba 'joms// gtso ba yid bzhin nor bu can// sangs rgyas zhing du rnam par rgyu// 'od dpag med par rnam bsgoms nas// pad ma chen po bdun
100a4: bzhag ste/ / rim bzhin gzi brjid gzings stod na// 'dab ma bye bas rnam brgyan pa// 'od bzangs gser ltar 'bar ba can// pad ma chen po 'phags par 'gyur// gos dkar can ma'i gsang sngags
100a5: kyis/ / yid las byung ba'i pad ma blang // pad ma'i rgyal po blangs pa yis// 'od dpag med pa gnyis par 'gyur// chos mdzad rnams kyi thog 'dren cing // sems can rnams la bdud rtsi stsol// sangs
100a6: rgyas zhing rnams snang byed gtse/ / bde ba can gyi rgyan du 'gyur// don yod grub pa rnam bsgom nas// ral gri bdun du rnam bzhag ste// rnal 'byor rim pa 'di yis ni// bsgoms pa de nyid kyis bskul na//
100a7: rdo rje 'bar ba lta bu'i 'od// ral gri chen po 'phags par 'gyur// sgrol ma'i gsang sngags zlos bzhin du// ral gri bla med blang bar bya// des ni ral gri mchog blangs nas// don yod grub pa gnyis par
100a8: 'gyur/ / sangs rgyas zhing du rnam rgyu zhing // sems can rnams kyis mi shes spyod// rtag du dri med skarang 'gyur te// chu yin gi ston zla bzhin// rdzas kyi dngos grub bstan nas ni// phyag rgya chen po bskul

100b1: par bya/ / rnal 'byor che la nam gnas pa// de bzhin gshegs kyi btsun me che// zhe sdang rigs ni 'dren mdzad ma// rdo rje gdan can mA ma kI// rin chen 'byung ba'i lha ma dang // lham 'gro ba dbang mdzad pa/
100b2: mkha' la longs spyod spyod mdzad ma// rim pa bzhin du nga yis bshad// de nas bu mo mig yang sa ma// lo ni bcu drug lon pa la// gzugs dang mdangs dang lang tshor ldan// gser gyi rna cha g.yo ba can//
100b3: gcig gcig bsgrims te btsal nas su// lha mo byi dor legs byas te// rigs lnga yi ni tshigs can ma// las kyi rjes su bsgom byas nas// bzhag te spad pa'i sbyor ba yis// pad ma la ni rdo rje
100b4: bzhag/ sprad pa dang ni khyad pa yis// rdo rje dang ni pad ma bskul// gar gyi tshul du gyur pa dang // de bzhin spro dang sdu ba yis// mod la sgyu mas drag myos nas// rdo rje las ni bdud rtsi 'byung // rnal 'byor
100b5: ldan pa'i shes rab las/ / pad ma la gnas bdud rtsi btung // rnal 'byor ldan pa'i kha yis ni// mthungs pas de bzhin gshegs lnga yi// sku ni yongs su 'gyur bar 'thob// nam mkha' 'dra ba'i
100b6: chos kun la/ / thabs dang shes rab rnam par 'phel// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// sku yi snying po bsgrub pa ste// 'dod lnga'i yon tan rjes 'jug pa'i// byang chub bde bas bsgrubs na ni//
100b7: rdo rje pad ma byin brlabs nas// rjes su chags pas 'thob par 'gyur// grub chen gsang ba'i dngos grub ni// sdug bsngal med pa'i bde ba'i thabs// rjes su chags pas bde ba yi// rdo rje theg
100b8: pas gnyis par 'gyur/ / sbyor ba'i khyad par 'di yis ni// lan gsum 'jug pa'i gsang sngags dang // lam gyi phyag rgya ngas bshad de// de dag lag pa'i phyag rgya dag/ ye shes phyag rgya rab gul

101a1: bas dam tshig mchog gis 'grub par 'gyur/ / thub chen sna tshogs gzugs mnga' ba// sna tshogs phrin las mdzad par 'gyur// de nas phyag na rdo rjes khams gsum gyi dam tshig gi 'khang/
101a2: lo 'di nyid kyi rdo rje'i sku dang gsung dang thugs las byung ngo // sa ni spyan du brjod pa ste// chu khams mA ma kaM nas bshad// sgrol ma rlung zhes kun tu brjod// gos dkar can ma me ru sbags// rdo rje dmatshig
101a3: nam mkha'i dbyings/ / ston pa rdo rje 'chang bas bshad ces de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sa'i dbang phyug bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa' chen pos gsungs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das
101a4: r do rje'i de bzhin gshegs pas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i sku dang gsung dang thugs de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid du gnas pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms
101a5: par zhugs nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor la rnam par bltas nas cang mi gsung bar gyur to/ / de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byams pas
101a6: de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la phyag 'tshal te/ 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i sku dang gsung dang thugs gsang ba 'dus par dbang
101a7: bstar ba'i slob dpon dal de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyis ci ltar lta bar bgyi ba lags// rigs kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang // byang chub
101a8: sems dpa' chen po thams cad kyis 'di ni rdo rje'i byang chub kyi sems su blta bar bya'o/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub kyi sems dang rdo rje slob dpon 'di gnyis gnyis su byar med pa'i phyir zhes bya ba

101b1: bar nas rigs kyi bu 'dor bsdus nas yang bshad par bya'o/ / phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams na sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs shing ba shes pa'i bar de dag tham
101b2: cad dus gsum du byon nas slob dpon la de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mchod pas mngon par mchod nas 'di skad ces bdag cag de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi pa yin 'dag cag de bzhin gshes/ thams cad kyim yino/
101b3: / bdag cag de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ston pa yin nas rdorje'i yigag su byu na pa yang rang rang gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing du gshegs par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu dper na/ sangs rgyas bcom
101b4: l dan 'das phyogs bcun bzhugs pa'i bar de dag gis sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rdo rje'i sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi bsod nams kyi phung po pas ni rdo rje slob dpon de'i spu'i khung du
101b5: gcig gi bsod nams kyi phung po ches khyad par du 'phags so/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rigs kyi bu byang chub kyi sems ni sangs rgyas kyi ye shes snying por gyur pa'i bar nas thams cad mkhyen pa'i
101b6: ye shes kyi 'byung gnas yin no/ / de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byams pa 'jigs shing skrag pa'i yid kyis cang mi smra bar gyur to// de nas yang de bzhin gshegs pa mi 'khrugs
101b7: ba dang / / rin chen 'byung ba dang // don yod grub pa dang // de bzhin gshegs pa 'od dpag med dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad rnams rdo rje 'chang thams cad kyi dngos grub kyi dam tshig
101b8: la dmigs pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag la bos nas shes ldan byang chub sems dpa' thams cad nyon cig/ phyogs bcu dus gsum

102a1: du byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams rdo rje slob dpon gyi drung du byon nas mchod par mdzad cing phyag 'tshal bar brjod do/ / de ci'i phyir zhe na// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang /
102a2: byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi ston pa yin pa dang / bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang de nyid ni sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi bdag po yin pa'i phyir ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa
102a3: de dag gis de bzhin gshegs pa de dag la 'di skad ces gsol to/ / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi dngos grub gang la gnas/ de bzhin gshegs pa
102a4: thams cad kyis bka' stsal pa/ rdo rje'i sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba gsum ni rdo rje slob dpon gyi lus dang ngag dang yid la gnas so// byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyis gsol pa// rdo rje slob
102a5: dpon gyi lus dang ngag dang sems kyis gsang ba gang la gnas/ mkha' la gnas/ nam mkha' gang la gnas/ rdo rje slob dpon gyi sems la gnas/ sems gang la gnas/ gang du yang ma yin no// de nas
102a6: byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag ngo mtshar du gyur nas cang mi zer bar 'khod do/ / dkyil 'khor dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / phyag rgya dang stang stabs dang / 'dug stabs dang / bzlas brjod dang /
102a7: sbyin bsreg dang // mchod pa dang / las la sbyar ba dang / slar bsdu ba rnams ni gsang sngags kyi tshul de kho na nyid bcu yin par gsungs so// dus gsum du 'byung ba'i rgyal ba thugs rje'i ro gcig pa rnams
102a8: kye gsang ba dang gsang chen dang ye shes rnam pa gsum gyi snying po bstan pa dag ni slob dpon gyi kho nas bla ma la gus pa'i slob mas shes par bya'o/ / bla mas dam tshig ci lta ba bzhin gyi dbang du byas nas

102b1: bshad par bya'o/ / bslabs nas sems can rnams la rnal 'byor dang // rnal 'byang chan po dang // lhag pa rnal 'gyur rnams gar ma bzhin bshad par bya'o// 'ad mtha' dag ni rgyud thams cad tu
102b2: shes par bya'o/ / de kho na nyid kyi dngos po mtha' dag yongs su mi shes par gsang sngags smra ba yin no nas mngon pa'i nga rgyal gyis gsang sngags kyi chog 'chad par byed na dpa tshig thams cad nyan par
102b3: 'gyur ro/ / dam tshig las nyams na bdud kyis bzung bar 'gyur ro// skyes bu shi nas dmyal ba'i gnas mi bzad pa chen por 'gro bar 'gyur ro// sems can rnams la brten te byang chub thob par 'gyur
102b4: bas sems can la bslu bar mi bya'o/ / zhes shes par byas nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i lam de nyid la sems can de dag sbyar bar bya'o// gang zhig 'di la brtson par ma byas pa de dag gis ni lag
102b5: pa dang rkang pa dang / mig sbyin pa'i dka' ba spyad pa dang // bka' thub ci lta bus kyang sdig pa gzhom pa 'am/ bdud rtsi'i ro thob par mi nus so// rnal 'byor gcig khong du chud nas dben par song ste bsgom
102b6: byas na sdig pa las grol zhing tshe 'di nyid la sangs rgyas kyi yon tan rnams dang / / chos bdag med par bsgoms pas thams cad mkhyen pa'i rnal 'byor khong du chud par bya'o// shes rab dang ye she
102b7: kyi 'jo tshul gyis gsang ba lnga'i bdag nyid kyi gtso bo la mchod par bya'o/ / dngos po thams cad dngos med par// bzhi bcu'i don ni rtogs pa dang // rdo rje pad mas dbang bskur bas// bdud rtsi lngas
102b8: ni dga' bar byed/ / gsang bar bya ba'i chos gsang ba// gsang zhing skas te gzhag par bya// 'dod yon lnga yi rnam pa ni// gzugs sgra dri re rog bya sogs// rnal 'byor sems dpa' sbyang bya zhing /

103a1: de bzhin bza' dang btung byas na// bltas dang khu tshur rnam pa yis// sems can thams cad dbang du byed// rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po sgyu 'phrul dra ba las cho ga thams cad bstan pa rim par phye
103a2: ba ste bcu pa'o/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang // lha dang mi dang lha ma yin dang dri za dang / thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor de dag yid rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon
103a3: par bstod do/ / rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po sgyu 'phrul dra ba theg pa chen po'i yang theg pa chen po'i tshul zab mo gsang bas kyang ches gsang ba chen po rdzogs s+ho// zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos
103a4: bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ / rgya gar skad du/ sarba ta thA ga ta kA ya bA ga tsing ta kriSh+NaSh+Tha ya mA ri nA ma tan tra/ bod skad du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs gshin rje gshed
103a5: nag pa zhes bya ba'i rgyud/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gshin rje gshed la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung
103a6: dang thugs rdo rje'i btsun mo thams cad kyi b+hag rnams la bzhugs te/ / gti mug rdo rje gshin rje gshed dang / phra ma rdo rje gshin rje gshed dang / 'dod chags rdo rje gshin rje gshed dang / phrag dog rdo rje gshin
103a7: rje gshed dang / zhe sdang rdo rje gshin rje gshed dang / tho ba gshin rje gshed dang / dbyug pa gshin rje gshed dang / pad ma gshin rje gshed dang / ral gri gshin rje gshed dang / mtshams rnams su rdo rje tsar
103a8: tsi kA dang / / rdo rje phag mo dang / rdo rje dbyangs can ma dang / rdo rje go rI ste ma rnams 'tshams su'o// de dag la sogs te gshin rje gshed kyi tshogs chen po dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// de nas phyag na/

103b1: rdo rje bcom ldan 'das rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po la gsol ba btab pa dang // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos bdud thams cad rnam par 'joms
103b2: pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin 'di nyid kyi sku gsung thugs rdo rje las nges par bton to/ / zla ba rdo rje sbyor ba yis// gshin rje mthar byed bsgom par bya// bdud rnams zhi bar bya byir dang // de sdang thams
103b3: cad bsal ba'i phyir/ / 'od zer lnga yis 'khrigs pa yis// rdo rje bsrung ba'i don du bsgom// phyi mtshams rdo rjes gzhi dang // rab drab de bzhin no// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa
103b4: s kyed pa po bdud 'dul ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas gti mug rdo rje gshin rje gshed la sogs pa thams cad kyis bon 'di nyid kyi sku gsung thugs rdo rje rnams la ngas par phyung
103b5: dbus su ya dang k+She ma med yang ts+tsha ni rA dzA sa do ru Na yo ni ra'o/ / ya sogs yi ge dang po las// gshin rje gshed du gyu rab yin// yi ge k+She ni gti mug brjod// yi ge ma ni phra mar gsungs// yi ge me/
103b6: ni 'dod chags nyid// yi ge d+ha ni phrag dog 'gyur// gshin rje gshed sogs lnga ru grags// yi ge ya las tho bar 'gyur// yi ge ts+tsha las dbyug pa'i gtso// lag na pad ma ni yi ge las// lag na ral gri
103b7: rA las yin/ / dza las tsar tsi kA zhes brjod// yi ges las phag gdong ma// yi ge d+ha las dbyangs can bsgrags// yi ge ru las go rI dran// Na yo ni ra mtshams kyi bzhi// thod pa bzhi ru 'dod pa
103b8: na/ rnachags rdo rje'i 'jigs ru ba// rnam mkha' rdo rjed dkyil dubasam// dedakyil bzhugs pa'i gshin rjegashed// gnag cing 'bar ba bsgos par bya// shar du gti mug rdo rje rje/

104a1: lho ru de bzhin phra ma yin// nub tu 'dod chags rdo rje ste// de bzhin byang du phrag dog go// mtshams kyi rdo rje rtse bzhi la// car tsikA sogs rnam par bskam// sgra ya rdo rje rtsa ban la// tha
104a2: la sogs rnam par bsgom/ / sna tshogs rdo rje'i mtshams bzhi ru// mi yi mgo bo bzhi dag go/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos gshin rje gshed po rdo rje zhes bya
104a3: ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas zhe sdang chen po'i rigs kyi sngags gsungs pa/ / oM hriHSh+T+rIHwi kri tA nan hUM hUM phaT phaT swA hA// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
104a4: kyi bdag pos gti mug rdo rje chen po'i sngags gsungs pa/ / oM dzi na dzika/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos phra ma rdo rje'i sngags gsungs pa// oM rad na d+hika/

131b3: gshin rje dgra nag po'i 'khor lo gzhan gyi lto ba la gnas 'cha' bar 'dod pa'i gtan 'pho ba ma yin pa'i tshe bya'o/ / 'khor lo snying khar lta bar che// sa bon tshul te lte ba la// yi ge ma lus 'dod pa yang
131b4: mtshan nyid ngan pa'i rtog pa las/ / grol te mtha' gsum ngo bo las// k+Sha ni zad pa'i bdag nyid la// u Ni hUM gi bdag nyid de// de ni sems kyi rang bzhin nyid// dga' las 'das pa'i ye shes te// thams
131b5: ni shes rab ldan pa las/ / dus thabs bsten pa'i bdag nyid kyis// 'thob te gzhan du de mi thob// chu 'gram chen po'i pas mtha' dang // du khrod shing drung dgon pa ste// dben pa'i yul dang ma mo'i khyim//
131b6: der ni mgon po 'di la 'bad// gzhan du bsgrubs kyang de mi 'grub// skad cig de la rang bzhin kun// nges par mi snang rig pa yi// lam du gyur pa med par shes// 'bras bu de ni rgya chen te// mtha' yi 'thob
131b7: pa de yin no/ / de nas yang thams cad kyi bdag po bde bar gshegs pas rdo rje sa'i cho ga gsungs pa ni// skyob pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// spyod pa'i tshul dang khyad par kyis// sa dang pha rol phyin pa la/
131b8: lha mo khyod ni dbang du gyur// bsrung ba'i dkyil 'khor rab gnas pas// sdang pa'i lag 'dren skye bo dang // bgegs rnams bsal ba 'di skad gsungs// dpal ldan bdag ni rdo rje 'dzin// bsrung ba'i 'khor

132a1: lo rab sbyor bas/ / bdag gis ye shes rdo rje yis// lus ngag yid du bcas pa dag/ sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag nyid ni// khro bo gshin rje nag pa bdag/ slob dpon gyis ni dkyil 'khor bri// zhes
132a2: lan gsum gyi bar du brjod par bya'o/ / dkyil 'khor gyi ni drung nyid du// dar gyis gdong ni bkab pa la// sgo drug gnas pa khyod gang yin// slob dpon gyis ni rab brjod de// dri bdag skal pa ldan par brjod/
132a3: de ltar tha med dpa' bo yis// mgon la dbang ni bskur bar bzhin// bla med byang chub gnas bya'i phyir// bdag la'ang mgon pos dbang skur gsol// me tog sogs te mchod pa'i mchog/ rab 'byam rgya mtsho/
132a4: ma lus pas// slob dpon dpa' bo de nyid la// yang yang mchod cing bstod pa'i tshogs// rgyas par mnyes bya de 'og tu// dpa' bos de la dbang rnams sbyin// de nas rgyal po bde chen po// dpa' bo longs
132a5: spyod kun ldan pa/ / dgro don brtson pa'i sku gsum bdag/ nyid kyis 'di skad bka' stsal to// sbyin sreg med na 'bras mi sbyin// de bas bdag nyid dam pa yis// de yi las la 'bad par bya// gos nag
132a6: rgyan gyis rnam rgyan la/ / gshin rjes rnam bltas rnal 'byor pas// khro bo'i dkyil dkrung bcas pa yis// sra ba'i stan la bdag 'dug nas// las rnams bsgrub par bya ba ni// mtshan mo 'am nyi ma phyed nyid
132a7: na/ / raM byung me'i dkyil 'khor du// hUM phaT mtha' na yod pa yi// sngags kyis thog ma bar tha mA// sbyin bsreg bya ste de me ni// dur khrod me 'am rus pa'am// rdo nyid las ni byung ba'am// tsan Da li yi khyim nyid
132a8: nas/ / thab khung gru gsum can der ni// tshe ram can gyi bud shing brdzang // brlung yab sbar te hUM dz+wa la raM// dza la hUM brjod me sbar brjod// lag g.yas ku sha bcas pa yis// mthe bo srin lag rtsa ru gzugs// oM

132b1: e h+ye hi ma hA b+hA ta de ba ri dri dza sa gam thaM hi ta a hUM ti ha ram a smin saM ni hi to b+hA ba zhes brjod la spyan drang ngo / / 'bar ba me yi dbus nyid du// ming de zad byed ces bya ba// khro bo me ltar phun sum tshogs// pa sU
132b2: kham pa de bzhin du/ / du mdog zur mig steng du gzigs// sgra che mche ba bzhi ldan stobs po che// yaM las rlung gi dkyil 'khor te// bzhugs nas drag po'i yi ge brjod// spyan gsum pa la phyag bzhi pa/
132b3: rig pa'i gnas la legs par zhugs// zhal bdun rnam rtsigs ma he la// byibs pa du ba'i phreng rnams 'khrigs// phyag gnyis mdud dang rdo rje 'dzin// gnyis kyis ral gri gri gug 'dzin// de yi g.yas kyi
132b4: phyogs nyid du/ / de bzhin mdun gyi phyogs nyid dam// spyan drangs byin brlabs ldan pa la// a sgra sogs kyi mchod paH// oM a r+d+ha ma pra tI ts+tsha swA hA// lag g.yas 'dzub mo mtha bong dag/ skam pa lta
132b5: rnam byas pas/ / chu blangs bgyod pas dbul bar bya// oM ba ta mthar ni mngon gyis brjod// zhabs bkru pa la shis pa yis// dgang gzar yu ba sor bcu drug/ de min sor ba zhi thabs sor gnyis// zung
132b6: gsum dbus su sor gnyis chad/ / rtse gsum phreng bas yongs su bskor// de yi dbus su'ang mtshan ma ste// stag sbrul gang 'dod pas mtshan bya// khra bcud 'dzag pa sor gcig go// khro bo rdo rje mchu yi
132b7: dbyibs/ / byin brlabs sor gcig chad can no// thugs gzar yu ba sor bcu bzhi// zabs su sor gcig gru gsum dang // yu ba'i mthar ni rtse gsum pa// gdengs pa byin brlabs mngon spyod kyi// gzar bu
132b8: yin par nga yis bstan/ / gnam lugs cher ma can sogs shing // de la de byas sangs rgyas 'jig/ bsreg rdzas gzugs brnyan la sogs pasreg/ stong du chang bas 'bras bu ni// nges par 'byin par byed

133a1: ba yin/ / g.yon gyi rtsa der dgang gzar la// g.yas pa blugs pa'i gzar bu yin// kha ni pad ma'i mdab ma yin// sor mo gnyis par bde rgyas so// rdo rje bar gyi thod pa dag/ bsreg rdzas kyi ni sdod
133a2: yin la/ / rdzas rnams rdo rje rin chen dpa'// hUM phaT kyi ni mtha' can gyis// bsreg byas chu me dang rlung // nam mkha' lta bu'i dbus su gnas// kha bye gnas pa rtag du'o// kun du'ang kha phye bskor bar bya// gzhi gaN+DI
133a3: mdab ma'i steng du ste/ / lte ba dang ni yang dag ldan// lhan cig rnam par shes pa'i lha// nam mkha' nyid du nges par 'bar// de yi mtshan mar shes bya ba// rdul gyi rnam par de nyid do// thig le yi ge med pa ste//
133a4: rkun mi 'chad par 'od kyis gnas// brgyar bshags sgra yi tshad kyis so// ar+g+has rab tu sbar bar bya// sngar gsungs 'byung ba rnam bzhi dang // nam mkhar yang dag ldan pa yi// sor mo lnga dang nges ldan pas//
133a5: gang gi sbyin bsreg des bya'o// gzhan dag sor mo gsum gyis bsreg/ dmigs pa thams cad 'gags par 'gyur// rten med stong pa nam mkha' 'dra// shes rab pha rol phyin pa yi// phyag rgya chen po
133a6: dbang du 'gyur/ / bde gshegs kun dang mnyam 'gyur ba// shes rab dang ni snying rje ches// 'gag pa med pa'i chos 'gyur ro// bde chen nam mkha' lta bu ste// rnal 'byor pa yi dmigs pa yin// mdog nag/
133a7: mdab brgyad lta bu la// rgya dang zabs su sor mo ni// nyi shu de bzhin bcu pa'i thab// byang du rtse mo bstan pa la// rdo rje tho ba'i mtshan ma de// sor ni bzhi par bri bar bya// de steng sor mo gsum bor bar// kha khyer
133a8: kyang ni de yi tshad/ / sa nag bong bu rnga mo'i spangs// mi rus 'bras kyi phub ma dang // sol ba'i phye mas rnam thugs la// mi zhim dri dang bdug pas mchod// dur khrod shing ngam bong bu dang // rnga mo'i spangs skam bung shig//

133b1: sor gcig gis ni dma' ba yin// nim bde bzhin seng ldeng dang // se bde bzhin pas shing dang // dur khrod shing bu sor bcu pa// rtsa ba'i cha las rnam byung ba// dur khrod mar bu rnams brlags la// de yis yam/
133b2: shing bya ba yin// bya rog 'ug pa'i gshog pa dang // nim pa'i 'dab ma thal ba dang // rkang rjes sa dang bung bu dang // rnga mo sogs kyi spangs dang ni// skra dang zhag dang bshang ba dang // gci ba mi dris yungs dkar dang /
133b3: yungs mar dag dang lan tshwa dang // de las sogs pa re re zhing // ji ltar rnyed pa'i rdzas rnams ni// dug dang khrag dang smyo byed kyi// mdab khung bal bsol ba dang // 'bras kyi phug ma la sog/ la// dgra bo dag gi
133b4: gzugs byas la/ / mgo nas brtsams te ral gri yis// dum bur gtub cing lcags phur du// khrag dang chu dang mi rnams dang // bong bu'i gcin la phaT ldan pa'i// gdug pa'i yi ge rnams bzlas pa'i/
133b5: rdzas la bsang gtor byas nas kyang // slob dpon la sdang rmongs pa 'di// brjod cing sbyin bsreg dbul bar bya// de la 'di skad ces bya ste// 'byung po chemi bya gtor ma dang // bstod bzlas mnyes par bya ba dang // dbang
133b6: gidabye ba bstan pa dang / / dkyil 'khor 'jug par bya ba dang // de yi sa la mchod pa sogs// cod pan du ni bde gshegs gzhag/ mngon spyod hom gyi cho ga dang // bsdus nas bar du rnam pa brgyad// pad ma
133b7: dkar 'dra mgrin pa ring / / gzugs mdzes ha cang ring ba min// lus la rdul 'byung yid 'phrog ma// dri ni shin du 'ang zhim pa yin// lta stangs mi sogs ri dgas 'dra// mgrin dang lto ba'ang ri dgas kyi// skal
133b8: bzangs rked pa'ang ri dgas kyi/ / glang chen dri ldan bzhin 'phel che// myos shing nu ma rab tu rgyas// gzhan yang kun rdzob bden pa ni// bong thung de yi sra yang thung // rkang lag ring shing bzhin ring ma// nya yi dri bro bong

134a1: ring ma/ / zla 'dra skye gnas rab tu ring // skye gnas chung zhing yan lag chub// bong ring de bzhin nu ma mkhrang// sra srab dal smra yan lag chung // sngo bsangs ri mo mnyam pa de// gsang ba shes rab rnam
134a2: gnyis la/ / rig ma rang yis bsgrags pa yin// dad pa'i 'gros dang bsgra 'khyil ma// bzhin zlum nu rgyas lus kyang rgyas// shin du ring man dal bar smra// dbus nas rna 'chang gnyer gsum can//
134a3: mtshan nyid ngan zhing le lo che// yan lag nag cing sgra 'khyil la// khang par gnas shing lus rtsub ma// sa la'i dri 'byung sa li bri// nu spangs de ni skyes bu bzhin// chang gis myos pa'i dpa' mo ste// chang la
134a4: shin tu chags pa yin/ / de gnyis de la shis pa yin// tha ma tha mar nges par yin// 'chi ba'i bsam gtan de nyid ni// bde ba dam pa kho bos 'dod// 'di la'ang bde ba de nyid yin// ka sogs spangs pa'i
134a5: a li ni/ / bcu drug yin te phrag gnyis po// 'khor lo sogs pa'i sa bon yin// zla ba de dag sum bcu gnyis// a sags spangs pa'i kA li ste// bcu bdun gnyis pa de stengs su// ya sogs spangs
134a6: pamin panyid/ / gsum pa'i gsum dang bzhi pa'i gnyis// bcu phrag bzhi ste de phrag gnyis// senam pangs sogs sa ban su// nyi mar rnam sngags de dbus gnas// hUM dpa sa yi rang bzhi na las/
134a7: sogs so sor rtog/ thim pas nan gtan ye shes te// chos kyi dbyings nyid dag pa ste// gshin dgrar bdag nyid 'dod pa yin// rgyan gyis bye brag lus la gnas// de ni 'di skad bya ba ste// rig pa shes rab
134a8: bstan pa dang / / bskyed pa'i rgyu yi bye brag ni// tha mar bstan te sdom gsum mo// mtshon par byed pa'i bdag nyid de// mtshon ma sngon bstan nyid yin no// gshin rje gshed nag po'i las thams cad grub par byed

134b1: pa'i 'khor lo'i rgyud chud kyi rgyal po rdzogs so/ / / pa tita pA ro phyag rdum gyi zhal snga nas/ ra rdo rje grags kyis bskur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/
134b2: rgya gar skad du/ shI badz+ra ma hA b+hai ra ba nA ma tan tra// bod skad du/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sa bya ba/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po khros pa'i rgyal po chen po la phyag 'tshal lo//

134b4: rung bar gnas la dgos pa thams cad bsgrub par bya'o/ / de la gnas gsungs pa ni/ ru khrod dam// chu klung gi 'gram mam/ shing gcig gam/ mtshan ma gcig pa 'am/ bzhi mdo 'am/ ri'i rtse mo 'am/
134b5: khang stong ngam/ ma mo'i khyim mam/ lha'i khang pa 'am/ 'thab mo'i gnas sam/ grong khyer ram/ nags khrod dam/ khrong par la sogs pa'i gnas su sngags pa gnas te/ nga la rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po'i rdo rje'i

135a1: rta babs bzhi yis rnam par brgyan// dril bu dar gyi 'phan la sogs// me tog phreng bas rnam par krugs// grwa rnams dag ni thams cad dang // sgo khyud kyi ni phug dag tu// rdo rje rin chen gyis spras pa/

135a3: rgyu ma byang du rkang pa gnyis/ shar gyi grang thod pa/ lhor thod tshal/ nub byang du dur khrod kyi ras/ byang shar du skyes bu gsal zhing la btsugs pa'o// de dag ni 'khor lo'i dbus su mtshan ma'i phyag rgya'o//

136a1: las thams cad nges par 'grub pa/ / 'di ni 'jam dpal zhes bya ba'i ming dpal rdo rje 'jigs byad chen po'i 'khor lo'i skyer ba'i rgyud las dkyil 'khor bstan pa'i sa rtog pa dang po'o// de nas

136a3: dang po kho nar sngags pas re shig gnod mdzes su bya ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rnal 'byor gtso bo yin pa'i phyir ro// rnal 'byor gyi rgyud la lha'i sbyor ba dang ldan pas thod ma ni bye ste/ myo ba po yin pa'i phying ro/ pa di ba
136a4: ltar gsad par 'gyur 'dod pa'i sngags pas dur khrod kyi ras la/ drag dang khrag dang / lan tsha dang / skye tshe dang / nim pa dang / d+ha dra ra'i khra ba yis rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po'i 'khor lo li tshe bcu drug pa bya
136a5: rog chen po'i sgro rtse'i smyu gu'am/ mi'i rus pa'i smyu gus skyes bu sgra bshig pas kha lhor bltas te/ ma he'i gdong gi sbyor bas bri bar bya'o// me gnyis kyi dbus su bsgrub bya'i ming dang bcas par bzhag
136a6: la de yi ge bcu pas bskor zhing hUM brgyad bri/ / zur rnams su phaT kyi yi ge rnams bri// bdag nyid tsha ba'i mar gyis lus byugs la/ thod pa gnyis kyi dbus su 'khrul 'khor rab tu btsug la

136a8: yang rims kyis thebs par 'dod na 'khor lo de nyid mi'i nya phyis gnyis kyis dbus su legs par bzhag la me thab kyi 'og tu zu phyed brko sa la bcug nas me sbar na rims nad kyis 'dzin no/ / de la le che

136b1: bcwa drug pa'i rang gyur ba 'di gsungs te/ 'on kyang 'di'i lda par ni yig sum bcun gnyis pa'i sngags dang ldan pa lag bcu pa'i sngags pabartsub pa'i ming dang lhan cig tu mi ge dang sngags stsal lo// sngon du gsungs/

136b3: na 'chi bar 'gyur ro/ / shing gcig gi drung du sbas na bskrad par 'gyur ro// mtshan ma gcig par sbas na dbye bar 'gyur ro// chu'i nang du sbas na rengs par 'gyur ro// khyim du bzhag na zhi bar 'gyur ro// phyung nas
136b4: legs par bkrus na grol bar 'gyur ro/ / gzhan yang rab tu sbyor ba gsungs pa gshin rje'i 'khor lo sngon gyi tshogs dur khrod kyi ras la bris te/ dur khrod dam/ lam bzhi mdo dang / shing gcig dang / grogs mkhar
136b5: dang chu 'gram dang / mtshan ma gcig pa pa dang / rgyal po'i sgo dang / rnam par snang mdzad dang / rdo rje chu dang / dur khrod kyi sol bas bsgrub bya'i gzugs brnyan tshad sor brgyad pa byas la de'i snying khar 'khor lo'i sngags
136b6: bcug ste/ / mi'i rus pa'i phur bus gnas lngar gdab par bya'o// tshigs thams cad la tsher ma rnon pos dgad par bya ro// de thod pa gnyis kyi dbus su bcug ste/ de grog mkhar dang gnas bdun gyi sas
136b7: gshin rje'i gzugs khru gang tsam zhal gtsigs pa/ gsus pa che ba/ zhal gcig pa/ phyag gnyis pa/ phyag na ral gri dang / zhags pa 'dzin pa/ gcer bu sgra gsil ba byas la/ de'i snying khar thod pa gnyis

180b2: mngon par rab tu dang bas ro bcung thams cad myong shing longs spyod par 'gyur ro/ / rdo rje gsor zhing dril bu dal gyis la khrol bas gnas de la bstod par bya'o// gti mug dga' ma la sogs pa rnams la byi/
180b3: nas mngon par 'dod pa zhus te mchod pa'i mthar bzhad pa'i sngags rnam pa brgyad brjod par bya ste/ de la sngags 'dis gshegs su gsol lo// hA hA he hai ho ho hUM hU~M/ ba~M sa ra t+na ye ta/ oM AHmu zhes pas kyang /
180b4: ro// phyi nas sgrub pa po'i mngon par 'dod pas/ sems can kun gyi don mdzad phyir// ji ltar rjes 'jug dngos grub stsol// sangs rgyas yul du gshegs nas kyang // slar yang 'dir ni byon par zhu// de bzhin
180b5: gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs gshin rje gshed dmar po'i rgyud las gtor ma'i rim par phye ba ste bcu gcig pa'o/ / // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
180b6: kyis bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa' chen po la bstod pa mdzad de/ gti mug rdo rje'i rang bzhin khyod// gshin rje gshed po shin du 'jigs// ston pa sangs rgyas kun rang bzhin// rdo rje'i sku la phyag 'tshal
180b7: bstod/ / phra ma rdo rje'i rang bzhin khyod// gshin rje gshed po shin tu 'jigs// rdo rje'i thugs dang rab mtshungs pa// rin chen rdo rje phyag 'tshal bstod// 'dod chags rdo rje'i rang bzhin khyod// 'dod chags
180b8: chos kyi 'byung gnas gtso/ / gsung mchog kun gyi rab mchog ste// rdo rje'i gsung la phyag 'tshal bstod// brag dog rdo rje'i rang bzhin khyod// gshin rje gshed po las kun pa// rdo rje'i sku dang rab

181a1: mtshungs pa/ / phyag na ral gri phyag 'tshal bstod// sangs rgyas kun gyi rang bzhin khyod// sangs rgyas thams cad gcig bsdus pa// sangs rgyas kun gyi rab mchog gtso// dkyil 'khor
181a2: dbang phyug phyag 'tshal bstod/ / rdo rje'i mig dang rdo rje'i rna ba dang rdo rje'i sna dang rdo rje'i lce dang rdo rje'i lus dang rdo rje'i yid ces bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa na mig la sogs pa byin gyis brlab pa'i
181a3: dam tshig go/ de nas gshin rje gshed 'jigs kyi// dkyil 'khor bdag gis rab bshad bya// gshin rje gshed po dang mtshungs pa// don rnams thams cad sgrub byed pa// srad bu gsar pa legs bsgrim
181a4: shing / / mdzes shing tshad dang yang dag ldan// gshin rje gshed kyi dkyil 'khor la// shes rab can gyis thig gdab bo// mtshan nyid thams cad yongs rdzogs pa// don med thams cad rnam par 'jig
181a5: zhi ba la sogs rab sgrub pa'i/ / maNaN la dkyil 'khor rnam pa la// las kyi rdo rje bri byA ste// de la rtse lnga mtha' dag la// de'i dbus su rdo rje bri// rdo rje 'bar bas kun du 'khrigs// shar gyi rtsibasal
181a6: 'khor lo bri/ / 'khor lo'i 'od zer kun du 'khrigs// lho ru rin chen bri byas ste// 'od zer phreng bas kun du khyab// nub tu pad ma bri bya ste// pad ma rA ga'i 'od zer mdzes// byang du ral gri bri bya ste/
181a7: sprin gyi kha dog 'od zer mtshungs// shar gyi 'tshams su 'khor lo bri// lho ru rdo rje bri bar bya// nub tu pad ma thi bya ste// pad ma gdong bcas rgyas pa'i zhal// byang du ral gri bri bya ste// 'od zer lnga dang
181a8: mtshungs par ldan/ / shar gyi ga/ ru thob ste// rdo rje dazug pa lho ru'o// rub kyi sgo ru u gyes te// rdo rje ral gyibang du'o// dkyil 'khor rdzogs par shes byas la// byad par can gyis mchod bya ba// 'dod pa'i

181b1: n a bya smyan ga la
181b2: sa / / danas bco bldan 'das bzhid ga shegs pamams cad kyisaldan 'das bzhin gshegs thathams cad kyi dig du chen po la bad pa
181b3: 'dis gsol ba gdab bo/ / phyag rgya gsungs pas rab sbyor ba// gang gis rdo rje rnams la bstod// phyag rgya rdo rje'i phyag rgya yis// dngos grub mang po sgrub par mdzod// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'chang// tshig
181b4: 'di dag ni gsung bar mdzad/ / dkyil 'khor ba rnams thams cad kyi// spyi bor gshin rje gshed po bsgom// rtag tu dkyil 'khor zum byas la// rtag tu sbyin pasreg mchod pa bya// rtag tu dam tshig
181b5: bsgrub bya zhing / / de yi sdom pa gzung bar bya// dang po cod pan dbang bskur te// gnyis pa ral gri sbyin par bya// gsum pa rdo rje dril bus te// bzhi pa zla ba'i bza' ba'o// dbang bskur chen po bzhi pa ni/
181b6: ra ka ta yi zhal nas byung // dbang bskur 'di yi mthu yis ni// byang chub rgyal ba'i ro bcud 'thob// de nas bdag gis sngags bshad pas// 'byung po kun la gtor ma bya// sngags chen po ni brjod pa
181b7: yis/ / 'byung po thams cad rab tu 'bar// sngags kyis bon hrIHSh+T+rIHsogs// mthar ni sA spa nges par sbyar// biT ma tra chub zes kyis// maN+DaDal zur gsum byas nas ni// lha rnams mnyes bya rnal
181b8: 'byor bas/ / nA hA nes grogs slar dran bya// 'khor lo rim gsum bya ba ni// brgyad dang bcu gnyis bcu drug rnams// mkhas pas cho ga bzhin du zi// sngags ni kun du dgod par bya// brtul zhugs

182a1: can gyis bcu gnyis par/ / grub pa'i sngags rnams dgod par bya// khams gsum g.yo dang mi g.yo ba// ma lus lus pa med pa 'grub// ya ma rA dzA sa de ma ya/ ya me do ru Na yo da ya/
182a2: yang yo ni ra ya k+She ya/ ya ke ya ts+tsha ni rA ma ya/ ya dbus k+She ni shar du ste// ma yig 'jam pa'i rdo rje lhor// me yig nub tu bri bar bya// byang du ni dkar po ste// bsgrub bya'i ming ni bzung byas nas// stong
182a3: ba'i mtshams la dgod par bya/ / hUM gnyis dag gis brten par bya// dgos pa thams cad sgrub par byed// ya tsA ni ra/ dzA sa do ru/ Na yo ni ra/ zhes pas kyang ni phyi rol du// g.yon nas brtsams zhing
182a4: yang dag bri/ / don kun rab tu bsgrub pa'i phyir// re mig gsum pa'i mdun nas ni// re mig cha re spangs par ni// shar nas brtsams te bri bar bya// hrIHSh+T+rIHzhes pa'i sngags rnams kyis// re mig
182a5: brgyad kyi bar bar du/ / re mig rnams la yang dag bri// che ge mo ku ru mA ra ya// ud tsa tA ya/ ba shI ku ru/ bi de Sha ya/ shAM ta~M ku ru/ puSh+TiM ku ru/ zhes pa la sogs pa ni las kyi rjes su 'brangs te/
182a6: oM ni dang por na maHmthar// mthar ni bsha bo ShaT// hU~M phaT yi ge dang ldan pas// ni rgyas dbang du byed pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs gshin rje gshed dam po'i
182a7: rgyud las dbang bskur ba dang 'khrul 'khor gyi snang ba zhes bya ba'i rim par bya ba ste bcu gsum pa'o/ / // bcom ldan 'das kyis brtse bar mdzad// gshin rje gshed chen yang dag gzugs//
182a8: zhozhe sdang gis mnan 'gro la gzigs// zhe sdang thams cad zad par mdzad// bcom ldan 'das kyis brtse bar mdzad// gti mug gshin rje gshed mchog gzugs// gti mug gis mnan 'grol

182b1: gzigs/ / gti mug thams cad zad par mdzad// bcom ldan 'das kyis brtse bar mdzad// phra ma gshin rje gshed mchog gzugs// phra mas mnan pa'i 'gro la gzigs// phra ma thams cad zad
182b2: par mdzad/ / bcom ldan 'das kyis brtse bar mdzad// 'dod chags gshin rje gshed mchog gzugs// 'dod chags kyis mnan 'gro la gzigs// 'dod chags thams cad zad par mdzad//
182b3: bcom ldan 'das kyis brtse bar mdzad// phrag dog gshin rje gshed mchog gzugs// phrag dog gis mnan 'gro la gzigs// phrag dog thams cad zad par mdzad// byams bcar tsi kAr
182b4: gsungs te/ / phag mo de bzhin snying rje'o// dbyangs can dga' bar shes bya ste// btang snyoms gau rI'i gzugs su'o// bdag nyid dngos po thams cad kyis// slar yang dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs
182b5: pa/ / rnal 'byor snying kha'i sa bon spro// mgrub 'gyur 'di la the tshom med// de nas spyod pa'i mtshan nyid mchog/ bdag gis yang dag bshad par bya// gshin rje gshed po'i 'jigs gzugs kyi//
182b6: sku dang gsung dang thugs rnams dag/ dgon pa chen po'i phyogs rnams la// mahe mchog la zhon byas te// sngal gyi rgyan gyis rnam par brgyan// lugs kyi rdo rje bsgom par bya// sra ni dam nge sar dgyed
182b7: du 'khyil/ / khyad du 'phags pa'i gzugs can bya// mgo la thod pas yang dag bskor// dmar dmang ser badz+ras pa ste// hrIHSh+T+rIHla sogs sngags rnams brjod// rdo rje dbyug pa yang dag gsor/
182b8: gshin rje gshed kyi rnal 'byor pas// seng ge'i sgra ni bklag par bya// cung zad mthu ni thob pa yis// grong khyer zhugs te rol par bya// rab mdzes gar ni bya ba dang // drug 'gyur la sogs glu blang ngo //

183a1: srang du rgyal mtshan dubalta zhing // de la 'o ma rab tu bsgrub// 'o ma la 'dris rtse gcig sems// phyag rgya chen po rab bsgrub bya// phrag mo'i gzugs su bsgom byas la// 'dod pa'i mtha' la btsun ma
183a2: kun/ / seng ge bzhin du 'jigs med pas// 'dod don kun 'grub rnal 'byor pa'i// de nas lag brgya rab bsgrub pa// bdag gis yang dag rab bshad bya// yi ge gcig gi sngags chen te// de yi bzlas pa nges
183a3: par bshad/ / hrIHyig sa bon las byung ba'i// ma he'i gdong ba rnam par bsgom// rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor la gnas pa// ma he'i steng du bsgom par bya// gang zhig sa la gnas pa yi// sna tshogs mtshon cha'i
183a4: rang gzugs rnams/ / blo dang ldan pas lag na bsgom// ma he'i gdong can sgrub pa'o// de nas rdo rje dbyug pa yi// sgrub thabs bdag gis rab bshad bya// yi ge hrIHni gsang sngags che// ma he chen po la zhon pa/
183a5: 'bum phrag gnyis ni rdzogs pa'i phyag/ thal ba'i rdul gyis lus la byugs// ri rab bzhin du mtho ba la// ro ldan 'og tu yang dag gnon// de nas phyag ni bye ba yi// sgrub thabs bdag gis rab bshad bya/
183a6: wi kri tA na na gsang sngags che// hUM yig las byung gtso bo ste// oM wi kri tA na na haM hA hiHhoHhUM hUM he heHhoHhaHswA hA// dgos pa thams cad rab sgrub pa'i// dam tshig sgrub pa 'dir bshad do// sngags kyis dub

183a8: chen lus la mngon par byug/ 'di yis lus la blugs tsam gyis// 'gro ba mtha' dag dbang du byed// rnam snang sin du pA ranya tsa// de bzhin bil ba'i lo ma dang // so phag phye ma lhan cig tu// gser shing

183b1: lo ma'i khu ba rnams/ / 'di yis lus la dril phyis bya// rdo rje chen po'i bdud rtsi bzhin// rang 'byung me tog btung ba bzhin// 'di ni rnal 'byor rab mchog go// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang

183b3: ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs pa dang / / rdo rje phag mo'i rnam pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs pa dang / dbyangs can ma'i rnam pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs pa dang / gau rI ma'i rnam pa'i ting

184a1: gas pa' thung bas rab sgrub bya// ban pa bcu banal// dudaHla dang ldan pa mas// shal mas ni thug paraH// zlas pa yis na dngas tha / sa sa na par yul/

184b1: don gyi bying su mdog dmang ba'o/ / spyan gsum ni 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang dkar gyi dus gsum so// phyag gnyis na dngas pa dang dadas pa med pa'i rnam par rtog pa rnams 'dams pa'o// shes

184b6: dang 'gog pa dang lam gyi bden par bshad do/ / sgo bzhi ni bdud bzhi skrag par byed pa'o// zur bzhi ni tshangs pa'i gnas bzhi rab tu rdzogs pa'i phyir ro// ka ba brgyad ni sgyu ma'i dpe brgyad kyi phyir te/ sprul pa'i

185a1: khams kyi dbus song nas/ / nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor mchog bsams te// rtse lnga pa ni rnam par bsgom// de'i steng du pad ma dgod// 'di mdog nag las 'jigs chen mo// phyag drug mdzes pa'i

185b1: dun phyin byud pa byud/ / gangs ldan pa da u0f7f// chud bzhi na pa // na mamo gas // nga du la pa dag dab na/ mgag thas dang ma me dang / drarnamamams

186a1: kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs gshin rje gshed dmar po'i rgyud las dngos grub nges pa'i rim par phye ba ste bcu drug pa'o/ / // de la 'dir thig gdab pa'i dam tshig mchog ni/ a kA ro mu khaM sarba
186a2: d+har+m+ma NA mA d+ha nud pan nad tra/ / dpal ldan gshin rje mthar byed gzugs// slob ma rnam par snang mdzad bya// ye shes thig mchog rtse dag bzung // mnyam gzhag nas ni legs par gdab//
186a3: del 'di ni dkyil 'khor chen por rab tu 'jug pa'i dam tshig go/ oM AHhUM/ dkyil 'khor nyis 'gyur ring ba la// sgo yi nyi shu cha yis sdom// ba yi rnam lngas legs par thug/ skud
186a4: pa gnyis su med par brtag/ de la 'di ni rdo rje chen por rab tu 'jug pa'i dam tshig ste/ kye ma sangs rgyas slob dpon che// kye ma chos dang tshogs kyi gtso// dam tshig de nyid bdag la stsol/
186a5: byang chub sems kyang bdag la byin// de la 'di ni sa chen po yongs su gzung ba'i dam tshig go// rdo rjes yi lha mo spyan drangs la// skyob pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// spyod pa'i tshul dang khyad par dang /
186a6: sa dang pha rol phyin pa la// lha mo khyod ni dbang du gyur// sgo ni dkyil 'khor brgyad cha ru// bdag nyid chen pos shes bya ste// khams chen po ni ma gtogs pa'i// tshad ldan shin tu mdzes pa'o// sgo dang sgo khyud
186a7: des shes bya/ / de yi byed kyis snam bu ste// glum rngam gar ma sogs// rdo rje'i lha mo yang dag ldan// de yi byed kyis rdul tshon sa// sgo yi phyed kyis 'gram dang logs// 'dir yang dra ba dra byed dang // nyi ma zla ba ma
186a8: dog phreng / / lha'i rnam bu dang po'i tshad// de bzhin phyi yi dkyil 'khor ro// de la snying po chen po 'di// bdag gis 'khor lo nam mkhar dgod// rang gi phyag rgya'ang de ru brten// dam tshig ye shes gzhug byas nas/

186b1: dkyil 'khor rab tu bsgrub par bya// shar du dkar po chen po ste// lho ru ser po dang ldan pa// dmar po nub kyi cha la ste// byang du ma ra ka kA ldan// in+d+ra nI la'i 'od mtshungs pa// dbus kyi sa gzhir yang dag bri// las
186b2: kyi cho ga mthong ba yis/ / de yi phyag rgya dgod par bya// dbus su rdo rje yang dag bri// sha ral 'khor lo legs par bri// de ltar bu las sogs par blta// phyag rgya rtag tu nam mkha' mtshungs// de la thugs gzar
186b3: dgang gzar tshad/ / 'di yi tshad kyis yu ba bya// khwa gang tshad dang ldan pa la// de yi rtse mor dkyil 'khor bya// sor mo bzhi yi tshad ldan la// gting du sor gnyis zab pa la// de la so re byad bcud lung du/
186b4: thugs gzar pad ma'i rnam pa bzhin// mthe bo'i lto gad tshad la ni// gting du sor mo'i tshad ldan no// rgyud 'di la ni rab tu sngags// dkyil 'khor du ni ma zhugs shing // mtshams med lnga ni byas pa dang // gang
186b5: gis srog chags gsod pa dang / / nya dang sha sogs za ba dang // tshang dang 'dod ma la chags dang // char lha'i brtul zhugs 'dzin pa dang // mngon par dbang ni ma bskur dang // bya ba ma yin byed spro dang // grong khyer dbyen byed
186b6: bas kyang ni/ / dmar po'i gsung ni ji lta bar// gshin rje gshed rgyud mchog la gzhol// 'grub 'gyur 'di la the tshom med// de nas byams pa la sogs pa'i rdo rje'i byang chub sems dpa' kun gyis rdo rje chen po'i

186b8: g.yo bar byed/ / rkang pa dag gi 'og tu yaM// lte bar raM ste snying kha ra laM// mgo bo la ni paM yig go/ gzhu yi rnam pa nag po che// gtum po'i rlung ni 'jigs byed pa// sreg byed zur gsum me bzhin 'bar// nyi ma dmar

187a1: po'i 'od dang mtshungs/ / rdo rjes gzhi'i rim pa ni// ser po chen po gru bzhi pa// ri rab ri yis mnan pa yi// nor 'dzin de ni bsgom par bya// dkar po zlum po bum pa bzhin// sprin bzhin dun char
187a2: 'dzin/ / stong gis rab tu gang ba yi// gangs kyi ri bo lta bu rabasil// gnas bzhi rab tu sbyor ba yis// slob ma rdo rje can la bsgom// rdo rje snang ba mtha' yas sbyor// myur ba nyid du 'bebapa par byed// de la 'di
187a3: ni dri ba'i dam tshig go/ rdo rje chos ni mgon chen po// snang ba mtha' yas bde ba che// gsungs shig 'dod chags chos chen po// dge dang mi dge legs par 'dri// khru gang nas ni bzung nas ni// ji srid khru ni stong gi
187a4: bar/ / slob ma chen po 'phar bar 'gyur// 'di ni dbab pa'i dam tshig go// ri mo bri ba'i mtshan nyid rnams// bdag gis yang dag bshad par bya// sa ni snum pa blangs byas la// brtul zhugs can gyis gnan
187a5: par bya/ / sran gre de bzhin 'o ma sha// bu ram pas yab la sogs pa// til dang nim pa'i lo ma dang // de bzhin nA Di'i sa bon no// dang po dkar po bri bar bya// de la kha dog gzhan gyis bri// thod lo dkor dang btsag dag

187a7: po mtshal gyis so/ / ka ped khu ba de la sbyin// chung ngus ma yin lhag de bzhin// lhag pas nag po dman pa yis// skye bo ru ni 'gro bar byed// khro dang zhi ba rnam gnyis kyi// gzugs kyi mtshan nyid bshad par bya//

192b2: mug bag chags 'dod chags dang // zhe sdang rdo rje 'khor lor gnas// re rab nye zla ba don las// 'byung bzhi'i rdo rje de bzhin no// khyams bzhir me long po bo dang // dri mchog zhal zas las byung ba// gzugs

192b6: med pa zung bzhi yin/ / dran dang dbang po sgo bzhi ste// bsam gtan bzhi ni rta babs bzhi// rnam thar brgyad phyir ka ba brgyad// byang chub yan lag bdun dag phyir// dra ba dang ni dra ba byed// phyogs bzhir

193a1: 'khrig pa dag/ pu dza.a a gong dem// ka ma hA ko kA la ka te// bra gras sun sa ma ku// tanya h+ya ho ho ta// a i u ma ma a// rnam pa sna tshogs rnam par smin// rnam par 'jogs

193a5: dang 'gro 'od sbyar/ / lus med sems ni ci bder 'gro// bsnyems nas 'gro zhing 'bar bar byed// dbang du byed dang kha sbyar bsgom// 'dun pas bsgrub dang sa bon bsgyur// 'phen dran par dor don sgrub
193a6: 'gyur/ / tshe 'di yi ni de bzhin du// nying mtshams sbyor dang srid mtshams yang // rnal 'byor rgyal po thabs ldan pas// bde chen sa gsum bde blag 'gro// srid zhi dag dang nges pa dang // rten 'brel

193a8: kun tu bsgrub pa'o/ / oM a kA ro mu khaM sarba d+harma naM a d+ya nud pa na nad tra ta sarba ni swa b+hA ba hUM/ bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rje losogapa

193b1: 'khor de dag thams cad rab tu yid rangs te/ tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod cing mchod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa thams cad kyis mchod pa la brtson par gyur te/ 'jig rten mgon po
193b2: bcom ldan legs/ 'gro ba nyon mongs bskyab slad du// stong pa'i ting 'dzin spangs nas ni// khyod kyis byams chen skur bstan mdzad// thugs rje chen po bcom ldan legs// sems can sdug bsngal
193b3: bsgral phreng du/ / zhi ba'i mtha' la mi gnas par// brtse chen rnam par 'phrul par mdzad// bde chen rgyal po bcom ldan legs// lus can bde don bsgrub slad du// zag med dbyings thugs mi gzhos
193b4: bar/ / dgyes chen kun du snang mdzad lags// gtso bo rdo rje rgyal po legs// skye bo dub pa dal bso'i phyir// mtha' gcig rgyun chad mi bzhugs par// ma lus 'tshal bsgrub pa spang// de nas 'khor gyi

194a1: 'gyur ro/ / me 'amamam yin pa la sogs pa'i gnad tha thams cad dang / 'a dang / yang ba dang / bkru pags pa thams cad 'byung bar ma 'gyur // gang gi ba na gnas pa ya
194a2: mchod rten du bya bar 'gyur ro/ / rig pa dang dngos grub thab cad kyi gter tshad med par 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' de dag dang / lha dang / mi dang /

195a1: de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po chen po zla gsang thig le skul bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ rang gi thugs kyi gsang ba'i thig le las shin tu dgyes pa

196a1: sdang bas snang bar byas te/ da kyi thugs kyi zla ba'i thig le la stug po gcig tu gyur nas bzhugs te/ thugs kyi zla ba'i thig pa'i dbus su 'od zer des dgyes par bskyed cing drangs na

197a1: kun tu sdug bsngal yongs bral te/ / che ba'i ye shes lhun gyis grub mchog ldan pa bde spyod bde la rol par mdzod// ya la ga du gas pa yis// shin tu srid pas mya ngan 'das
197a2: dga' chen de bzhin gshegs pa rnams/ / dkyil 'khor 'di la byin gyis rlob// de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje bde ba chen po zhal 'dzum pa dang bcas pas rgyas pa spyan ud pa la kha phya ba bzhin smin
197a3: ma dang su rnam par 'gyur ba/ / klog dang chu rlabs bzhin du// 'gyur ba'i rnam par gnon pas nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs rdo kho na nyid 'di gsungs so// dkyil 'khor dkyil 'khor zhes
197a4: bya ba/ / rdo rje ye shes thugs la gnas// dkyil 'khor rdo rje'i mchog nyid ni// bdag nyid sbyor bas brtags pa yin// rdo rje dgyes pa chen po yi// dkyil 'khor zla ba gang ba 'dra// 'od zer dkar po
197a5: phreng bas mdzes/ / byang chub sems mchog 'dra ba yin// rdo rje dpa' bo'i dkyil 'khor ni// mdzes pa zla ba kham pa yi// mthing ka'i bar ba kun rgyas pa// me dang rlung gis bus pa bzhin// shin tu dgyes
197a6: pa'i mchog sgrub pa/ / rdo rje rin chen dkyil 'khor ni// dga' byed dkyil 'khor cha brgyad kyi// 'bar dang bcas pa'i nyi ma bzhin// dkyil 'khor dgyes mchog 'byung byed pa// da pA mo'i dbang po pad mo
197a7: 'dra/ / 'dab ma brgyad po gyes pa yi// ge sar zla bas mdzes byas pa'o// thams cad las ni grub byed pa// rdo rje'i las kyi dkyil 'khor ni// dga' byed dkyil 'khor gru gsum te// rab tu 'bar ba medang
197a8: 'dra/ / de las sogs pa mtha' yas pa'i// dkyil 'khor rnams ni brtag par bya// spyod pa rdo rje sems dpa' yis// ji ltar de nyid sprul pa yin// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa

197b1: thams cad yang bzhengs nas brjid pa'i rdo rje gA dag gis gar mdzad cing bladang sil snyan gyis gling zla dang be ba dang / rnga rnga dang / rdu duH dang / ba nas dang / bral ka dang / zhi ba'i thal ba la sogs pa dang /
197b2: rnam pa sna tshogs kyis kun tu brdung ba dang / sil snyan la sogs pa'i rnam pa rol pas lha'i ro dang / ro'i zas dang / bza' ba dang / btsa'i ba dang / btung ba dang / theg pa dang / stan dang / gos dang / ldag pa dang /
197b3: bzhib pa dang / 'jams la sogs pa rnam pa sna tshogs kyis bcom ldan 'das bde ba chen po dpal rdo rje 'dzin la bstabs nas gus pa dang bcas pas pad mo'i sor mo khong stong du mdzad de g.yon
197b4: tu btung ba'i tshul gyis 'dzum pa dang bcas pa'i spyan gdangs te/ / yang de kho na nyid bskul bar mdzad pa'i dbyangs 'dis bstod pa mdzad do// shin tu bde ba'i byams pa kun tu gzigs pa'i thugs rje
197b5: spyan mnga' bas/ / byang chub chen po snying por 'gro ba stsol bas sgro yid mi mnga' ste// 'thun pa'i lam ston nyon mongs drug las bskal ba'i phyir// nam mkha'i tshul dugazungs kyi rang bzhin pade gshegs
197b6: kun la stobs/ / e ma'o bde ba kun tu rgyas pas che ba'i ye shes 'dren cing bsnams// sa yi khyad par bde bas rdzogs pa'i sku nyid stong pas tshogs pa'i rgyal po bzhin// chos nyid ji bzhin de la pa/
197b7: bas su nyid che ba kun ston cing // snying po byang chub bsgod phyir 'gro ba thams cad sgom bsam gyis mi khyab bstan// dpal gyi snying po gzungs su bstan te rigs lnga'i gtso rnams mnyes mdzad cing //
197b8: dgyes pas dngos la mnapas shing rab tu dgyes pas rol mo mdzod// de bzhin gshegs pa'i bde ba mnos te bying ba'i gnas nas bslang ba'i phyir// gnod sbyin cha lugs kye 'gog med pa'i tshul

198a1: dang rnam par ldan/ / snying rje chen brgyun dang bcas nas bde ba can pa ston pa'i chos nyid nam mkha' bzhin// dgyes pa mchog gi dang la sprul pa'i lha mo dpa// rol pas 'dus pa/
198a2: tshetshogs la bde mchog stsol bar mdzod// gta to bde la gnas shing bde bsgoms hUM// dgyes pa mchog dang ldan pa'i mi skye bde mchog bde la char pa rab tu dbab du stsol// rnam pa kun tu mtha' dang
198a3: bral ba'i dbyibs la bde gshegs slob ma gzung du gsol/ dpa kye rgyal po tshul bzhin de ltar bzhugs pa'i gnas su bsnams su gsol// ngo mtshar byang chub che ba 'di nyid 'gro ba rten bzhin bde thob
198a4: papha rol phyin drug dngos nyid gang la'ang mi brten par mi skye mya ngan 'das pa'i gzungs dang rtag tu rnam par ldan/ / mtha' dang bral ba'i bde bas chos kyi dbyings la gnas pa yi// rmongs pa'i bde
198a5: bas bying zhing gnas pa'i 'gro la snying rje'i chus khrus mdzod do/ / de nas shin tu dgyes mchog mi chags pa// 'di ni glu ru blangs pa yis// yid dang 'thun pa'i bde chen po// dngos grub myur du thob par
198a6: 'gyur/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das kun tu bzang po bde ba chen po dpal rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po la gsol ba'i dbyangs kyis bstod pa nye bar gnas nas yang chu
198a7: skyes kyi 'das ma 'dri ma med pa dang 'dra ba'i spyan gyis kun tu gzigs shing 'dzum pa dang bcas pas zhal rgyas par gyur nas/ yang tshad med pa mtha' yas pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing rdul phra rab kyi tshogs
198a8: kyi 'jig rten gyi khams mang po bskal pa rgyas pa'i sprin gyi rgya mtsho ma lus lus pa med pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa dang / rdo rje dang / nor bu rin po che dang / pad mo dang / las kyi rigs thams cad las byung ba'i de bzhin/

198b1: gshegs pa dang / rdo rje 'dzin dang / rin chen 'dzin dang / chos 'dzin dang / sna tshogs rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po thams cad dang / rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug gi tshogs chen po dang / thugs las byung ba dang / mtshan dang dga'
198b2: dang / sgeg mo la sogs pa'i rnal 'byor ma'i dbang phyug chen mo'i g.yog gi tshogs tshad med pa 'dren par byed pa dang / 'gugs par byed pa dang / 'jib par byed pa la sogs pa'i rdo rje nam mkha' la 'gro ba dang / nam
198b3: mkha' la 'gro ba chen mo'i tshogs dang / / grangs med pa'i rdo rje 'phrogs par byed pa'i tshogs dang / gzhan yang phyi rol gyi rdo rje dang / rin po che dang / pad mo dang / las kyi rigs la byung ba'i rnal 'byor dang / rnal
198b4: 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po dang / nam mkha' la 'gro ba'i tshogs rnams la rnam par bde ba chen po gyur pa dang bcas pa'i kun tu gzigs pa'i spyan gyis gar mdzad pa dang / rnam par 'gyur ba dang bcas pa'i
198b5: rnam par gnon pas kun tu gnon pas rnam par 'gyur ba dang bcas pas 'dag cing tshems kyis 'debs pa dang / rnam par 'gyur ba dang bcas pa'i kun tu 'brel pa'i phyag gis gar mdzad pa dang / rnam
198b6: par 'gyur ba dang bcas pa'i sgeg pas 'gying ba dang / spyod pa dang mi spyod par bcas pa'i rnams dang / kun tu 'dor ba'i rnam par gnon pas 'khor gyi tshogs kyi dkyil 'khor chen po la byin gyis brlabs nas
198b7: dgyes pa chen po rdo rje gdon mi za ba zhes bya ba dkyil 'khor gyi rgyal po chen po nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las gsungs pa/ / bdag nyid de nyid mnyam bzhag dang // de bzhin lha yi de nyid dang // sngag
198b8: dang phyag rgya de nyid ni/ / de yis dkyil 'khor mchog tu 'gyur// yan lag thams cad bsgom las 'das// rtog dang mi rtog rnam spangs pa// 'dren dang tshig la yang dga'adas// 'di ni dkyil 'khor mchog

199a1: ces bya/ / chos dang chos min rnam spyod pa// chos rnams thams cad brtag par bya// rnam dag nam mkha' 'dra ba yi// dkyil 'khor 'di ni bstan pa yin// 'dod chags mi chags 'dod chags mnyam
199a2: chu yi pad mo dmar po 'dra/ / rang sems bsod nams shin tu chags// 'di ni dkyil 'khor mchog yin no// gzugs dang gzugs min dri med pa'i// gang khams kun la 'jug 'gyur ba// sems ni chu dang skul
199a3: byed pa/ / dkyil 'khor dkyil 'khor zhes bya'o// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po g.yog dang bcas pa dang // pho nya dang / pho nya mo dang / nam mkha' la 'gro ba chen po dang / nam mkha'
199a4: la 'gro ba chen mo'i tshogs kyi dkyil 'khor de dag thams cad yang bcom ldan 'das da gra bang po rdo rje 'dzin gtso bo chen po la phyag 'tshal nas 'di skad ces gsol to/ / kye ma'o rab gyes sems
199a5: dpa' mchog/ kye ma'o rab dgyes phyogs sbyar pa// rnal 'byor ma yi tshogs mchog gi/ dkyil 'khor gsang ba nyid kyis gsungs// sangs rgyas sbyor ba sbyor che ba// rdo rje sbyor ba bla na med// 'jigs
199a6: gsum bde mchog thob 'gyur 'i/ / gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor nyid kyis gsungs// rin chen pad mo sna tshogs che// sna tshogs sbyor ba gang mdzad pa// rnam grangs thig le'i 'jig rten du// rnam dag
199a7: dkyil 'khor nyid kyis gsungs/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das rnal 'byor ma thams cad gar dang bcas pa'i phyag pad mo'i sor mo'i 'dab ma kun tu 'brel ba'i rdo rje'i thal mo dang / gar rnam par 'gyur ba'i
199a8: brjid bag tu bcas pas mtha' 'grol zhing ma mchu tshems kyis mnan nas chu skyes sar pa'i 'dab ma bzhin gzigs par bzhad pa/ / gru'i phyag rgyas dbyangs len pa dang / gcig la gcig bskul ba dang /

199b1: bdag nyid kyi dpung pa la 'dogs shing g.yas dang g.yon pa'i rnam par gnon pa'i tshul gyis/ oM hU~M a la las to// kun tu snang zhing mi chags par// mi chags pa yi bde mchog gis// bde pa'i rnal 'byor
199b2: gzungs kyi rnams/ / stobs shing bde ba sbyin mdzad pas// a lal 'a to// bsam gyis mi khyab nam mkha'i rang bzhin te// bzhengs shing gzhan la stobs la grub par mdzod// chags pas mi gos dngos po yi//
199b3: bde ba kun la reg par mdzad cing dgongs su gsol// de nas kun tu bzang po shin tu dgyes pa chen po rdo rje'i bdag po de kho na nyid kyi dbyangs chen pos bskul bas thugs sad par gyur te/ shin tu dgyes pa
199b4: chen po kun tu longs spyod pa rdo rje dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i rdo rje gdon mi za ba'i rnal 'byor ma'i tshogs kyi dkyil 'khor chen po 'dir sna tshogs
199b5: shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i rnam par gnon par gar mdzad/ shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i rdo rje'i dbyangs kyis mgur len/ rdo rje rnam par rol pa chen pos rnam par rol// shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i rdo rje
199b6: bzhad pa chen pos bzhad cing nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i zla ba'i thig le'i dkyil nas/ oM ma hA su ka hU~M zhes brjod nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag mo ye shes dbyings phyug
199b7: mabyung ngo / / steng du zla gam ldan pa yi// gnyis pa yi ge ma lta bu// mtshan du thig le ldan byas pa// ye shes gsal ba'i rnal 'byor ma'o// A li kA li 'dren bya ba// dbus su ri mo brtags byas te// de yi
199b8: mgo dang mjug dag tu/ / khro bo gnyis po mchog bsam bya// 'di ni btsun mo'i rab gsal ba// dkyil 'khor rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'o// 'di ni dran pa tsam gyis kyang // bsod nams kun gyis byin rlob 'gyur/

200a1: A li gnyis dbus ri mo bri// ldan pa 'dren pa yang dag ldan// de steng zla ga ma thig le dga'// mgo madrug gnyis su gzhan yang tsaM// 'di ni don dam gsal ba ste// rin chen rnal 'byor ma dpa
200a2: sbyin/ / dran pas bsod nams thob 'gyur te// sdig pa rnams kyang 'jig par byed// A li gnyis dang ldan byas te// tsheg drag yi ge gnyis su bshad// 'di ni rab dga' kun tu chags// chu srin ma zhes
200a3: bstan pa yin/ / dang po skal pa chen po yi// tsheg drag po dang bcas pa gzhan// sangs rgyas kun gyi A li 'di// sangs rgyas byang chub rab sbyin byed// bdag nyid la'am yang na gzhan// phyag rgya 'di yis
200a4: rgyas btab ste/ / bslab bya'i dkyil 'khor grub byed na// dngos grub myur du thob par 'gyur// 'di ni dkyil 'khor rnams kyi mchog/ yo ge'i phyag rgya'i mngon gnas pa'i// 'dzin pa'i bsod nams ci 'dra gab
200a5: bris pa yis kyang khyad par 'gyur/ / e ma'o bde ba ye shes che// de yi ye shes tshe 'di la// 'dod byed bde ba sten byed cing // 'di yi tshul gyis thob par 'gyur// khams gsum mchog gi dkyil 'khor 'dir//
200a6: 'di las rgya che mchog gzhan med// sgrub pa po yi sems can kun// tshe 'di nyid la sangs rgyas 'grub// zla gas thig le'i gsang ba'i rgyal po chen po shin tu dgyes pordo rje gdon mi za ba'i dam tshig
200a7: dkyil 'khor chen po rgyas pa mchog tu gsang ba las/ / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje btsun mo rnams kyi gsang ba chen po rnal 'byor ma'i dbang phyug chen po rnams kyi mchog tu gsang ba'i ye shes
200a8: kyidakyil 'khor te dang po rdzogs so/ / // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ngo mtshar du gyur te/ dgyes pa'i yid bde ba dang / mgu ba dang yid dga' ba bskyed nas gar dang shin tu dgyes pa

200b1: chen po'i rdo rje bzhad pa mdzod cing yang shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i bde ba gnyis su med pa'i ye shes rdo rje zhes bya ba 'du ba mdzad nas / bcom ldan 'das la gsol ba 'debs par gyur to// ba byed chen po
200b2: bshad pa shod/ / bde ba chen po bshad pa shod// gsang ba chen po bshad pa shod// dgyes pa chen po bshad pa shod// khyod las 'dod chags yang dag 'thung // khyod las zhe sdang chen po ste// khyod la theg byed
200b3: sdug bsngal dang / / khyod las khams gsum thams cad 'byung // khyod las skyes pa ma ning dang // khyod las 'dod gzir bud med dang // khyod las 'dod las rnam grol dang // khyod las byang chub bla med 'byung //
200b4: khyod las nam mkha' rlung dag dang // khyod las gzi brjid me yi khams// khyod las de bzhin chu dang sa// khyod las spyod dang mi spyod kun// khyod las sangs rgyas dpa' chen po// yang nas yang du 'byung bar 'gyur//
200b5: khyod las chos dang dge 'dun dang // khyod las pha rol phyin pa'i tshogs// byang chub sems dpa' chen po dang / raM dang skye bo thams cad 'byung // khyod las rdo rje sems dpa' dang // khyod las dri med pad mo
200b6: dang / / khyod las rin chen tshad med che// de bzhin rdo rje sna tshogs 'byung // khyod las phyag rgya sngags kyi rnams// khyod las rig pa snying pa 'byung // de nas bcom ldan 'das spyan mi 'dzums pas smin ma
200b7: brkyang ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa' pha rol tu phyin pa las sogs pa chen po dang / rnal 'byor ma chen mo'i tshigs dang / rdo rje nam mkha' la 'gro ba dang / nam
200b8: mkha' la 'gro ba'i tshegs dang / 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa dang / gzhan yang lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye

201a1: chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa kun 'dus pa thams cad la skad cig skad cig tu kun tu gzigs nas brjid pa dang bcas pa'i phyag 'jam pos/ nyid kyi snying ka'i rdo rje gsor zhig nyid
201a2: kyi mtshan ma'i phyag rdo rje rjes su chags pa rab tu rgyas pa chen po'i lta bas 'khor thams cad zil gyis mnan te/ nyid kyis thugs pad mo phra ba'i dkyil 'khor yi ge'i thig le'i dkyi lanas 'od ze yung
201a3: ste/ kun tu snang bar byin gyis brlabs nas/ shin tu dgyes pa gdon mi za ba'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // dang po'i yi ge
201a4: bcu gsum pa/ / thig ler bcas pa bsam byas te// bde chen tshul bzhin gzhag byas la// gzhan gyis mi phyed thig ler bcas// yi ge drug pa 'dren pa ru// tshul bzhin 'og tu yongs su
201a5: brtag/ 'di ni gsang ba chen po ste// rmad byung yi ge'i phyag rgya'o// bde chen bde bar bskyed pa'i phyir// sangs rgyas kun gyis bsgrags pa yin// ye shes kyi ni phyag rgya 'dis// skad cig snying
201a6: pos rgyas btab na/ / dkyil 'khor rnams kyi 'chad ba po// ston pa rdo rje 'dzin par 'gyur// bde ba chen po skul byed pa'i// sangs rgyas rnams kyi rtogs par byed// yi ge ye shes grub pa yis// ye shes
201a7: dbang phyug nyid du 'gyur/ / 'phrul gyi mig dang shes rab tshe// mi shes sdig pa 'joms par byed// rdo rje sems dpa' nyid 'dra bar// tshe 'di nyid la 'thob par 'gyur// bde ba chen po reg pa che// sdug
201a8: bsngal 'dod pa 'joms byed pa'o/ / shes rab ye shes dngos grub che// byang chub myur du 'thob 'gyur te// rig ma 'bum phrag brgyas skor cing // sems dpa' chen po de dang rtsen// rdo rje pad mo mnyam

201b1: sbyor bas/ / thal mo brkyang se rol ba yis// tshe dang lang tshe skal dang ldan// dran pa tsam gyis 'thob par 'gyur// 'dod pa yis ni dgos pa'i rnams// byung ba nyid du 'grub par 'gyur// 'og dang seng gi
201b2: nam mkha' la/ / bdag 'dod bzhin du 'gro 'od byed// sa yang rnam par phug nas su// stobs chen de 'dir 'ong bar byed// sangs rgyas kun la gnod byed do// byang chub par ni gdon mi za// bde ba chen po'i
201b3: rnam mdzad pas/ / gzhom zhing de bzhin myang ba yi// rdo rje blo yis bdud kyis rnams// rnam par 'gyur bas thams cad bsgral// bde ba chen po gtong ba yis// skad cig nyid du gsol bar bya// grub pa'i
201b4: rdo rje 'dzin pa che/ / dpa' bo chen pos dgug par bya// rnal 'byor ma rnams ci 'dod par// rnam gnon tshul gyis gnon par bya// dbang po nye dbang dbang chen po// gnod byed stobs kyis dgon gnas
201b5: par/ / rab tu rnam 'joms gnon pa yis// gzhom pa'i tshul gyis bsgral bar bya// mtshon cha lnga yis rnam gnon pas// gzhan gyi bud med rtsen par bya// kye ma'o bde ba bde gnas pa'i// sems can
201b6: chen po grol byas te/ / byang chub sems ni bde 'byung bas// sems dpa' bdag nyid mchod par bya// dam tshig rjes su ldan pa yis// rnal 'byor rtag pa'i ngo bor 'gyur// skad cig mtho ris 'gro bar
201b7: bye/ da nga 'grob byed/ rje'i chugs kyis thams cad// sems can skad cig 'di ru'o// sangs rgyas kun gyis gnas su 'gyur// sems can rnams dang grags chen po// thams cad kyi ni rigs rnams dang // pha rol
201b8: byin rnams skye gnas te/ / de bzhin rigs dang pha rol phyin// de dag 'di la rab tu gnas// dbang por gyur pa brtan chen po// yon tan tshogs ni nam mkha' bzhin// de nyid dngos po thams cad la// thams

202a1: cad dus gsum mnyam gnas te/ / rdo rje sems dpa' mchog tu bde// sems dpa' thog ma tha med yin// bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i shin tu bde ba chen po'i rdo rje chos kyi yi ge
202a2: zhes bya ba yi ge chen po'i phyag rgya'i ye shes so/ / // bcu gsum gyi ni yi ge che// ye shes thig le ldan pa ste// rdo rje yid 'byung lhags pa yi// ha langs btags dbu bskor bya// 'di ni yid las skyes pa ste
202a3: shin tu dgyes che mdzes pa yis/ / yi ge'i phyag rgya phyag rgya che// gtso bo'i spyan sngar gnas pa yi// gsang ba'i snying gi pad mo la// phyag rgya 'di yis rgyas btab pas// de ni de ma thag nyid du// shin tu dgyes pa'i
202a4: mnyes par 'gyur/ / gtso chen rdo rje sems dpa' la// de yi bde bas mnyes byas te// dbang po yi ni sbyor ba yis// de dang rol pas myur du 'grub// de gnyis phan tshun dgyes pa las// shin tu dgyes pa'i gzhir
202a5: gyur te/ / rig 'dzin mchog gi gzugs ldan dang // lha min kun gyis mchod par 'gyur// de dang lhan cig rol pa na// lha chen tshangs pa gtogs 'dod nams// phyag rgya sbyor ba'i tshul gnas pa'i//
202a6: bdag nyid che la phyag byed pa'o// nyes gsum dri ma spangs pa yi// shin tu sbyor ba'i rgyas btab pa// sems can gar ni byed pa dang // sems dpa' chel mnyes par byed// de ni sa dang nam mkha' la// bde bar
202a7: gnas shing 'gro bar byed/ / sna tshogs lha mo bde che ba'i// sna tshogs bde bas nyer spyod do// phyag rgya ga kyis pa dpang/ sems can myur du rtogs par byed// ral grir gyur pa gzi chen po// nam mkha' kun tu
202a8: phan tshun 'gro/ / lha mo 'phrul gyi 'gro ba dang // lha min klu yi bu mo dang // gzhan yang 'phrul ldan mi bu mo// de yis bud med kun bsrub bya// phyag rgya'i ye shes rab gnas pas// de nyid kun tu 'gro byed de//

202b1: 'dod par dkyil 'khor du// rdo rje sems dpa' che gnas so// sangs rgyas thams cad myur du 'grub// thams cad chos ni bde chen po// dge 'dun chags med thams cad rnams// de dag thams cad yin no//
