208a1: spyod chen rol pa dang / / res 'ga' bdud las rgyal bar mdzad// res 'ga' byang chub mngon byang chub// res 'ga' 'khor lo bskor mdzad de// res 'ga' sna tshogs 'jug par mdzad// res 'ga'
208a2: don du shin tu mdzes/ res 'ga' bud med skyes pa dang // res 'ga' lha dang skye dgu'i bdag/ res 'ga' 'dod dbang rgyal po ste// res 'ga' 'dod la rgyab kyi phyogs// res 'ga' zhi la res 'ga' drag/ res 'ga'
208a3: gdon chen bgegs mdzad de/ / de la sogs pa mtha' yas pa// phyag rgya bde yis rgyas btab pa// ci dgar dngos grub 'dod pa la// bdag gis ngo bor ston par byed// mi phyed cho ga sbyor ba yis// 'dren
208a4: pa mi phyed nye byas te/ / phan tshun rig pa chen po yis// rdo rje can gyis de 'bigs te// gzungs ma mang po tshogs kyi rnams// bde byed chen po gzhan ci smos// spyod bcas mi spyod bde dam pa// 'bad
208a5: pa mi dgos 'thob par 'gyur/ / brjid pas byang chub snying po ru// rtag pa ru ni gnas 'gyur te// phyag rgya 'di yis rnal 'byor pa// sbyor ba rjes sdud ldan pas so// thams cad cha ni rnam bral ba// byang chub
208a6: sems ni mchog bzhin du/ / yi ge 'dis ni sbyor ba yis// bdag nyid chen por de 'gyur ro// rdo rje shin tu dgyes pa chen po tshim pa'i yid las skyes bdedab med pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i yi ge'i phyag rgya ste/
208a7: las thams cad grub par byed pa'o// // dang por oM ni sbyor ba ste// tha mar gnyis po rdo rje'i sgra// rab dgyes rdo rje byin rlabs pa'i// lha mo dngar byed dbus su gzhag/ 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi//
208a8: rab dgyes thob pa rmongs byed ma// rdo rje ye shes thugs gnas pa// dngos grub thams cad bsgrub par bya// sngags mkhan yi ge phyag rgya 'dis/ bdag gam gzhan la rgyas btab ste// rdo rje 'dam skyes

208b1: bcug byas na/ / de nas de myur dngos grub po// thams cad las byed dpal dang ldan// tshe dang lang tshe skul ldan pa'i// rdo rje 'dzin dang 'dra 'thob ste// rdo rje sems dpa' rab tu 'grub// sangs rgyas rnams dang dpa'
208b2: bo yi/ / sangs rgyas kun dang rtsen byed cing // sde dbang rnams dang lha rnams kyi// 'phrul gyi bud med 'phrog byed do// rdo rje rab tu dgyes pa chen mo dngar byed kun tu myang ba me tog gi rgyal mtshan dang ldan pa zhes
208b3: ga phyag rgya ste/ / sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel ba las thams cad byed pa chen mo gdon mi za ba'i gzhan gyis mi byed ma'o// / tshangs pa'i gsung gis nga ror bcas// thamar dril bu'i
208b4: nga ro gnyis/ / dbus su ming gi phreng ba ste// yi ge 'di ni chu 'dzin mchog/ 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// yid kyi dngos grub thob byed de// 'dod pa yi ni thams cad rnams// yi ge skad cig 'grub
208b5: par byed/ / 'di yis rgyas btab bud med rnams// bdag nyid rang gi slob ma'ang rung // de nyid sbyor bas bsten byas na// rdo rje 'dzin dpal 'dra bar 'gyur// rnal 'byor ma rnams bdag por ni// myur du mkha'
208b6: la 'gro byed de/ / tshangs pa gtogs 'dod dbang chen dang // lha rnams kyis ni mchod par 'gyur// lha mo'i tshogs dang rtsen byed cing // lha mo kun gyi bdag por 'gyur// 'phrog byed la sogs bdag po che//
208b7: 'jigs par byed dang sku byed pa// sems can kun gyi mchog dam pa// sems dpa' chen por de 'gyur ro// sdug pa'i tshogs kyi dbus su ni// brjid la sogs pas spyod pas 'gro// brjid che pad mo chen
208b8: mo la/ / thams cad kun tu brjid pa yis// bde byed chen po myong byed de// rab tu dgyes pas bsgeg pa bzhin// rab tu skal ldan mgrin mkhyud pas// rnal 'byor chen por de gnas te// 'di ni snying la

209a1: bris pa yis/ / ci 'dod par ni 'dod pa 'thob// phyag rgya chu skyes btab byas te// de ltar byas na phyag rgya dgyes// rdo rje shin tu dgyes pa chen mo'i dri ma med pa'i mdog dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i yi
209a2: ge'i phyag rgya ste/ / thams cad las byed pa dge ba'o// // dang po nyid du oM bya ste// thig le'i rgyal pos nye bar brgyan// tsheg drug bcas pa 'dren pa gnyis// ldan pa mtha' mar bzhag byas te//
209a3: rdo rje rab dgyes brgyan byas pa// rdo rje ston ka dbus su bsam// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// ye shes snang ba rab grub pa// yi ge yi ni phyag rgya 'dis// nyid kyi snying khar rgyas btab na// sangs
209a4: rgyas ye shes mchog byed pa/ / de yis ston ka ma dngos grub// sde dbang lhar bcas lha rnams dang // gnod sbyin srin por bcas pa dang // sbrul dang mi 'am ci gnas pa// thams cad 'di yi g.yog tu
209a5: 'gyur/ / 'di ni 'od zer rab tu 'bar ba yis// sangs rgyas mchog gi thugs ldan de 'gro ste// sna tshogs rab 'byung dpal gyis yang dag khyab// chos mchog dam pa byed pa gtong byed cing // spyod bcas mi
209a6: spyod 'jig rten snang byed de/ / sprin dang bral ba'i zla ba'i 'od mchog byed// mkha' dbyings rnam par bsgyings pas rab dga' bas// A li kA li pad mo bde mchog la// myong zhing mchog byas bskal par
209a7: gnas par 'gyur/ / 'di yis sdig pa 'phrog byed de// 'di yis myur du dga' bar 'gyur// 'dis ni bde ba'i ngo bo de// 'di yis dngos grub grub par 'gyur// skye ba'i sdug bsngal rgyab phyogs pa//
209a8: 'di nyid la 'thob par 'gyur// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje shin tu dgyes pa ye shes kyi snang ba dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya chen mo ste// thams cad mkhyen pa ye shes 'grub par byed pa'o// /

209b1: dang po oM dang yang dag ldan// tha mar dgyes pa'i yi ge gnyis// rdo rje shin tu dgyes pa che// dbus su gsal ba'i yi ge bsam// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// sna tshogs chen mo'i mdun du 'gro// sna tshogs
209b2: chen mo 'di yis ni/ / sna tshogs ye shes dngos grub bo// sngags mkhan nyid kyis byin brlabs pa// sna tshogs bdag po chen por 'gyur// sdig pa'i yan lag kun spangs te// bsod nams kun gyi yan lag dge/
209b3: kun tu 'gro ba'i dngos grub ni// 'di nyid kyis ni rab tu 'grub// sna tshogs sgyu ma'i bde chen gyis// sna tshogs chen po'i bskal par gnas// rdo rje'i bdag nyid brgyan pa yi// bud med kun dang rtsen par 'gyur// de nas des
209b4: chos dbyings gnas/ / dbang phyug mchog gi dngos grub bo// pad mo'i mdun du thog ma'i lha// byas te rdo rje bsrub par bya// mthe bong srin lag de byung ste// ba yi nang du gzhag par bya// chang bzhin myang bar byas nas ni//
209b5: mod la 'dod pa'i gzugs su 'gyur// A li kA li rab sbyor bas// bud med rnams dang rtsen par byed// blo ldan rdo rje sems dpa' yi// 'di ni shin tu dgyes zhes bya// bsil ba dga' byed chen mo ste// sna tshogs 'di ni
209b6: 'gro la gnas/ / dang po oM ni gnas pa ste// trata dang ldan tha mar bya// rdo rje shin tu dgyes che ho// sgeg mo dbus su bskul ba'o// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// bsgrags par bya ba sprul pa yin// 'di dag mnyam par
209b7: sbyor ba yis/ / sgeg mos ye shes bskyed par bya// rdo rje bro ldan brtan po yis// bde bar 'dod pa'i pad mor gzugs// 'dod pas 'dod pa spyad par bya// myur du 'dod pas dngos grub bo// de nas rdo rje 'dod dpal te//
209b8: bde byed thams cad nye bar sgrub// sems can kun gyis 'dod skyed pa// bde ba chen por de 'gyur ro// mthu yis pha rol phyin pa'i mchog/ pad mo'i tshul du bsgrags pa yis// rdo rje sbyor thabs la gnas pas// rdo rje

210a1: chen po de dngos grub/ / ci dgar 'dod pa'i 'dod chags kyis// rtag pa'i lam dang yang dag ldan// rtag pa'i chos kyis rjes 'thun spyod// bsgrubs na rtag pa rtogs par 'gyur// 'di yis kun tu bzang
210a2: zhes bya/ / de ni dngos po kun yin te// 'dod pa med cing nyon mongs med// nga rgyal med cing 'dzin med pa// sangs rgyas mchog tu rtag pa yi// sangs rgyas chen po de yi dngos// dpal ldan thog ma tha ma med// chos
210a3: rnams kun gyi rjes 'thun pa'i/ / 'dis ni dngos po thams cad kyi// sangs rgyas bdag por bdag nyid 'gyur// sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad dang // 'di la khyad par cung zad med// shin tu dgyes pa chen po rdo rje bdag
210a4: po'i dpal shin tu dgyes pa sgeg mo dpe med pa dang ldan pa'i yi ge'i mchog gi sku'o/ / // dang po oM bcas lha mo yi// tha mar tsheg dreg mi phyed gnyis// de gnyis dbus kyi phyogs nyid du// he zhes bya ba rnam
210a5: brgyan te/ / shin tu dgyes pa'i rdo rje che// bzhad pa nyid ni rab tu sbyar// yi ge yi ni phyag rgya 'dis// nyid kyi snying la rgyas btab na// phreng ba'i rgyan gyis rnam brgyan par// dpal ldan de ma thag tu 'gyur// yid kyis
210a6: jiltar bsams pa bzhin/ / de ni sangs rgyas yul du 'gro// de ni do phyir sangs rgyas mthong // chu skyes de dang rtsen par byed// de nas 'dus pa dgyes 'gyur te// sangs rgyas yang dag zhing nyid nas// sangs rgyas rnams
210a7: kyis bde ba che/ / dngos grub rnal 'byor de la sbyin// byed pa dang ni zlog pa dang // bde ba chen po 'phrog pa yis// rnal 'byor gsang ba'i dbang phyug la// gsang ba chen pos mgu bar byed// thabs bcas shes rab
210a8: chen po la/ / rgyal ba nyid kyis stobs byed de// A li kA li mnyam sbyor bas// bde ba chen po mgu bar byed// bde ba thabs kyi dngos grub rnams// sgyu ma'i tshul gyis bsgrub par bya// yi ga yi ni phyag rgya 'di//

210b1: shin tu dngos grub mchog tu brtag/ rdo rje shin tu dgyes pa'i bde ba'i phreng ba rgyas pa dpe med pa dang ldan ma zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya ste/ las thams cad kyi don gyi dngos grub sbyin pa'o// // oM ni dang por
210b2: gtsug tor bya/ / te ta skad snyan tha mar te// dbus su he dga' zhes bya ba// bde chen dga' ba rdo rje dbyings// rdo rje shin tu dgyes che yi// phyag rgya 'di ni rab dgyes 'brel// bris pa dang ni 'dzin pa dang /
210b3: dran pa yis kyang dngos grub ster// sdig pa kun las grol byed cing // bsod nams thams cad nye bar 'gro// mi dag thams cad ma lus spong byed cing // sems ni phyag rgya'i yi ge brgyan te 'gro// 'jig
210b4: rten thams cad kun tu bkur sti byed/ / rig ma stong gis mngon par mchod byed cing // rig 'dzin mu sman bud med rnams kyis ni// g.yag rnga dkar po'i tshogs kyis g.yob byed pa'i// 'jig rten dbang po bde
210b5: mchog 'brel pa 'thob/ / blo ldan nam mkha' ngos ni thams cad du// rdo rje 'dzin gyi dgyes pa'i rnal 'byor ma// yid du 'ong ba'i spyan ni rgyas pa dang // rnal 'byor spyod pa'i bde bas 'bigs pa yis// mgul
210b6: nas 'khyud pa'i rtsen pas rol bar byed/ / pi bang gling bu ya mtshan sgra snyan gyis// glu blangs dngos grub rgya che thob par byed// ji snyed yid du 'ong ba'i glu dag ni// 'jig rten grags pa'i bde ba'i bde ba dag/
210b7: bde ba'i sgra yis bskyed par rnams bsgyur ba'i// de dang 'thun pa'i dbyangs 'dis sgrub par byed// Sha Ta pad gar dza'i dbyangs// glu ru blangs pas pad mo gnas// dngos grub myur du 'thob par byed// 'di
210b8: yis byin rlabs dge pa dang / / 'di yis byin rlabs bde ba'i rnams// sbyor ba 'di yis sbyar ba yis// 'dod byed thams cad 'thob par 'gyur// shin tu dgyes pa chen po rdo rje sems dpa'i mchog tu dgyes

211a1: pa chen mo'i dbyangs dpe med pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i yi ge'i phyag rgya'o/ / de bzhin oM ni dang por te// dbus su te dgyes bde ba che// rdo rje gar byed de pa gnyis// 'di ni thams cad bde byed de/
211a2: sangs rgyas rnams kyi rab dgyes nyid// rnal 'byor yi ni rgyas btab na// bde dang ldan par byed cing 'gro// 'og min gyi ni gnas chen du// sangs rgyas rnams dang thabs gcig 'grogs// bde byed chen po'i dbang
211a3: chen dang / / chos kyi rgyal po bde chen 'thob// ji snyed gar gyi gtsug lag las// sbyar bar byed pa bshad pa dang // ji snyed de snyed phyag rgya'i rnams// gnyis min 'dus pas 'dis dngos grub// kye ma'o dgyes pa
211a4: bde byed che/ / kye ma'o bde ba bde chen po// kye ma'o 'dod pa 'dod chags che// kye me'o sna tshogs bdag nyid che// de la sogs pa tshad med pa// 'jig rten gyi ni yo byad rnams// pad mo gsal ba gar gyis
211a5: rnal 'byor gar byas dngos grub po/ / sangs rgyas kun gyi phyag rgya 'di// sna tshogs gar ni ston byed pas// myur du gar ni mang byas pas// gar gyi gtsug lag dngos grub po// rdo rje shin tu dgyes pa
211a6: chen po'i dpal bde ba chen po dga' byed gar zhes bya ba'i yi ge phyag rgya phan tshun bcu brgyal mtshan dang ba dan gsum pa'o/ / bcu gsum yi ge dang po nyid// rdo rje shin tu dgyes pa che/
211a7: rdo rje'i sku ni sna tshogs // tha mar 'bar dang 'dra ba'i dza// nam mkhar zla skar 'dra ba yi// phyag rgya'i ye shes rmad 'byung ba'i// 'di yis thabs kyis maN+Dags // gzung ba gsal bar gzung ba yi// tsha ba'i
211a8: gser gyi gzi brjid 'dzin/ / ye shes snying khar bsam par bya// nam mkha' nyi ma bum 'dra bar// de ni de ma thag tu 'gyur// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad nyid// shin tu rmad 'thung thob par 'gyur//

211b1: rnal 'byor kun gyi bde 'brel ba// rdo rje blo mchog dngos grub bo// sangs rgyas rdo rje 'dzin dge yi// sna tshogs tshon po thob 'gyur nas// 'dod pa'i chos kyis mi gos blo// 'dod pa chen po sten par byed// de
211b2: bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po shin tu dgyes pa chen po dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i rdo rje ma lus pa lus pa med pa'i rdo rje'i sku dpe med pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i yi ge chen po'i phyag rgya'o/ /
211b3: de bzhin oM ni gzhag bya ste// rdo rje shin tu dgyes pa che// rdo rje'i sgra ni bde 'brel pa// tha mar khro bcas sbyar bar bya// phyag rgya 'di ni bde mchog ste// bar bcas pa yang thos par 'gyur// khams gsum
211b4: ngo bo thams cad ni/ / sgra yi thos pa dngos grub po// 'di yis sangs rgyas thams cad nyid// tshe 'di nyid la dngos grub ste// bud med pad mo ud pal dang // ma lus rgyal ba'i rnams dang rtsen// rdo rje par
211b5: mo'i sbyar bas na/ / dga' byed myur du dngos grub po// rab tu dgyes pa chen po dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i tshad med pa'i yon tan gyi sgra dpe med pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i don gyi dpal thams cad grub par byed
211b6: ma'o/ / oM ni spyi gtsug thig ler babs// rab dgyes chen mo rdo rje can// rdo rje dri bder 'bel ba yi// tha mar gnas sher rab sbyar bya// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// sna tshogs chen mo mdun du 'gro//
211b7: sna tshogs chen mo 'di yis ci// sna tshogs ye shes grub par 'gyur// bdag nyid rdo rje brdzun pa yi// de ni mtshan ldan kun dang chen// de nas chos dbyings gnas pa des// A li kA li mnyam sbyor bas//
211b8: dga' byed lhan cig rtsen byas na// dbang phyug dam pa dngos grub 'gyur// 'di ni rdo rje sems dpa' yi// blo ldan rab tu dgyes zhes bya// rdo rje'i dri dpe med pade// ldan ma zhes bya ba'i yi ge'i phyag rgya'o//

212a1: oM mchog gtsug tor rnams byas te// shin tu dgyes che dbus nyid du// rdo rje ro ni sbyor che ba// tha mar ha ste thig le gnyis// 'di yis rab tu dgyes par 'gyur// dpal ldan dpe med
212a2: bde ba dang / / bcom ldan rdo rje sems dpa' nyid// sna tshogs sbyor ba sna tshogs bdag/ sangs rgyas kun gyi rol pa yis// mchod pa mi zad byed par 'gyur// sangs rgyas rnams kyi gnas thams cad//
212a3: nam mkha' mnyam pa nyid thob bo// rab tu dgyes pa'i dbang po shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i ro mchog gi rgyal mtshan dang ldan pa zhes bya ba sems can thams cad kyi don thams cad grub pa'o// de bzhin
212a4: gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i bdag po zla gsang thig le bshad pa'i rgyal po las/ / chos kyi 'khor lo ste gnyis pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das shin tu dgyes pa
212a5: c hen po dpal rdo rje sems dpa' kun tu bzang po nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las shin tu dgyes pa chen po gdon mi za ba'i rgyal po zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po bshad nas cang mi gsung
212a6: bar gyur to/ / de nas nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad kyi rdul phran dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad gsang ba'i gzungs dang g.yog tu bcas pa rnams kyis yongs su bskor ba/
212a7: byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor chen po dang bcas pa rnams kyis mdun du byas pa ma lus pa lus pa med pa'i nam mkha' la 'gro ba dang // nam mkha' la 'gro ba'i tshogs dang ldan pa// phyi nang gi
212a8: pho nya dang pho nya mo rab tu rgyas pa rnams shin tu ngo mtshar rmad du gyur te/ / dgyes shing spyan ni rgyas pa yis// bzhengs nas dgyes pa chen po yi// brjid pa'i phyag gis gar mdzad cing // thal mo

212b1: sbyar nas gtsug nyid du/ / bzhag pa yis ni 'dun pa byed// bskul ba yis ni dbyangs 'di yis// de dag gtso la mnyes par byed// kye ma'o chos ni ngo mtshar che// kye ma'o spyod pa ngo mtshar che// kye ma'o
212b2: sbas pa ngo mtshar che/ / kye ma'o bde ba yang dag 'byung // kye ma'o kun du bzang po'i don// kye ma'o rab dgyes yang dag 'grogs// kye ma'o bde ba dag pa che// kye ma'o bde ba ba de mchog ste// kye ma'o sngags kyi
212b3: yang dag sbyor/ / kye ma'o snying po yang dag bsdus// kye ma'o phyag rgya mnyam par bzhugs// kye ma'o sgrub pa rmad 'thung ba'o// kye ma'o pha rol phyin ma yin// kye ma'o ji ltar mthu rig ma'i// kye ma'os
212b4: tshogs dgos pa che/ / kye ma'o dag pa gsum sbyar ba// kye ma'o rdo rje mnyam sbyor ba'i// kye ma'o pad ma rnam phye bas// kye ma'o dbang po gnyis sbyor ba'o// kye ma'o mchog dang mnyam pa'o// kye ma'o//
212b5: gar ni dag pa che// kye ma'o glu rab dri ma med// kye ma'o sil snyan rnam par 'brel// kye ma'o brda ba dang mun pa sel// kye ma'o dag byed me tog phreng // kye ma'o pog sdod dge ba ste// kye ma'o mar me
212b6: mun pa sel/ / kye ma'o dri ni shin tu bsil// kye ma'o rnal 'byor mnyam par sbyor// kye ma'o sgyur ba nam mkha' 'dra// kye ma'o sangs rgyas rdo rje mchog/ kye ma'o rin chen bde mchog skyed// kye ma'o sna tshog
212b7: pad mchog ldan/ / kye ma'o sna tshogs sbrum mdzad// kye ma'o ngo mtshar sangs rgyas dang // kye ma 'o ngo mtshar dpa' bo rnams// kye ma'o ngo mtshar sems dpa' rnams// kye ma'o ngo mtsharaHyi rnams// shin/
212b8: du dgyes che rdo rje la// rgyan pa kun gyis bstod byas te// rdo rje sems dpa'i 'gying ba yis// dga' dang bde byed skyes par 'gyur// de nas pha rol phyin thams cad// 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor dgyes 'gyur te//

213a1: sem sa dpa' che la phyag byas nas// mchog gi dbyangs kyis bstod par byed// chu skyes zhal ni 'dzum bcas pa// yangs pa'i spyan gyis gar mdzad de// phyag dang zhabs ni bsgyur ba yis// rab tu
213a2: dgyes ldan srin ma bsgyur/ / yid tsam 'dzum pa'i spyan zur gzigs// shas rgyas b.rIn nu mar mdud// rkeng ba'i dbyibs ni rnam par yangs// snam gyi ngos kyang che la mdzes// chags pa chung zad tshems kyis
213a3: dod 'ayas ci bra la nang kau pi ga zlo pa 'dagapa byin cing / ma'i bas tod paci rjes su gas pa'i bgani drug pathal ni bdad cing bdu byas te skyes par bstod/ des de nga 'ongs spyod pachog tudapa rang baninin papa brtsis ma bya bdan/ ngas pa'i
213a4: dbang dang ldan pas 'gro ba ya mtshan chen po'i sgo nas 'dul mdzad cing / / gsang ba'i thig le 'jig rten gsum po 'dir ni dngos grub gtser bstan te// 'jig rten gsum po sbyang bar bya ba'i chos de bde gshegs
213a5: don tu mdzad/ / ngo mtshar yon tan ldan pa dam tshig bde las 'byung // bde mdzod pade spyod dga' la rol pa yul bzhin mdzod// thams cad dga' ba'i rang nyid thig le'i dkyil du bskyed mdzad de// byang chub snying po
213a6: 'gro ba'i lam 'di bde bar skul la bsnyen pa mdzod/ / ngo mtshar de bzhin gshegs pa'i dam tshig rig pa che la dgyes shing bzhugs// bdag cag 'du shes rnams dang bral ba nyid kyang bzhugs spyod 'dzem bcas
213a7: bas/ / tshangs pa'i rgyal po dbang dang ldan pas kyang ni de la rag lus so// a la la la'o// yangs pa'i spyan can drangs shing bcug ste rol pa tshul bzhin mdzod// rnam dag ye shes chu nges 'gro ba rnams kyi sdig pa khrus/
213a8: byams ma'i gzungs ma bdag nyid che dang rab tu rtsen mdzod la// thugs rje chen po'i rang bzhin dag pa'i chu des bdag cag dbang skur cig/ mi g.yo mnyam pa nyid kyi rang bzhin ye shes thob 'dod phyir/

213b1: dam cig chen po gsum po 'di la gnas nas na// zla gsung thig la'i dbyings su bdag cag dgas mad 'gro bar bsti// dbyungs kyi rgyal ba 'di yis ni// shin tu srid pas sgru ba yi// sangs rgyas kun kyang 'du
213b2: pa bzhin/ / glu blangs myur du bskul bar 'gyur// de nas bcom ldan 'das la dbyangs kyi rgyal po 'dis bstod pas shin tu dgyes te de bzhin gshegs pa dang byang chub sems dpar bcas pa dang / rdo rje dang rin po
213b3: che dang pad ma dang las kyi rigs kyi btsun mo de dag thams cad la rdo rje shin tu dgyes pa'i bde ba chen pos mnyes par mdzad de/ / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po'i tshogs/
213b4: rnams dang / byang chub sems dpar bcas pa dang / nam mkha' la 'gro ba dang / nam mkha' la 'gro ma'i tshigs su bcas pa rnams dang / phyi nang gi rdo rje rigs las skyes pa'i rnams la shin tu dgyes pa dgyes
213b5: pa chen po'i gar dang dbyangs dang / brdung ba dang zhi ba'i thal mo la sogs pa rnam par mdzad pa chen pos rab tu mdzad nas/ dam tshig chen po rdo rje shin tu dgyes pa 'dod pa'i dbang mo dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge
213b6: 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas bde bar cang mi gsung bar gyur to/ / de nas de dag kun dgyes nas// shin tu dgyes pa nyid byas te// thal mo sbyar nas sa steng du// pus mo'i lha nga btsugs mdzad de/
213b7: chos kyi phyir ni gsol ba 'debs// dkyil 'khor dam tshig bdag nyid la// bcom ldan dgyes pas bshad du gsol// gang gi sems can pa de nyid kyi// bde bas dkyil 'khor bsgrub par bgyid// de nas
213b8: bcom ldan 'das dam tshig 'dod pa nye bar longs spyod pa'i dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ dkyil 'khor mdzad do// phyag gnyis gar dang bcas pa yis// mdun du thal mo

214a1: bkun par bya/ / sor mo kun gyi rtse mo la// pha rol phyin pa'i tshigs rnams pasam// de dag ming gi brda yis ni// ser mo thams cad brtag par bya// snyam pa phan rgan bskul byas te// shes rab
214a2: mchod rten du ni brtag/ / rdo rje mchod rten skyer byas te// lhag ma 'odi bzhin spo bar bya// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// shes rab pa rol byin ma dge// gang gis bcings pa tsam gyis kyang // sangs rgyas kyang
214a3: chub byin rlob bo/ / phyag rgya 'di yis rgyas btab pas// drug pa'i pho brang 'gro 'o byed/ sa sarbAs spang mdzad dpal dang ldan// bco ma'i gser gyi kha dog 'dzin// shes rab ldan pas sbyor byas na// 'di yis
214a4: myur du dngos grub po/ / skal ldan 'phrul gyi bu mo la// 'di yis byin rlabs gar byas te// rdo rje ngagasor gzhug byas nas// sems ni gzhug pas bsgrub byas la// de nas sems de blang byas te// blo ldan de
214a5: yis btud byas te/ / grub pa gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor du// yang dag dngos grub 'gro bar byed// shes rab dang ni 'phrul gyi 'am// de bzhin gshegs pa 'phral rtag 'thob// sangs rgyas rdo rje blo ldan
214a6: gyis/ / kun tu 'phrog par yod mi nus// shin tu dgyes pa kun du longs spyod pa'i bde ba zhes bya ba shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma'o// thal mo de nyid khro skyes pa// sbom po dkyil krung gzhag byas te// sna
214a7: tshogs phreng ba 'bar byed pa/ / rnal 'byor gyis ni lhag ma spro// 'di ni rdo rje thams cad kyi// shes rab pha rol phyin ma gsal// phyag rgya 'di yis rgyas btab pas// rdo rje ye shes bla na med// 'di yis myur
214a8: tu 'thob par 'gyur/ / phyag rgya 'di yis rgyas btab pas// 'di ni bcings pa tsam gyis kyang // ring du sdig pa 'jig par byed// tshe dang dpal dang ye shes skal// rdo rje 'dzin gyis thob par 'gyur// 'di ni

214b1: dbang bskur tsam gyis kyang / / rdo rje 'dzin rdzar de 'gyur te// rdo rje dkyil gyis mtshan btab pas// sa chen 'ong zhing 'gro bar byed// 'di ni dga' byed rdo rje rigs// rdo rje bud med 'grogs pa dang // rdo rje gzungs kyi
214b2: dkyil 'khor du/ / rdo rje sems nyid 'thob par 'gyur// ji ltar dngos grub 'dug pa dang // sangs rgyas rdo rje dpa' bo rnams// skad cig gcig gis 'dren par byed// bsgral dang mnyes par bya ba dang // rgyas
214b3: btab de bzhin rmongs pa dang / / gso bar byed dang za ba dang // phan tshun du ni skyed par byed// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje chen po'i dbang skur ba rdo rje'i phreng ba zhes bya ba shin tu dgyes pa bde ba thob
214b4: par byed pa dpe med pa'i rdo rjer byed pa'i phyag rgya'o/ / rdo rje'i thal mo de nyid las// khro mo rgyab ni bskum byas te// sor mo lhag ma snga ma bzhin// phyag rgya 'di ni dbang bskur ba'o// rims dang gdon dang dug la sogs
214b5: de ma thag du 'phrog par byed/ / 'di ni bcings pa tsam gyis kyang // sangs rgyas kyi ni dgyes pa 'thob// 'di nyid kyis ni dbang bskur dang // 'di nyid kyis ni bde dam pa// 'di nyid kyis ni rgyal po che// 'di nyid kyis ni
214b6: dpal dam pa/ / 'di yis rtsen pa byas pa yis// rab dga' 'gug pa dngos grub po// mi la 'di yis byin rlabs te// nyi ma phyed na spyad byas na// 'di ni de ma thag tu yang // dpal ldan rdo rje gzi brjid 'dzin// nyi ma bcu
214b7: gnyis 'od 'dra 'gyur/ / zhag bdun gyis 'gyur gzhan gyis min// sangs rgyas kun gyis 'dul ba dang // dge ba thams cad dbang du byed// grol 'dod rnams kyi mun pa sal// blo ldan phyag rgya mchog tu 'gyur// /
214b8: de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi// bde ba chen po gzi brjid dpe med pa dang ldan pa'i phreng ba zhes bya ba ba dan gsum pa'i 'jig rten gsum du bde ba chen po 'thob par byed pa'i dam tshig gi phyag rgya chen po'o// /

215a1: pha rol phyin pa'i phyag rgya nyid// dge ba'i khro mo dang bral ba// pha rol phyin pa'i chos yin te// tshig dang tshig du rnam bral ba'o// phyag rgya 'di ni bcings pa yis// chos kyi dbyings nas rje ru 'gyur// sangs/
215a2: rgyas kun gyis dbang bskur bas// dbang phyug dam par de 'gyur te// thams cad dag pa mos pa yis// pad mo dmar po mchog 'dzini 'gyur// pad ma sgyu ma rnam mdzad pas// sna tshogs chen por de 'gyur ro// sdug
215a3: bsngal thams cad 'phrog par byed/ / sems can kun la thams cad sbyin// 'dod chags chen po nyes spangs te// de ni bdud rtsi 'dra bar 'gyur// 'di ni myur du gar byas pa// bsgrub par mi byed cung zad med//
215a4: 'di ni pad mo sbyor ba yis// bde mchog rtag pa thob par 'gyur// shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i myos par byed pa'i dpal pad mo phreng ba zhes bya ba thams cad kyi don dpal shin tu dgyes par byed pa'i phyag
215a5: rgya'o/ / 'di nyid gnyis pa'i spyi gtsug tu// bsgyur nas gzhag par byas pa ni// ma lus dri ma 'phrog byed pa// sna tshogs chen por de 'gyur ro// 'di yis dbang ni bskur ma thag/ khams gsum sna tshogs
215a6: byed par 'gyur/ / sna tshogs dbang po rgyal po che// sna tshogs gzugs dang sna tshogs bdag/ bsgrub pa thams cad bde dam pa// 'dod pa kun gyi dbang phyug rgya la// 'dod pa'i don kun bsgrub byed pa// thams
215a7: cad 'di yis dngos grub po/ / bud med 'di yis byin brlabs nas// sngo bsangs khur tshes dkar mo dang // de dang lhan cig gar byas pas// sna tshogs bdag po chen por 'gyur// sngo bsangs zhing ma phreng ma
215a8: dag/ byin gyis brlabs nas dus gsum du// mtshan gyis mthar ni bsnyen byas nas// las kyi dngos grub thob par 'gyur// rigs ngan can dang sme ma dang // gar mkhan de bzhin gar byed dag/ phyag

215b1: rgya ye shes byin brlabs te/ / bsnyen dang dngos grub thob par 'gyur// shin tu dgyes pa sna tshogs bde ba sbyin par byed pa zhes bya ba 'dod par byed pa thams cad kyi mchog bslab par byed pa'i phyag rgya'o//
215b2: phyag rgya de dag bstan pa'i rnams// gar gyi tshul gyis rang gi gnas// dam tshig mchog gi dam tshig gis// dngos grub chen po'i mthur 'gyur ro// thal mo de nyid sbyar byas te// rdo rje bcings pas bcing
215b3: bar bya/ / de nas dga' byed dbang bskyed de// mda' yi tshul gyis gzung bar bya// 'di ni rab dgyes gtso bo yis// pha rol phyin mchog sdug pa yin// sangs rgyas rnams kyi myos byed pa// dpa' ba rnams
215b4: kyang rmongs par byed/ / 'di ni bcings pa tsam gyis kyang // mi shes byed pa 'jig par byed// las kyi don ni bka' bzhin du// dga' nas bran bzhin byed par 'gyur// 'di yos byin gyis brlabs pa yis//
215b5: bad chen rgyal po 'dra bar 'gyur// dga' dang lhan cig gar byed cing // 'dod dbang sar ni 'gro bar byed// dpal rdo rje sems dpa' shin tu dgyes pa kun tu bzang mo'i dgyes pa chen mo'i bde ba gnyis su
215b6: med pa dang ldan ma zhes bya ba sbyor ba'i phyag rgya chen po'o/ / snying kar gzung ba'i sbyor ba yis// 'di yis las kun byed 'gyur te// bdud rnams thams cad 'bigs par byed// rgyal ba 'dod chags bral
215b7: spyod pa/ / bde gshegs mya ngan 'das kun dang // thams cad 'di yis slob par byed// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyes byas nas// myur du las la sbyor bar byed// dbang po nyi dbang dbang chen gyi// gdug pa
215b8: thams cad 'joms byed do/ / 'jigs byed drag po chen po yis// gdug pa thams cad gdung par byed// rdo rje pad mor bcug pa yis// mche bas ma mchu bzung byas te// sor mo phan tshun bsnol ba

216a1: yis/ / dang ba brgyang ste gar du bya// sna tshogs chen po brgyas pas// de chen po yi bde 'thob bo// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// 'dod da thangar bar grub byed te// phyag rgyu 'di yis
216a2: rgyas btab na/ / 'dod pa bzhin du 'phur bar byed// rab dgyes 'brel bas gar byas shing // nam mkha' gzungs ma'i thabs nyid kyis// phan tshun bcu pa'i gnon pa yis// bcings ni 'di yis dngos
216a3: grub bo/ / de ni de ma thag tu yang // lha dang lha min mchod byed de// dbang po nye dbang dbang chen dang // nyi zla gshin rje chu dbang rnams// spyi bo yis ni phyag byas nas// rang gi dpal mchog stobs byed de//
216a4: rdo rje 'dzin pa thams cad kyang // nyid kyis dpal can stobs pa yis// brtan pa de la mgu byed cing // sangs rgyas dgos pa rab sgrub byed// 'di yis las kyi tshul gyi rnams// las dang rjes su 'thun 'gyur te//
216a5: rnal 'byor dbang phyug rnam mdzad pas// sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam sbyor te// gzungs dang gnyis med sbyor ba yis// yid la 'dod pa'i las kun byed// 'dzum dang gnas dang sbas pa dang // spyod pas gar gyis
216a6: byas pas so/ / gzhan dag kyang de dngos grub che// pad mo'i 'dab ma rnams phye bas// byang chub sems ni rab bsgrub pa// bsgrub pa pos ni pad mo bsgrub// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi// bde ba gnyis
216a7: su med pa'i dpal/ / shin tu dgyes pa'i pad mo 'dab ma zhes bya ba shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i bde ba 'tho bar byed pa'o// thal mo de nyid bcings pa yis// bcings pa gyen du bzung byas te// mthe'u chung gnyis
216a8: di bsgreng byas te/ / de bzhin sbom po gnyis kyang bya/ phyag rgya 'di ni chu srin zhes// rgyal mtshan ldan par bshad pa yin// rdo rje sems dpa' sprul pa ste// 'dod bral chags par bsgrub pa yin// phyag rgya 'di/

216b1: yis bde ldan gyi// byung rnon por 'gro bar byed/ der byin chos kyis 'khor lo dag/ tha med par ni sor bar byed// sungs smras pa rol gyin mas bstod/ sdig smrangs rnams ni zhag nas kyang /
216b2: spyod pa drag po'i tshul gyis ni// bskal pa bye bar bsten par byed// yang dag byang chub gnas pa yi// sangs rgyas 'di yid mnyes par byed// de nas dgyes te sna tshogs che// sna tshogs ye shes
216b3: ba yi/ / rang gi dam tshig gsungs pa yi// sems dpa' chen po grub par byed// tha med dngos grub thams cad kyang // 'di yis thams cad grub par byed// sbyor dang ldan pas byin brlabs te// snying
216b4: khar nye bar bsam byas na/ / las kyi ngo bo tshul 'di yis// thams cad las ni byed du gzhug/ gar dang dbyangs kyi ro dga' dang // sil snyan brdung ba rnams byed dang // pi bang gling bu rdza rnga ya/
216b5: phyag rgya 'di yis bsgrub par bya// dpal rdo rje shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i thugs kyi dgyes pa dpe med pa dang ldan ma zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// thal mo de nyid mnyam bzung nas// 'gying zhing 'gying bas ga
216b6: byas te/ / bcing ba chen po bcings byas nas// sbyor ba chen po gnyis su bya// khu tshur gnyis po dgu lji du// g.yon du 'gying bas btan par bya// phyag rgya 'di ni rgyal la sogs// bde ba dam pas mchog/
216b7: byas te// 'gying ba'i sbyor bas gar byas na// dngos grub thams cad grub par byed// 'gying ba tsam gyi sbyor ba yis// 'gying ba thams cad 'phrog par byed// lha dang lha min rig ma yis// 'bum phrag brgya yis mchod par/
216b8: byed// rab tu dgyes pa bde mchog che// kun tu gar byas gnas par 'gyur// klum lha dang lha min dang // de bzhin mi 'am bdag por 'gyur// nam mkhar 'gro ma'i khyor 'gyur te// rnal 'byor ma kun bde ba che//

217a1: gzungs ma rnams kyi dag pa bdag/ gas ba pha rol phyin pa'i rje// las kyi sbyor ba 'di yas ni// thams cad las ni byed par bshad// sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba che// gsang chen sbyor bas
217a2: dngos grub bo/ / dpal shin tu dgyes pa bdeb chen mo sems can thams cad sgrol bar sbas paM zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya thams cad 'grub pa'o// phyag d+ha de nyid mnyam bzung sa// lag pa'i rab ma gar dang bcas//
217a3: sbyar bar skad du dor ba yis// mgyogs su 'gro ba dngos grub po// 'di yis sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// rmad 'byung dam pa mchod byas pa// sbyor ba gar gyis mchod byas na// thams cad las byed dngos
217a4: grub po/ / gang dag dngos grub med pa dang // gang dag bde ba med pa'i rnams// de dag phyag rgya 'dis btab na// nam mkha'i dkyil 'khor 'gro bar 'gyur// de yis thams cad las rnams ni// mad 'byung ngam
217a5: pa 'grub par byed/ / btsun mo chen po de bzhin gshegs// 'di yis de ni 'grub par byed// gzhan yang mchog tu rgya che ba// mnyam dang mi mnyam chos kyi dbyings// brdzun mo dam pa de bzhin gshegs//
217a6: phyag rgya'i sbyor bas dngos grub po// dpal bde ba chen po rdo rje rab tu dgyes pa'i me tog gi phreng ba zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// de nyid 'og gi ngos su dong// steng du cung zad pa sgrub par bya// 'di yis sangs rgyas thams cad
217a7: de mchog yid ni tshim byed pa/ / 'dis ni bcings pa tsam gyis kyang // bdud rnams shin tu ring bar 'gyur// phyag rgya bcings te bsdigs pa yis// sgra ga nas dngos grub sbyin par byed// sangs rgyas dam
217a8: tshig gsum gnas pa'i/ / 'di yis mchod pa byas par 'gyur// de nas gtso 'o 'dis mnyes nas// mchog gi thabs ni stob par byed// phyag rgya bcings pa sbyor ba yis// 'di ni thams cad byed par 'gyur//

217b1: rgyun tu byas na rnal 'byor pa// dgas pa thams cad byed par 'gyur// sdig pa thams cad 'phrog byed de// bde ba dam pa 'thob byed cing // tshe 'di dang ni pha rol du// b+hag rgya'i gnas srang 'gro'o// dpal shin tu dkyus
217b2: chen po'i bde ba ches par byed pa zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya ste/ / dri ma thams cad spong ba dpal shin tu dgyes ma'o// thal mo de nyid sbom po brnyed // rta la gsal pa'i nyim bzhin// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad hU~M/
217b3: ye shes mchog tu snang byed pa'o// thog ma med nas bskor ba mas// 'di yid gti mug 'phrog byed de// mnyam par gzhag nas bcings ma thag/ sangs rgyas kun gyis byin gyis rlob// mnyam nyid ye shes dri med
217b4: dang / / pad mo dra ba dga' ba che// sna tshogs dra ba dpal chen po// bde phyed chen po 'thob par 'gyur// rdo rje dgyes pa chen mo'i dpe med pa'i dpal dang ldan ma zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// g.yas dang g.yon pa'i lag
217b5: pa yis/ / brjid pa'i gar gyis gar bya zhing / thal mo de nyid mnyam sbyar te// g.yon gyi khu tshur spyi bor gzhag/ rgyal ba rnams kyi phyag rgya 'di// mchod pa thams cad grub byed do// thams cad don rnams grub pa dag/
217b6: bkra shis rgyal ba 'thob par byed// gang zhig bcings pa tsam gyis kyang // mchod pa'i sprin nyid rgyas pa che// mtha' yas dri med gzi brjid dang // sangs rgyas zhing ni dngos grub po// phyag rgya sbyor bas sbyar byas te//
217b7: skad cig gcig gis gar byas na// rdzogs sangs rgyas dang sras mchog kyang // 'di yis thams cad 'bab par 'gyur// sna tshogs kyi ni sbyor ba yis// sna tshogs gar gyis gar byas na// dpa' bo thams cad
217b8: kun tu 'gro/ / phun sum tshogs pa 'dis 'grub po// dpal shin tu dgyes pa chen po bde ba'i sems 'phel bar byed ma zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi

218a1: bdag po dpa la kun tubang po shin tu dgyes la chen po bde ba'i bdag nyid rnam par snang mdzad chen po bshad pa mthas klas pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mchog tu gsang bzlagasang thig le mchog tu pa
218a2: rol du phyin pa/ gsang ba chen po dam tshig gi phyag rgya'i ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor shin tu dgyes pa/ rdo rje gdon mi za ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po bskal pa'i mtha' klas pa zhes bya ba gsum pa rdzogs so// /
218a3: de nas bcom ldan 'das kun tu bzang po'i gsang ba'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i dam tshig gi ye shes kyi phyag rgya'i dkyil 'khor 'di bshad nas slar yang bde bar cang mi gsung bar gnas par gyur to// de nas de bzhin
218a4: gshegs pa de dag thams cad dang / / pha rol du phyin ma rnal 'byor ma chen mo'i tshogs thams cad dang / nam mkha' la 'gro ba dang / nam mkha' la 'gro ma'i tshogs thams cad ngo mtshar du gyur nas phyi nang gi rdo rje
218a5: rigs su gtogs pa 'phrog par byed pa'i tshogs thams cad la slar dbugs byung ste/ / de las bzhengs nas gang mdzad cing rab tu dgyes pa'i spyan rgyas pas bcom ldan 'das la yang dang yang du lta zhing
218a6: dbyangs kyi mchog bde ba 'dis glu blangs te dgyes par byed do/ / rnam mang bde ba'i rol pas bdag nyid chen po yis// skye dang mi skye'i chos nyid ya mtshan rmad dag dpal bstan pa// shin tu bde ba'i dkyil 'khor
218a7: 'jig rten 'dir phyung ste/ / rang bzhin dag pa'i gzungs ma'i dkyil nas bskyed par mdzod// ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos nyid das 'o// mdzad cing // bdud rtsi'i rang bzhin 'dus pa rnams la dbugs 'byin cing //
218a8: gsang ba'i thig la dngos nyid nam mkha' 'dra ba rnams spyad de// bde ba phun sum tshogs pa'i longs spyod rgyu la dbang mdzad pas// byang chub mchog gi lam 'di nyon mongs mtha' dang rnam bral zhing // bde ba'i

218b1: 'byung gnas skye shi med pa'i sgo mor pad mo rnam dag pa/ / nyon mongs mi gos sgyu mar gnas pa chu zla'i dkyil 'khor bzhin// e ma'o kun tu bzang po rig pa rgya chen bsam gyis mi khyab pa// dngos nyid med/
218b2: pa'i chos la dga' ba'i rol pos gzungs su 'gyur// sangs rgyas kun gyis bde mchog bdud ci ras yin// ji ltar bde la rten cing kun tu snang bar mdzad// kye ma bde mchog bde bas rol pa tshul bzhin mdzod/
218b3: sdug bsngal 'gro ba'i las can bde bas tshim par mdzod// byams pa'i spyan can thugs rje nyi mas 'gro ba kun la shar mdzad nas// gti mug thibs po'i mun nag byang chub sems kyis gsal bar ston// de ni
218b4: 'dus pa'i tshogs la bde sbyin rol pa'i rgyal pos gsungs/ byang chub mchog gi sems des snying po mngon thang dpa lung ci// dbyangs kyi phyag rgya 'di yis ni/ skad cig skad cig bskul byas na/ rab tu dgyes pa'i
218b5: bdag nyid kyi/ / mdun du gnas te dngos grub sbyin/ de nas bcom ldan 'das shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i bde ba'i bdag po kun tu bzang po chen po rdo rje zla gsang thig le chen po la rdo rje nam mkha' la 'gro ba gsang
218b6: ba chen po tshad med pa dang / mchog tu pha rol tu phyin pa'i rnal 'byor dang / rnal 'byor ma'i tshogs chen mo de rnams kyis bstod cing bskul ba byas pa dang / gsang ba thams cad kyi bde ba chen po shin tu dgyes pa
218b7: longs spyod pa'i dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyal po 'di la snyoms par zhugs nas/ / shin tu dgyes pa chen po gdon mi za ba'i dam tshigs ces bya ba rnal 'byor ma'i dkyil 'khor chen po 'dir
218b8: gi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo / / gru bzhi pa la sgo bzhi pa// rta babs rnam pa bzhi yis brgyan// dar dang dril bu'i chun po dang // nyi ma zla ba rnam par brgyan// rin chen mu tig 'bras bus spras//

219a1: dog lag du bla rnams kyis brgyan// sna tshogs gdugs ni nam thul ba// sna tshogs phreng bgos kyis brdzun// srad bu ba ni dang ldan pa ste// ka ba brgyad mchog yang dag gnas// ma
219a2: byed stan la ni/ / dngul la sogs pas rnam par brgyan// sna tshogs pad mo der gyis g.yogs// thams cad stan de dag ces bya// dbus su rdo rje shin tu dgyes// stan de la ni gzhag par bya// tshad med pa ma
219a3: dmar 'dra ba'i/ / sna tshogs rgyan gyis rnam par klubs// yid bzhin nor bu dbu rgyan ldan// rin chen gtsug gis rnam par mdzes// tshad med dar ni dbyangs pa yis// dbul chun pos mdzes par bya// sna tshogs
219a4: sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag/ sna tshogs ye shes rab tu gnas// chu skyes spyan ni yid tsam rgyas// dga' byed yid tsam g.yon tu 'dud// g.yas pa'i phyag gi rdo rje che// snying kar gsor la shin tu brtson// de la sogs
219a5: pa'i yon tan ldan/ / thog ma nyid du rnam par gzhag/ slob ma 'am yang na gzhan yang rung // mtshan kun gyis ni rnam brgyan pa// tshul bzhin byin gyis rlab bya ste// dbus kyi dkyil du gzhag par bya// bdag nyid
219a6: kyang ni mnyam gzhag ste/ / de la sogs pa yon tan gtso// dbus kyi bstan la 'dug pa na// bdag ni rab dgyes zhes su smra// des ni slob ma byin brlabs te// thams cad las byed phun sum tshogs// rdo rje
219a7: pad mo las 'byung ba'i/ / gsang ba yis kyang dbang bskur ro// rab dgyes la sogs yon tan ldan// yid 'ong bu mo bcal byas te// mgrin pa dpral ba snyid spyi bor// lha la sogs pa'i 'bru ba sgoms te// mtshan
219a8: phyag rgya 'ab ba/ / rdo rje ba dmor mnyam sbyor ba'i// ral 'thud pa'i phyag rgya yis// tshul bzhin thams cad gzhag par bya// mdun du rna ma skye byed pa// mamathu 'dzin pa'i ram dgyes// dka

219b1: dadamar pa dog 'das pa yis/ / thams cad rgyan dang yang dag ldan// lo nu bcu drug yon du'i mchog/ shes rab can gyis mdun du gzhag/ g.yas sul mo gsong byed pa// btsun na'i bad+ma ni 'drenapa
219b2: btson/ / do shal kang gdub dag gis brgyan// lo grangs nyi shu lon pa ste// gser gyi ri bo zhu ba 'dra// chu skyes spyan ni yid tsam sde// sems dpa' che la dgyes mdzad cing // 'di ni tshul bzhin gzhag par bya//
219b3: rgyab du lha mo rmongs byed ma// pad mo dmar po mdog gi 'od// chu srin rgyal mtshan mdzes ma'o// sku tshe tshad ni nyi shu gcig/ dga' byed 'dod pa'i ro la dgyes// sna tshogs na bza' yang dag gsol// sna tshogs
219b4: rgyan gyis rnam par klubs/ / sna tshogs pad mo sbyor la sogs// gar gyi bya ba rab bslabs gzhag/ g.yon du sna tshogs chen mo ste// sna tshogs dgos pa'i rjes bslabs pa// sku tshe'i tshad ni bcu gnyis ldan//
219b5: rnal 'byor la ni shin tu brtson// lha dang lha min mi yi rnams// 'gro ba thams cad myos 'gyur ma// sna tshogs rgyan gyis rnam par klubs// sna tshogs dar gyi na bza' gsol// grwa rnams kyi rnathams cad du//
219b6: gzugs sgra dri ro reg gi rnams// bdug pa me tog bsung ldan pa// gzi brjed chen po 'od dang ldan// tsi rigs par ni gzhag par bya// sgo yi phyogs rnams thams cad du// rang gi las kyi phyag kyar ldan//
219b7: ldan dga' la rnam mos pa// sgo srungs bzhi ni gzhag par bya// gzhan yang rnam pa sna tshogs rnams// pi bang gling bu brngub pa dang // rdza rnga rnga chen mu ku dang // mu ra dza dang dar dang // gar dang dbyangs dang bzhad pa che//
219b8: rol mo'i yo byad sna tshogs rnams// dga' byed dkyil 'khor gzhag par bya// phyi yi dkyil 'khor thams cad do// dkyil 'khor 'di yi phyi rol du// rdo rje nam mkhar 'gro ma gzhag/ yi dgas rgyal po yang dag

220a1: zhon/ / dpa' bo 'dregs byed gzugs 'dzin te// skal ldan rang gi lag car ldan// gdug pa'i sems kyis bsdigs byed cing // sha khrag dang ni d+hA ma dang // rkang dang rgyal zan spyod pa// dkyil 'dzuH
220a2: byas te 'dug pa ni/ / tshogs kyi dkyil 'khor gzhag par bya// dga' bar byed dang 'dren par byed// gsod par byed dang spro bar byed// rdo rje mkha' 'gro tshogs kyi rnams// shar gyi phyogs su gzhag par bya// gzi
220a3: brjid che dang 'bar byed ma/ / 'jigs bye dbong bu'i lha ru ste// gtsug lag mthong ba'i rgyu yis ni// mkhas pas tshul bzhin gzhag par bya// chags chen mo dang chags bral dang // 'khor lo mo dang rgyas 'debs mo//
220a4: rab tu sbyor bas sbyor byas te// ci rigs nub tu gzhag par bya// sna tshogs lus dang srung ba dang // gnod sbyin ma dang yang dag 'phrog/ sngags dang phyag rgyas byin brlabs te// sngags mkhan ci rigs byed
220a5: du gzhag/ shar gyi grwa ru gzhag pa ni// bya rog gdong ste mig 'dra zhing // 'jigs pa'i mig dang 'jigs pa'i gdong // ji ltar rjes su 'thun byas te// yi dgas stan la yang dag 'dug/ sna tshogs mchog gi mdog
220a6: 'dzin te/ / lag pa dri dang khar gzhong thogs// mchog tu sha dang khrag za ba'o// nub dang lho yi mtshams gzhag pa// bzhad dang 'ug pa'i gdong ring ma// khros pa'i khyi dang phag gi gdong// gsus po che la lto 'phyangs
220a7: ma/ / rngub byang gi ni mtshams dag tu// rnga mo bung bu'i gdong 'dzin dang // khros pa'i ra dang byi la'i gdong // rgyu ma'i mgo nas za byed rnams// shar dang byang gi mtshams dag tu// keng rus dkar ba'i 'dzin pa ste// khros
220a8: pabarus pa'i phreng bas klubs/ / lto 'phyangs mo la bum pa 'dzin// phan tshun 'thab par brtson pa yi// lce sbyang gi ni 'khor gyi rnams// 'jigs byed gdong ni mche ba 'byin// rnam par 'gyur ba'i gzugs 'dzin pa'o//

220b1: grosrungs kyi ni phyogs kun du// sgo bzhi rnams su gzhag bya ba// byang gi phyogs su 'bod 'grogs te// bum pa na ni shar nyid du// nub tu rnam par 'jig pa'o// lhod ni ga shin rje rgyal po gzhag/ de dang gzhan yang
220b2: rgyal po mchog/ nam mkhar 'gro bas kun tu bskor// bum pa rnam pa sna tshogs te// gser dang dngul las byas pa la// sna tshogs gos kyis yang dag dkris// me tog 'bras bu rnams kyis brgyan// bdud rtsi
220b3: lnga yis gang byas pa/ / sman lnga dang ni yang dag ldan// rin chen lnga dang ldan byas pa// 'bru sna lnga yis brgyan byas pa'i// bum pa bcu drug gzhag byas te// bcu gnyis brgyad dam yang na phyed// than chung ngu gcig
220b4: tsam yang / / ji ltar rigs bzhin gzhag byas te// dbus su bum pa ro yi mchog/ dam tshig chus ni gang byas pa// gser ram dngul lam zangs kyang rung // lcags sams las byas pa la// zla ba nyi ma dri chu dang //
220b5: btung ba sum por ldan pa yi// dbang po kun las 'byung ba rnams// sha srad gcig gis rab bsres pa// kun las 'phags pa ro yi mchog/ tshogs kyi dbus su bsgrub byas te// btung ba bzhin du myangs pa yis//
220b6: rdorje tho ldan bskul par gnas// rnam pa sna tshogs nye ba'i zas// bza' ba dang ni bca' bas mchod// mchod pa nye ba'i zas lnga dang // tshad med 'dod pa'i yon tan lngam// tshad med rnal 'byor mtshogs la//
220b7: cig skad cig mchod par bya// sngags mkhan tshul bzhin mnyam gzhag ste// 'thung po rnams la gtor ma sbyin// lha rnams kyi ni thams cad la// he ru ka yi phyag rgya yis// nyid kyi gtor ma byin brlabs te// spyan drangs
220b8: gtsang sbas byas pa dbul/ / gzungs kyi tshogs ni de rnams la// mnyes pa byas nas slar gshegs so// rnal 'byor mchen dkyil 'khor du// slob ma'i mchog ni gzhug par bya// mtshungs par spyod pa rab mdzes ma/

221a1: sna tshogs gos kyis yang dag dkris// lag pa g.yon gyis bzung byas te// rab dgyes longs spyod phyag rgya yis// bcug nas sgo yi ga nyid du// blo ldan dam tshig bsgrag par bya// 'di las mi bya cung zad
221a2: med/ / thabs dang shes rab sems nyid kyis// rtag tu dogs pa med byas te// 'dod pa lnga yi yon tan spyod// gzhan yang dam tshig nyams pa dang // skye bo gang dag dmal gnon// brtul zhugs khyod kyis de drangs te//
221a3: khrag chen po ni btung bar bya// gang dag slob dpon smod byed dang // gang dag bka' rnams mi byed pa// de dag khros nas khrag chen po// blo ldan snying las btung bar bya// dkon mchog gsum la gnod byed dang // slob dpon
221a4: la yang gnod byed pa/ / rdo rje khro bo bsdus pa yis// dam tshig bsgoms te bsgral bar bya// de nas dam tshig blud byas te// rdo rje bdud rtsi ro yi mchog/ dung chen por ni gzhag par bya// rdo rje bdud rtsi'i chu brud do// kye ma/
221a5: dmyal ba yi ni chu 'di ste// khyod kyi snying la kun du gnas// dam tshig bsrungs pas dngos grub ste// rdo rje bdud rtsi'i chu 'di 'thung // oM badz+ra u ta ka hU~M Tha// dam tshig la ni brgyar bzlas pa'i// byin gyis brlabs te
221a6: 'thung du gzhug/ gzhan du dam tshig mi 'gyur te// dngos grub nyid du'ang 'di 'gyur ro// bdag ni dam tshig skal dga' zhes// slob ma sngags ni brjod du gzhug/ sgo grang gnas nas dri bya ba// kye khyod dga' ba ci
221a7: la dang / / 'jug pa yis kyang smra bya ba// bdag ni skal ldan bde mchog la// rab dgyes 'phrul la bdag dga' ste// mchog tu dga' la bdag dga' 'o// de nas rnal 'byor ma mchog gi/ dkyil du me tog bor byas te//
221a8: khe tog gang la lhung ba yi// lha nyid du ni dngos grub po// dbang bskur ba yi phyag rgya yis// de nas spyi bor dbang bskur bya// bum pa rnam pa bzhi yis kyang // mnyam par bzhag ste lnga po yis// pad mo dkyil 'khor

221b1: zhugs byas te/ / de nas yang ni dbang bskur bya// ci rigs par ni gzungs ma rnams// bdag ni skal ldan zhes su smra// gang dag 'gro bar gyur pa yi// lha de nyid ni bstan par bya// dga' bar byed pa'i gzungs pa de'i//
221b2: khyod kyis rtag tu bsgrub par bgyi// de nas rgyal dbang slob ma de// nang gi sbas pa bsdus pa yi// gsang ba mnyam par 'jug pa yis// sbyor dang ldan pas dbang bskur bya// rdo rje pad mo las drangs pa// sbom po dang ni dbang /
221b3: gis blang // rdo rje dag ni du gnag byas na// rtag pa dge ba bde ba che// kye ma'odam tshig bde brjod cing // kye ma bde ba blang bar bya// 'di ni gsang ba zhes bya ste// dbang bskur ba yi thabs mchog go// da rje slo bdon gaganyi
221b4: rang gi khar ni rdo rje gzhag/ sems dpa' chen po drangs byas na// sems kyis byang chub bde ba 'thob// 'di ni mchog tu gsang ba ste// dbang bskur ba yi bde ba'o// slob ma mi shes pa rnams la// 'di dag thams cad
221b5: bsgrags mi bya/ / rdo rje slob dpon gyis bya ba// yang nas yang du brtag par bya// 'di yis dbang ni bskur ma thag/ slob ma tshogs kyi bdag por 'gyur// sangs rgyas rdo rje 'dzin pa yi// slob dpon nyid du bde bar 'gyur//
221b6: gzungs pa rnams kyis dga' ba'i bdag/ sangs rgyas rnams kyi rjer bshad do// mkha' la 'gro ba'i khyod 'gyur te// ri dang 'gro ba kun gyi bdag/ de nas shes rab ye shes dbang // slob ma mchog la sbyin par bya//
221b7: gzungs ma de ni bdag nyid la// bla ma nyid kyis byin brlabs te// dngos grub 'bras bu myur 'thob phyir// slob ma la ni sbyin par bya// dbang bskur shin du sbas pa yis// rdo rje slob dpon tshul ji bzhin// blo ldan the tshom
221b8: med pa'i phyir/ / rnam pa bzhi po 'di sbyin no// de tshun cad ni slob ma la// klud kun las ni gang chung zad// yi ge'i tshul gyis sbas pa rnams// gsang ba mchog ni bstan par bya// de nas de nyid langs byas te// slob dpon

222a1: rkang par gtugs byas nas/ / rgyal po dbang phyug bde dam pa// thams cad yon ni dbul bar bya// gzungs de dag na thams cad la// ci dga' bar ni yon yang 'bral// slob dpon nung zad gang 'dod pa/
222a2: yid la bsams pa'i yon yang rung // dam tshig 'das pas 'jigs pa yis// de dag thams cad dbul bar bya// slob dpon la ni yon gyi mchog/ rigs kyi khyad par dbul byas te// seng ge'i gdan la nyid kyi ma/
222a3: sangs rgyas byin ni yon mchog yin// glang po rin chen gser dag dang // sring mo bla ma'i yon mchog yin// rdo rje sems dpa'i rigs yin te// yon de mchog gi yon yin no// rin chen pad mo'i chung ma dang // shing
222a4: rta rta ni shin tu brgyan/ / sna tshogs rin chen nam dag pa// mu tig phreng bas shin tu mdzes// bu mo rin chen dra ba yis// brgyan te sna tshogs rdo rje la'o// rgyal po yi ni dbang phyug dang // chung ma bla ma dbul bar bya//
222a5: 'phrul gyi bzhon pa rnam sna tshogs// glang po rta ni shin tu brgyan// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi rje// nan tan bla ma dbul bar bya// bla ma'i yon gyi phyag rgya 'di// rdo rje blo ldan slob ma yis// ci ste bde byed kun 'dod
222a6: na/ / dga' dngams pa'i sems kyis byed// de la sogs pa'i sbyor ba yis// rab dgyes gdon mi za ba'i bde// gang gis myur du thob 'gyur te// slob dpon gtso mchog nyid du 'gyur// chos rnams kun gyi dbang
222a7: byug rgyal/ / rdo rje blo ldan mchog tu 'byung// rin chen kun gyi rigs kyi rgyal// de bzhin sna tshogs rigs ldan du// pad mo'i rigs kun dpal dang ldan// rdo rje rigs kun bdag por de// sangs rgyas kyi ni rigs
222a8: kun dang / / rgyal ba'i gtso bo mchog tu 'gyur// dkyil 'khor gyi ni 'khor lo'i gar// nyid dang slob ma'i tshigs gyur pas// rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba che// sems dpa' bdag nyid mchod par bya// pan tshun laso rba//

222b1: tshul gyis ni// shes rab mchod pa'i spor ba yis// rdo rje che yi thabs gnas te// mkha' 'gro kun la mchod 'gyur// phyi yi sbas pa gsang la sogs// nang gi mchod pa mchog gi rnams// phyag rgya'i sbyor ba tshul
222b2: gnas te/ / tshul bzhin rgyas bdab dbul bar bya// lus dang ngag sems bde byed kyis// mchod pa'i bdag nyid ma chad par bya// 'dod pa'i rol pa myong ba yi// myangs na mchod pa 'thob par 'gyur// mchod pa kun gyi
222b3: cho ga yis/ / rang rigs khyad par shes byas te// bsgrub pa thams cad bsgrub byas na// dngos grub thams cad myur du 'thob// dkyil 'khor 'khor lo 'di mthong bas// dga' mgu rangs pa'i yid kyis ni// rdo rje
222b4: sems la phyag byed cing / / rang gi dkyil 'khor gsol ba 'debs// bde byed chen po'i dkyil mo rgya// rigs kyi khyad par gyis ni lnga// lha rnams kyang ni re re yang // sems kyi khyad par mchod mtha' yas// 'das
222b5: pa'i dus nam byung ba/ / mtha' yas chos ni yangs pa bstan// 'dod chags rnams kyis dkris pa yi// sdug bsngal gzir ba'i mtha' nas 'gro// 'dod pa'i mchog gi longs spyod rnams// mos pa'i rjes su
222b6: zhugs shing spyod/ / kun tu chags par mi 'gyur zhing // bde bas lengs pa'i yid dang ldan// byang chub snying por bgrod pa ni// dam bcas rnams dang sems kyis so// de nas bcom ldan 'das shin tu dgyes pa
222b7: thams cad kyi bdag po kun tu bzang po chen po/ / rab tu bzhad cing spyan zur gyis gzigs pa'i thugs kyis shin tu dgyes pa// kun tu longs spyod pa'i dkyil mo dkrung gi dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la
222b8: snyoms par zhugs nas/ dkyil mo dkrung chen po'i dpal zhes bya ba rang gi phyag rgya'i ye shes nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // g.yas dang g.yon gyi tshul gyis ni// rkang pa gnyis ka bteg

223a1: byas te/ / bdag nyid brla ni mi snang bzhin// rtsa ba dkyil mo bcing bar bya// sbyor ba gar mkhan tshul gyis ni// gar gyi sbyor bas gar bya'o// rdo rje gdadun gyi bde ba che// 'di yis bdud las rgya la
223a2: bar 'gyur/ / gdug pa dang ni dgra thams cad// skad cig gis kyang spros ci dgos// rab tu dgyes pa'i stan 'di yis// yang dag byang chub myur du 'thob// mi phyed pa ni thig ler bcas// 'og gi phyogs su yi ge
223a3: drug/ shes rab can gyis bskyod cing bzlas// 'byung ba'i tshe ni phaT ces bshad// pad mo mi phyed 'dren pa dang // thig ler bcas pa sbyor bar bya// mi phyed oM dang yang dag ldan// tsheg drag bcas pa bde 'byung nel
223a4: bud med la ni zhag bdun du/ / 'di yis rtsen par byas pa na// nam mkha' thams cad gang ba yi// sangs rgyas rnal 'byor chen po mthong // rab dgyes longs spyod gnas pa yi// sems dpa' che la slong mdzad de// gzungs
223a5: kyi pad mo las byung ba/ / bde byed mchog gi dbang bskur ro// de nas rab dga' bde thob pa// sems dpa' de ni dngos grub po// thog ma dang ni mtha' med par// 'dod pa thams cad de longs spyod// tshe dang dpal dang
223a6: phun sum ldan/ / gdon dang du gdas che ba'i nang // mkha' 'gros nye bar gtses pa dang // sdig can 'khor ba las grol te// sa rnams kun la rnam par rgyu// gzi brjid nyi ma shar dang 'dra // sna tshogs 'dra ba 'bar
223a7: byed pas/ / sna tshogs thams cad snang byed cing // de yis sems can thams cad kyi// nad dang mya ngan 'jigs chen 'phrog/ phyag rgya 'di yis sbyor ba yis// ye shes lnga ni bsten par bya// rtsa ba'i dkyil mo
223a8: zhes bya ba phyag rgya chen po'i las kyi don thams cad sgrub par byed pa'o/ / bdag gi rkang pa dbus su bsdu// de yi rkang pas bcings byas te// sems dpa'i dkyil mo bzhin du 'brel// 'di ni bcings pa tsam gyis kyang //

223b1: khams gsum sgrub par bzhad pa yin// yi ge rnams ni snga ma bzhin// rang gi lhang ni sbyor brtson pas// bsgoms sam yang na bskyod kyang rung // sngags pa 'di yis dngos grub ste// sngags kyi sems 'dzin/
223b2: gtsang ma yi// zhag bdun bsgom pa bsgom byas nas// yang dag dngos grub nyid du 'gyur// phyag rgya 'di yis rgyas btab te// sbyor ba shin tu bsten byas na// gdon mi za bar rgyal po 'thob// yid bzhin
223b3: dgos pa thams cad byed/ / rdo rje dkyil mo dkrung ngo // gzungs ma bzung ste bcing ba na// rin po che ltar sbyar byas te// rang gi rkang pa mi snang bya// rin chen kun gyi dkyil mo dkrung // 'di ni rin chen thams
223b4: cad kyi/ / dbul zhing phongs pa 'joms byed de// sdig pa thams cad 'phrog byed ma// gnod pa'i dug kun 'phrog par byed// gdug pa thams cad rmongs byed de// dgra rnams thams cad 'joms par
223b5: byed/ / khro bo thams cad 'dzum byed de// gdug pa rnams kyi rgyas 'debs na// mi g.yeng zla ba gcig gis ni// 'di yis rgyal po dngos grub po// yid bzhin las rnams thams cad byed// ci ste
223b6: bdag nyid rgyal po ru/ / mchog tu rmad 'byung ba sgrub 'dod na// rin chen sems kyi rin chen mtshan// gsang ba'i phyag rgya tshul gnon pa// rgyal po khams gsum rgyal byed pa// zla phyed tsam gyis 'grub
223b7: par 'gyur/ / rin po che yi dkyil mo'o// de bzhin rkang pa gnyis bzhag pa// pad mo 'dra bar sbyar byas te// bdag gam de bzhin gzhan yang rung // blo ldan pad mo bde bsgrub bya// 'di yis sems can thams
223b8: cad dang / / mdor na sangs rgyas rnam dag dang // rdo rje nyi ma ma lus kyang // dbang du 'gyur ba gdon mi za// bde ldan pho brang chen po yi// bde byed 'di yis 'thob par byed// sems can khams rnams

224a1: thams ca / / sems dpa' chen pa 'gru'ang byed// pad pa 'ad kyil mo'o// de bzhin dkyil po d+ha ma b+h+yas// / swA tshogs rtul gyis spyod babya// sngags pa 'ananan po'i snor ba stis// rtags
224a2: mkhan yi ge shin du brtson/ / zlos pa byed cing rnam bsgoms na// dngos grub rtag pa thob par 'gyur// pi g.yeng sngon gyi gdug pa yi// las rnams thams cad 'phrog par byed// snga tshogs dkyil du ga nas
224a3: yis/ / bra med dngos grub thob par 'gyur// sna tshogs kyi ni dkyil mo'o// de nas mkha' 'gro ma'i dkyil mo rgyas// thams cad khrag ni 'phrog byas te// gzungs ma yi ni rkang pa gnyis// yid kyis gnyis
224a4: par rkang pa bteg/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyor ba yis// bsnyen pa khrag rnams 'phrog par byed// mnyam par bzhag nas gzungs ma yi// rkang pa gcig ni mgul nyid du// sbyor dang ldan pas bteg byas na//
224a5: zas rnams thams cad 'phrog byed de// btung dang bza' ba bca' ba dang // gos kyi rgyan gyis grubs pa yis// de bzhin zhag bdun nyid kyis kyang // thams cad las byed gdon mi za// tshangs pa rtogs 'dod
224a6: dbang po'i/ / dpal chen mchog ni 'phrog par byed// lag pa bsgreng ba'i tshul gyis ni// khams gsum rim par rgal bar byed// mig ni btsums par byed 'gyur ba// 'gro ba gsum po rnam par 'jig/
224a7: ru sbal bzhin du mnyam bzhag ste// mi g.yeng skad cig bcing byas na// gdug pa'i srog chags thams cad dang // dgra dang spyod bcas mi spyod phrog/ sbal ba bzhin du mnyam bzhag ste// dkyil 'khor
224a8: tshul gyis bskor bar bya'o/ / ma lus rnams kyang rmongs byed de// khams gsum rnams kyang rgal bar byed// gtogs 'dod kyi ni mnyam gzhag ste// sa gsum rnams kyi rgyas gdab bya// gar dbang gi ni

224b1: mnyam bzhag/ / / sa gsu ma rnams ni gar byed ga// rjem du yi na mnyam bzhag ste// sa gsus rnams ni gdab par u0f7f// gzhon du thaMd kyil bci pa ma// sangs rgyas pa chen 'thob bar
224b2: byed/ / dkyil mo byed ni mnyam bzhag nas// gnyis pa yis ni gnan byas na// khams gsum thams cad gnon 'gyur zhing // 'dod byed thams cad dngos grub bo// dga'abyed ma yi mnyam bzhag
224b3: pas/ / dkyil mo rab tu dga' thob ste// dga' byed ma yi yid 'ong ma// khams gsum thams cad dngos grub bo// rig 'dzin rnam par gzhag byas te// khams gsum skad cig gnan par bya/
224b4: kham gsum rnam par rgyal ba yi// mdor bsdus gzungs ma'i bcings pa yis// 'jig rten gsum ni rnam rgyal te// skad cig khams gsum bdag por 'gyur// rtag par phan tshun 'brel ba yis//
224b5: dpud pa gnyis ni bskum byas te// thams cad sgo ni 'gags pa yis// mche ba sbom po rab tu sbyar// g.yas kyi brkyad bskum tshul gyis ni// gnon pa'i gnas pas bsdigs byas te// mi phyed sbyor bas/
224b6: bskul bya ba// khros pa'i sems kyis med par bya// g.yon pa'i brkyang bskum sbyar bar bya// myur du gnan pas bteg bya zhing // mthe'u chung bod pa'i lcags kyu yis// 'dzub mo lce la reg byas te// sa bon
224b7: tsheg drag hri ldan pa'i/ / thig le'i spyi bor brgyan byas pas// bdud rtsi 'am rig ma drang bar bya// lce yi thog mar spro byas te// 'dren pa'i tshul gyis drang bar bya// rdo rje gnod sbyin mnyam bzhag ste/
224b8: kha yi phyogs su mche ba yis// sbom po lce dang 'ang byas te// khros pa mche ba sbyor ba yis// sor mo thod pa bzhin byas na// khrag mang po ni btung bar bya// yi ge dang po oM dang ldan// spyi bor thig le

225a1: ldan byas te/ / 'og gi phyogs su ra yi gdags// u 'dre nang ros brgyan par bya// 'di ni khro bo'i stong po ste// mchog tu thams cad las byed pa'o// gsod pa dang ni 'dren pa kun// dbang dang dbang rnam
225a2: byed la sogs/ / de la sogs pa'i las gzhan yang // tshul bzhin sbyar bas byed par 'gyur// shi ba bzhin du mig btsum nas// rang gi lus ni bskum byas te// bum pa lnga mtha'i sbyor ba yis// dgra rnams
225a3: thams cad bsad par bya/ / nga ro dang po yang dag ldan// bdag nyid ngo bo thams cad bya// sangs rgyas chen po bsgom byas te// zhi ba'i 'od zer sprin phung spro// de yi lus ni zhi bar 'gyur// de yis sems can thams cad
225a4: kyi/ tsha ba gdon dang dug la sogs// sdug bsngal mkha' 'gro'i mche ba dang // 'jigs pa thams cad bral bar byed// shes rab pha rol phyin mnyam gzhag/ bdag nyid kyis ni tshul bzhin du// 'di yis thams cad
225a5: nang gi rnams/ / sdug bsngal dogs pa 'phrog par byed// de la sogs pa mtha' yas pa// nam mkha' sa sted las kyi rnams// snying khar rdo rje sems dpa' gzhag/ yid bzhin thams cad byed par 'gyur// myur du
225a6: rdo rje slob dpon la/ / sngags kyi dngos grub don 'dod pas// gus pa zhes sar bcas pa yi// shin tu lhag par phyogs par bya// nam yang rdo rje slob dpon gyi// sems ni dkrug par mi bya ste// ci ste shes rab 'tshal
225a7: bas byed/ / myur dun rag ltung bar 'gyur// nad dang 'tshe ba dgra dag dang // gdon dang tsha bdug nyid kyis// slob dpon zhabs la spod byed pa// gti mug chen por de 'chi'o// bla ma las ni dngos grub 'thob// bla ma mtho
225a8: ris bla ma bde/ / de bas nan tan thams cad kyi// bla ma'i bka' las 'da' mi bya// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i bdag po kun tu bzang po chen po dpal shin tu dgyes pa chen

225b1: p o'i bde ba chen po rdo rje sems dpa' shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i bde ba gdon mi za ba'i rdo rje dmachog zhi dbang bskur ba'i ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor chen po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs
225b2: rdo rje mchog gsang ba sdus pa chen po zla gsang thig le'i rgyud kyi rgyal po shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i rdo rje rnal 'byor ma chen mo'i tshogs kyi dkyil 'khor te bzhi pa'o/ / / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs
225b3: pa'akhor dang bcas pa'i 'khor lo'i tsho gas dang/ rdo rje rnal 'byor pa dang / rnal 'byor ma dang / rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po'i tshogs dang / rdo rje nam mkha' la 'gro ba dang / nam mkha' la 'gro ma'i tshogs kyi
225b4: g.yog rnams mchog tu dga' ba chen po skyes te/ / ca co 'byin cing dbyangs chen po brjod par gyur te// kye ma'o rdo rje sems dpa' yi// rdo rje shin tu dgyes pa che// sna tshogs thabs ni bde byed che// sna
225b5: tshogs ye shes bde ba che/ / kye ma kun tu bzang po yi// dge ba'i ye shes bde ba che// gang bde phyir ni rig ma yi// pad mo las ni gnas pa mdzad// kye ma'o rig pa shin tu zab// shes rab pha rol phyin pa bde//
225b6: sems can kun la shes rab kyis// mun pa'i thibs po sel bar mdzad// kye ma'o thams cad ngo mtshar che// mkha' 'gro'i dra bas gar mdzad cing // rnam par mdzad dang myang ba dang // mnye ba dang ni 'phrog
225b7: pa'i mchog/ e ma'o shin tu rab tu dgyes// skal ldan skal la sprod pa dang // sna tshogs skal pas bde byed che// sna tshogs rdo rje shin tu mdzes// de nas bcom ldan 'das kun tu bzang po chen po shin tu
225b8: dgyes pa chen po kun tu longs spyod pa'i 'dod pa'i lha shin tu dgyes pa bde ba chen po la gnas pa la rnal 'byor ma thams cad dang / mchog gi pha rol phyin ma la sogs pa rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen mo

226a1: thams cad nga gi gdan las bzhed sa te/ shin tu dgyes pa bde ba chen po'i 'bring ba'i 'drud pas pa rdzu/ shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i bde ba 'thob par byed pa'i dbyangs kyi phyag rgyu chen pa
226a2: 'dis mnyes par mdzad do/ / sna ma'i bde bas nam mkha' kun tu gang ba yi// sprul pa'i rang bzhin skye ba mchog gi bde ston to// rjes su chags pa'i pad ma dga' bas kun khyab cing // chos kyi bde ba
226a3: nyid kyang kun tu btang snyoms mdzad/ / e ma'o 'di lta'i gzungs ma bde mchog dpal dang rnam ldan ma// byams ma'i phyogs su mi gtod ye shes nyid kyis 'jug/ 'dod pa'i yon tan 'di rnams chos
226a4: nyid rnam par dag/ dug gsum dbang du mdzad cing mos pa rnams mi bskyod// ngo mtshar phyogs dang ma bral byang chub snying por bgrong // de nas bcom ldan 'das dpal kun tu bzang po 'dzum pa dang
226a5: bcas pa'i spyan rgyas pas 'khor dang ga thams cad la yud tsam yung tsam kun tu gzigs te/ / rdo rje pad mo dang gnyis su med pa'i sbyor ba'i dpal chen mo zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhus
226a6: te/ cang mi gsung bar mnyam par zhugs te/ dbugs mi rngub dbugs mi 'byin/ dbugs rab tu gtong bar mi mdzad/ kun tu mi gzigs/ kun tu rnam par mi gzigs/ bzhengs par mi mdzad
226a7: bzhugs par mi mdzad/ gshegs par mi mdzad/ gsung bar yang mi mdzad/ rnam par rtog par yang mi mdzad bzhin du bcom ldan 'das shin tu bde ba chen pos nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad du
226a8: shin tu khyab par shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i bde ba las bcal te rgyas par mdzad pa na/ der de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad drangs bcug bcings dbang du byas te/ 'dod pa lnga'i yon tan gyis

226b1: mnyes par byas te bzhugs par gyur to/ / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad yang 'dra ba mdzad nas/ yang nas yang bcom ldan 'das ma gzigs te/ de ba che pon
226b2: tu byas pa dang gnyis su med par longs spyod pa dpal chen po zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs te/ skul nas bcom ldan 'das kyis thugs par zhugs te/ byang chub kyis pa
226b3: chen po la yang thim par gyur pa na/ khams gsum 'dir dam pa'i chos ston pa dang 'jug pa byed pa dang bstan pa la gnas par byed pa 'ga' yang med de/ sangs rgyas dang / chos dang dge 'dun 'jug par byed pa
226b4: yang med khros pa dang gtum po chen po dang rngam pa dang rab tu gdug pa chen por sems pa dang 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi mun pas bsgribs pa dang / gtum 'khrug chen po dang / gzhan gyi srog 'phrog
226b5: pa dang / gzhan gyi sems 'phrog pa dang / gzhan gyi bud med kyis 'chums pa dang / tshig rtsub mo la sogs pa'i nyon mongs pa dang / nye ba'i nyon mongs pas gzhan la gtses pa dang / gcig gi sha gcig zab
226b6: dang / thab med pa'i lam la gnas pa rnams kyis/ kye ma'o 'jig rten gsum po 'di brlag go zhes sngon gyi smon lam las kyis stobs la gnas pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis gzigs so// thabs
226b7: dang shes rab kyi thugs rje'i smon lam chen po nam mkha'i dbyings kun tu yang dag par gnas pa 'di lta bu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rab tu brlag par gzigs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
226b8: kyi bdag po shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i bde ba yang dag par zhugs pa kun tu bzang po chen po dpal rdo rje sems dpa' la dbyangs kyi rgyal po 'dis bskul ba mdzad do/ / ho rang bzhin dag ba pad ma bde ba'i mchog

227a1: mnga' ba/ / thugs kyi yid bzhin rin chen gzhan la dgongs nas bzhengs mdzad de// bskal pa mtha' nas bsgrubs pa'i byams pas gzugs kyis brjid pa dang // byang chub snying po'i chu las 'gro ba
227a2: rnams kyis rang bzhin khrus/ / a la lal to// pad ma'i 'byung gnas bder gshegs kun gyi mchog dang ldan// sdug bsngal kun sel ba yi thugs rjes 'jig rten gsum la gzigs// dga' ba'i rol bas gar dang
227a3: bcas te bzhengs shing dbang du mdzod/ / a la la la to// sngon gyi rgyal po rnams kyis ma bsgrags gsang ba ba'i// 'gro ba kun gyi yid dang 'thad pa'i gsang chen 'di byung ste// rnam dag spyod yul gzhan gyis mi 'phrogs nam
227a4: mkha' la/ / dngos med rol mo'i gzhan las 'phags pa bzhes shing mdzad du gsol// a la la la ho// skad cig ma yi spyod yul 'dis// mun pa thams cad sel ba'i phyir// gzhan la thugs rjes dgongs nas su/
227a5: lha rnams byin gyis bslab du gsol// dbyangs kyi rgyal po 'di yis ni// dgyes mchog dam pa bskul byas na// pad mo dra ba rdo rje dang // bde bar sbyor bas bzhengs su gsol// bde ba chen po bde gnas pa// gtso la 'di
227a6: yis bskul ba yis/ / sems can kun don bzhengs 'gyur te// rgyal ba thams cad gdon par mdzad// de nas bcom ldan 'das bde ba chen po kun tu bzang po dpal rdo rje 'dzin yang dag pa dang ldan pa'i bde ba
227a7: chen pos brgyan pa'i dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ bzhengs nas phyogs bcu mtha' yas rab 'byam mthas klas pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kun gzigs nas ngo mtshar du gyur te/
227a8: ma'o khams gsu 'di stongs so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi phyag rgya chen po rnams dang bral bas gdug pa thams cad kyis 'di dag nye bar gtses/ gnod sbyin dang srin po thams cad dang / nad dang 'tshe ba

227b1: d ang gdon chen po dang nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa thams cad kyis yang dag par zos shes dgongs pa na bcom ldan 'das kun tu bzang po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad gtong ba'i rdo rje ye shes kyi
227b2: bde ba chen po dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs rdo rje ye shes bde ba chen po'i rang gi rdo rje dang pad mo las byang chub kyi sems nye bar bsdu bar bya ste nyid kyi/
227b3: skudang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // thog mar oM ni thig ler bsam byas pa'i// rdo rje sems dpa' bcas pa 'brug gi sgra 'byin pa// mi 'byed 'dren pa yang dag gnyis dang ldan pa ste// 'di na ston pa'i
227b4: mchog ste rdo rje'i rigs nyid do/ / phyung nas nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad du gang ba'i spro bas snang bar byas te// slar yang 'dus nas rdo rje lta bur gnas so// yang spro ba dang bsdu ba byas nas slar 'dus pa las de bzhin
227b5: gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje sems dpa' lta bur gyur nas/ shar gyi dkyil 'khor dbus su bzhugs par gyur pa na/ hUM rU hUM zhes bzhad pa chen por bzhad cing a zhes brjod nas
227b6: bzhugs te/ rang gi sems dpa'i dkyil mos g.yon du yid tsam 'bying bas 'dud pa/ g.yas kyis rdo rjes gsor zhing 'dzum pa dang bcas shing spyan rgyas pa/ che ba'i chen po dbu lnga pa// phyag ni bcu drug rnams
227b7: dang ldan/ / sna tshogs su ni mchog 'dzin pa// dpa' bo thams cad las byed pa// kha dog rnam lnga gzi brjid che// mtshon cha rnam pa sna tshogs 'dzin// rdo rje sgyu mar rab tu gnas// mkhas pa gang gis snying kha nyid/
227b8: mnyam par bzhag ste 'dzin byas na// rdo rje pad mo bde che yis// rdo rje sems dpa' bde myur 'thob// de nas bcom ldan 'das nam mkhar 'gro ma kun longs spyod pa'i dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par

228a1: zhugs te/ / nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las mchog tu gsang ba de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi zla gsang thig le las/ nam mkha' shin tu dgyes pa 'thob par byed pa'i bde ba chen po
228a2: zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di phyung ngo / / oM yi gtsug tu thig le ste// mi phyed thig ler bcas pa yi// 'og tu gzi brjid yang dag bcas// mthar ni dril ste tsheg drag bcas// 'di
228a3: ni rin chen thams cad kyi/ / snying po mchog tu rmad 'byung ba'o// phyung ba yis ni nam mkha' dang // sangs rgyas kyi ni zhing kun tu// 'od zer sprin phung rgyas byas te// slar yang de nyid bzhugs par 'gyur// de
228a4: yi thugs kar zhugs nas kyang / / brda yi tshul gyis bzhugs par 'gyur// rgyal ba kun gyis dbang bskur nas// sems dpa'i tshul gyis sprul pa ni// kha dog rnam lnga yangs pa'i spyan// chu skyes bzhad pa
228a5: 'dzum dang bcas/ / nyi ma'i gzi brjid mdzes pa che// phyag rgya la sogs sna tshogs brgyan// dkyil mo 'gying ba yon du 'dud// g.yas kyi snying khar rin chen 'dzin// brgyad gnyis phyag rgya ngo bo yis// dri ma gsum
228a6: spangs brgyan pa ste/ / rang gi dkyil 'khor gang byas nas// sna tshogs lho ru gnas par 'gyur// rnam pa kun mkhyen mngon rig pa'i// nad kyis glongs pa 'jig par 'gyur// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi//
228a7: gzi brjid chen mo mdangs che ba// dbul dang nang dang gnod chen po// sems can kun gyi 'phrogs par byed// nyi ma 'char ba'i dus nyid dang // nyi ma phyed pa'i dus nyid du// nyid kyi snying kar 'di byas te// nor
228a8: bu rin chen bsgom byas na/ / zhag bdun gyis ni nges par yang // dngos grub nor mang sbyin mdzad de// dbang po gnyis kyi sbyor ba yis// kye ma'o bde bas dbang bskur bya// de nas bcom ldan 'das kun tu bzang/

228b1: po chen po mchog tu bde ba chen po dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i shin tu dgyes pa'i 'dod pa'i dbang gi dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te// pad mo chen po kun tu gzigs pa'i longs spyod pa'i dpal
228b2: zhes bya ba'i snying po chen po nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi ye shes mchog tu gsang bzla gsang thig le las 'di phyung ngo / / dang por oM dang ldan byas te// mi phyed rab btags 'dren par bcas// tsheg drag
228b3: pa ni sngags yin te/ / bsam pa thams cad yongs su bskor// sngags mkhan gang gis mnyam bzhag ste// snying khar 'di ni sbyar byas nas// bdag ni 'dod chags zhen sems shing // pad mo sbyar bas bsgom
228b4: par bya/ / mtshams kyi mtha' ma dus dag tu/ dam tshig 'di ni spyad byas na// zla ba phyed kyi nang logs su// dbang phyug mo ni dngos grub 'thob// pad mo che las byung nas kyang // thams cad du ni rgyas 'gyur te/
228b5: 'di nyid du ni slar zhugs nas// pad mo'i tshul gyis gnas par gyur// kun tu snang bas khyab byas na// sems dpa'i tshul gyis sprul pa ni// de nas 'dod chags babs nas kyang // pad mo'i dbus su zhugs
228b6: par gyur/ / dkyil 'khor du ni gang ba yis// rgyab nas rjes su mnyes mdzad cing // 'dzum bcas pad mo phye ba yis// thugs kyi dbus su yid tsam 'dud// dpal dang ldan pa zhag lnga 'dzin// phyag ni nyi shur
228b7: bzhis ma bltam/ / mtshon cha rnam pa sna tshogs ldan// sna tshogs rgyan gyis klubs pa yis// zla ba bzhin du rnam grol ba// brjid pas gar ni mdzad cing bzhugs// 'di yis pad mo'i gnas nyid du//
228b8: tshe 'di nyid la 'thob par 'gyur// dpal ldan gar dbang thob 'gyur te// 'dod chags kun gyis thabs gnas pas// 'jam pa'i phyag ni stong rnams kyi// gar du mdzad cing 'gro ba 'dul// de nas bcom

229a1: ldan 'das shin tu dgyes pa chen po'i bde ba chen po kun tu bzang pos yang sna tshogs chen po kun tu longs spyod pa'i rnam par 'gyur ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ nyid kyi
229a2: sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i ye shes mchog tu gsang ba zla gsang thig le chen po las phyung ba/ / sna tshogs chen po oM chen po// steng du thig ler yang dag ldan// 'di ni dbus te lha 'og khro// sngags kyi
229a3: mchog ni gzhag par bya/ / sna tshogs 'di ni thugs kar grags// sna tshogs phyung na kun snang bas// sangs rgyas tshul bzhin kun mnyes byas// de nyid slar 'khor rab bzhugs te// sna tshogs rdo rje gzugs
229a4: mchog gnas/ / skad cig sems dpa' sku gnas pa// rnam pa sna tshogs bzhad pas brgyan// 'gying bcas thugs kar sna tshogs 'dzin// sna tshogs gzi brjid 'bar ba gtong // phyag ni brgyad gnyis gnyis
229a5: kyis phyogs/ / kha 'byed sna tshogs mtshon cha gtong // zhal lnga sna tshogs yangs che ba// bgegs spong thams cad dngos grub mdzad/ dkyil 'khor gang bar gzhag nas byang du gnas// phyag tshogs rdo rje bdag mor
229a6: rdo rje yang dag gis/ / thugs khar mdzad nas bde bar yang dag gnas// sngags mkhan zhag bdun du ni bsgom byas na// sna tshogs gyur te sna tshogs de la bab// sna tshogs las ni sna tshogs byed par 'gyur// de
229a7: nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mchog tu ngo mtshar du gyur te/ / dbyangs chen po len cing dkyil 'khor chen po'i dbus kyi bcom ldan 'das la mnyes pa mdzad do// gtso bo byin gyis brlab
229a8: pa'i phyir/ / ye shes lnga yi dngos po dag/ rgyal ba nyid kyis bshad par mdzod// sangs rgyas sku la bstod phyag 'tshal// sngags rig phyag rgya yan lag bcas// lha yi de nyid pha rol phyin// bdag ni de nyid sna

229b1: tshogs che/ / sna tshogs ye shes bstod phyag 'tshal// gzungs kyi pad mo yang dag ldan// 'dod byed thugs kyi mchog yin te// shes rab pha rol phyin sbyor ba// sbyor ba'i ye shes bstod phyag 'tshal// chos kyi don ni gnyis
229b2: mad tshul/ / stong pa nyid kyi lam rig pa// yangs pa'i spyan ni so sor gzigs// me long ye shes yang dag 'byung // bya ba nan tan sems can don// rang gi yon tan mi mnyam shod// de nyid rig pas sems can
229b3: kun/ / rdo rje gsum gyis byin brlabs pa// gang gis byin gyis brlabs ma thag/ sangs rgyas gsum ni dbang du 'gyur// de nas bcom ldan 'das dpal kun tu bzang po gnyis su med pa'i mnyam pa nyid kyi rdo rje
229b4: ye shes zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i 'bru 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // oM b+h+rUM/ stong pa chen
229b5: po'i snying po yi/ oM badz+ra tsi ta hUM/ oM badz+ra kA ya oM/ oM badz+ra bA ga AH/ oM badz+ra a b+hi shinya tsatraM/ oM badz+ra sa pa ya hU~M// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad shin tu mgu/ rab tu dgyes pa'i yid kyis bcom
229b6: ldan 'das la phyag byas te/ 'di skad ces gsol to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyang rang rang gi snying po bcom ldan 'das la 'bul lo// de nas bcom ldan 'das kun tu bzang po chen pos de bzhin gsheg
229b7: pa thams cad la dge'o zhes bde ba chen po'i tshul gyis rab tu spro bar mdzad do/ / dge'o dge'o rgyal ba kun// dge'o dge'o rgyal ba mchog/ dge'o dge'o legs pa'i las// dge'o dge'o sngon 'gro ba// dge'o dge'o

244a5: 'gyur/ / mchog gi bcing pa 'di kun dang // 'di yis las rnams thams cad dang // yid la bsam pa byed pa 'thog// phan tshun du ni mgu byed cing // mgu bas dngos grub myur du 'brog// rdo rje thal mo mnyam sbyar te// rdo rje bkug nas sbom
244a6: bo srung / / ga mdzod kyi rdul du gtang // dga' byed mchog ni phyag rgya 'di// sangs rgyas 'bras bu dngos grub 'thobag// rgyal srid nor dang 'bru yi rnams// de bzhin nor bu 'di dngos thug de ni de mthag ta yang // lha dang lha min mchod//
244a7: par 'gyur// dag nyid kyis ni 'di ba cings te// mkhas pa yis ni dus mtshams phyid// gnas ldang rab sbyor ba yis// spyi bor dbang ni bsrung byas na// rdo rje badzin pakun gyi dang // de nas de nings par 'gyur/ log
244a8: tsam du mnyam sbyor bas/ / phan tshun du ni dbang bskang bas// khams gsum ba gyes bdag po ru// blo ldan rdo rje mig yang 'gyur// de nyid 'khor lo bsong byas te// snying khar 'khor lo bzhin du bskor// zla ba gcig tsam mnyam

244b1: sbyorabs/ / 'khor lo bskor ba rab tu bsgrag// de nyid g.yon par rabasbyar te// rgyal mtshan tshul du yang dag sde// zhag bdun du ni mnyam gzhag pas// 'jig rten du ni rgyal bar 'gyur// de nyid kha nas bkang bar sbyar// mnyam
244b2: bzhag zlab gcig tsam gyis/ / las rnams thams cad rab grub pa// bgang ba tsam gyis byed par 'gyur// thal mo de nyid mnyam bzhag ste// rtse mkha byed rnam bsgyur bas// som po za bar rnam byas te// lo ma lhag ma byas paraH/
244b3: rnal 'byor 'di ni bcings pa yis// sdig pa kun las rab tu grol// bsod nams chen pos byin rlob ste// bde byed thams cad grub par 'gyur// thal mo de nyid snying khar sbyar// mchog dang khro ma gnyis sbyar te// de gnyis tshig gsum
244b4: rab tu dgug/ sbom po dkyil mo tsam du bya// rnal 'byor dag tu sbyor ba yis// 'di yis zla ba gcig byas na// 'jig rtenanagasum las nam rgyal jer// dpa' bo chen por de 'gyur ro// thal mo de nyid mnyam sbyar te/ rang gi cing
244b5: khar bskor bar bya/ / de nas sngags mkhan chos ston par// mi g.yeng sems kyis de 'gyur ro// sbom po lde yi tshul bzhag pas// de nyid khar ni rnam gzhag na// 'jig rten kun gyi thams cad dag/ mdor na zhag bdun tsam gyis kyang //

245a1: pa las kun byed/ / thal mo nyid ni bcings byas nas// rdo rje gnyis ni pad mor sbyor// sdom pa'i zur ni sbrel nas kyang // chung ngu gnyis kyang de bzhin te// mgrin pa nas ni rtse mo brkyang // thams cad las ni sbyar byas te/ 'di
245a2: yis gdug pa thams cad dag/ rab tu sbyar bas 'jigs par 'gyur// thal mo de nyid mnyam gzhag nas// bcing bdam pos bcing bar bya// sbom po gnyis ni nang du gzhug/ khro mo gnyis kyang bskul bar bya// 'di yis gdug
245a3: pa thams cad dag/ 'dzums par rab tu byas par 'gyur// skad cig du ni gnod byed de// de bzhin bsdus dang btsir bar 'gyur// phyag rgya 'di yis rgyas btab pas// de nas dngos grub thams cad kyi// dngos grub chen po bdag po dang
245a4: thams cad las don 'grub par 'gyur/ / phyag rgya 'di yis rgyas btab pas// rim par myur du 'gro 'ong byed// lo gcig gi ni sbyor ba yis// las rnams thams cad sgrub par byed// rdo rje nal 'byor ma rnams kun gyi las

245b1: gnon par byed/ / ho ho zhes pas mnyas par byed// ha hang zhes pas bsrung bar byed// hUM hUM zhes pas gsod par byed// hu hra zhes pas mgu bar byed// ji sri pa ga shab byed tu zung ma phre byed / gi zhes pa 'i byed// r-i

245b5: cho ga'i rim pa rnams/ / rdzu 'phrul tho yi che ba che// dngos grub thams cad grub pa yis// sngags rgyal khyod kyis bshad du gsol// de nas bcom ldan sangs rgyas rnams// thams cad bdag po rgyal po che// thog ma med nas spyod

246a1: gsung thugs rdo rje/ / bde ba chen po'i 'byin mdzad de// skal ldan nye bar longs spyod kun// bud med thams cad dbang du byed// rang 'byung mtshan du thig le ste// bcu gsum dra ba dbu ru ldan// 'di yis bud med bskyed byas te// sa bon//

246a4: gzugs nyid du/ / de ste sa bon gzhag par bya// de nyid de nyid thabs kyi gnas// sngags kyi sbyor ba rab sbyor bas// de nas sngags mkhan der 'grub po// de nyid sngags dang snying po dang // phyag rgya rig dang mi ldan pas// sangs rgyas rdo rje sems

249b1: rje dang / chu bdag dang / lus srul po dang / tshangs pa dang / gtogs 'dod dang / dbang phyug chen po dang / lha mo dang / skal ba dang ldan pa dang / sal ba dang mi ldan pa dang / dngos po dang / dngos po med pa dang / mtshan dang / rdo rje dang / pad mo dang / rin
249b2: po che dang / ral gri dang / tho ba dang / dbyig pa dang / rtse gsum pa dang / 'khor lo dang / sbyor ba dang / rab tu sbyor ba dang / stong pa dang / stong pa chen po dang / mchog tu spong pa dang // shin du stong pa dang / stod pa rab tu stod pa dang / byang chub dang /
