249b7: 'gyur/ / 'dod chags bral ba ji ltar bde// gang gis zhe sdang rdo rje che/ gang gis gti mug rgyal ba che/ gang gis 'dod chags pad mod 'gyur/ gang gis nga rgyal nam mkha'i bdag/ gang gis phrag dog gdon mi za/ byang chub
249b8: sems ni ji ltar bde/ / gang gis bde byed mchod par 'gyur// mchod pa yis ni ji ltar 'gru ba ji ltar gzungs dang mnyam sbyor bas yi ge mchog ni 'grub par 'gyur// ji ltar 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga/ bsnyen pa yis ni

250a1: myur du 'gug ji ltar gsang ba mnyam sbyor bas/ / rmad du byung ba'i dbang bskur 'gyur/ ji ltar pad mo mnyam stor bas/ dkyil 'khor rab tu zhugs par 'gyur// ji ltar dri byang chub dang / khrag dang dang mad chen po yis/ dpa
250a2: tshig nyid du rnga ltar 'gyur/ ji ltar btung ba rab tu brtag/ de nas bcom ldan 'das shin du dgyes pa chen po'i bdag po kun du bzang po chen pos rdo rje pha rol tu phyin ma'i gsang ba tshan med dag thams cad la rang gi bdebs mnyas par byas
250a3: ma mnyam pa dang mnyam pa'i bras pa chen po shin du sam pa mchog tu gsang ba'i dris lan can pa nyid kyi su dang gsung dang thugs rdo rda las byung ngo / / na song gsum gyi 'jigs pad nga/ mams can nyon mongs snang byed pas/ de cir dan rdo rjes zhe sdang zhes
250a4: ni bsgrags pa yin/ ngan song 'jigs pa chen po ru/ sems can thams cad rmongs byed pas/ de phyir 'di ni gti mug ste// rtag pa thub pa mchog yin no// zabs dang shes rab tshul nyid kyis// 'gro ba thams cad dga' byed cing / pad ma'i tshul tu rabartogs
250a5: byi dpyir 'dod chags zhes bya'o/ / de chen sbyin pa'i sprin gyis ni/ sems can thams cad rgyal skyed// nam mkha'i bde ba bsdus pa'i phyir/ de phyir ma'a'achan dargyal yin/ ro la sogs pa'i mnyam sbyor bas/ khrag dag rdo rje gdon migasna tshogs pad mar
250a6: 'jug phyir/ de yi phyi ri ni sna tshogs che/ 'dod chags bral ba dga' med phyir/ bdag ni rab dgyes sbas pa che/ 'dod pa ma gtog bde byed med/ bde che 'dod pa yin no// 'dod chags med par byang chub med/ byang chub med na'ang 'dod chags med/ sdig pa'i
250a7: dang na chags thal te/ sangs rgyas bde mchog mnyes byed pas/ 'dod chags 'dod las bde byed kyi// bde ba mchog tu mad 'byung 'gyur/ byang chub sems med pa byed gzhan/ 'jig rten gsum po 'dir med do// thams cad byang chub sems go/
250a8: bde bkun gyis tshim par 'gyur// zhes pa ni rdo rjer bshad// ti zhes pa ni gzungs ma'i mchog/ tsi zhes pa ni zag par bgad// zhes pa ni bad pa che// mchod pa med pas bde byed med/ de ba med pas mgu pa med// mgubs dngos grub

250b1: thob par 'gyur/ / grub na bde byed rtag pa yi// phyag na rdo rje bde ba che// 'dod pa'i bde bas mchod byed cing // tshe 'di nyid la 'thob par 'gyur// bde ba kun gyi gzhir gyur pa'o// chos kyi dbyings ni rnam par 'dzin// rdo rje 'dzin phyir gzungs/
250b2: ma ste// hri zhes pa ni pad mo 'dzin// 'di dang mnyam par sbyor ba yis// yi ge myur du 'grub par 'gyur// 'dod pa lnga yi yon tan kun// rdzogs sangs rgyas kyis sprul pa ste// sangs rgyas rnams dang rdo rje 'dzin// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma'i
250b3: longs spyod de/ / de byir 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga// de yis bsnyen na grub par 'gyur// sngags kyi sku 'dzin dpal dang ldan// dbang phyug mchog gis sngags rgyal lo// rdo rje sems kyi thugs las skyes// mtshan can mchog tu sbas par
250b4: bshad/ / de dang mnyam du sbyor ba yis// mchog gi dbang ni bskur bar 'gyur// pad mo'i dkyil 'khor zhes bya ba// dkyil 'khor thams cad sgrub par byed// blo ldan de ru zhugs 'gyur na// dam tshig sbas pa tshogs kyi rnams//
250b5: dri chu byang chub dmar po'i mchog/ sha chen sbrang rtsi mar nyid kyis// lus la kun du khyab gnas te// de yi phyir ni dam tshig cha// dam tshig 'di yis dngos grub ste// dam tshig yi ger ldan pa yis// sbyor ces sbyar dang bskyed byas na// zang
250b6: bo dngos grub thob par 'gyur/ / de nas pha rol phyin ma kun// pad mo'i gzigs brgyas pa yis// dzum bcas g.yon nas gar mdzad cing // rtag pa la ni yang gsol ba// rigs ni rnam pa ru ru bstan// ji ltar sbas pa gsum zhes bgyi/
250b7: sna tshogs chen po de dag kun// bde la gnas pas bshad du gsol// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gnyis su med pa'i mnyam pa nyid kyi bde ba chen po zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/
250b8: de nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mchog tu gsang ba pha rol tu phyin ma'i de kho na nyid rab tu phyung ngo // de nyid sbyor ba bcom ldan 'das// rdo rje sems dpa' don chen sbyin// rigs kyi khyad par lnga

251a1: rnams kyis/ / spyod bcas mi spyod rnams la rol// rtag pa mi bstod rin chen mchog/ 'jig dbang gdon mi za gru ba rnams// rigs ni rnam pa brgyad bstan te// mdor bsdus nanam palnga// lus dang ga dang yid rnams kyis// byang ba sa
251a2: theg pa rnam pa gsum/ / de nyid gsum po rdo rje mda'// bde ba'i gnas la rol pa mdzad// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mchog tu ngo mtshar du gyur te// rang gi sdom pa gsol ba 'debs so// sdom pa dngos grug
251a3: kun sbyin pa/ / brtul zhugs bka' thub sngags mkhan gyi// dam tshig mchog tu bsrung ba'i rnams// bcom ldan gsang ba nyid kyis gsungs// de nas bcom ldan 'das kun du bzang po chen po mchog tu shin du dgyes pa'i bde ba la mngon par
251a4: chags pas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsol ba btab pas mkhyen te/ / zhal rab tu bzhad pas rgyas nas nyid kyi sku dang // gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las 'di byung ngo // sku dang gsung dang thugs sbas pas// nan tan du ni bsrung bar bya//
251a5: bsrungs pa yis ni bsod nams che// dngos grub shin du skye bar 'gyur// de ni 'di yis rgya che ba'i// yid kyis kha dog dbyings chen gyi// phyag rgya bcings la sogs pas btab// sbas pa'i sku ni rab bsgrub bya// rdo rje gsung du rab sbyor bas// chos kyi ngo
251a6: bo phyag rgya brjod/ / ngag sbas gsang bar brjod pa ni// nga ro spangs pa rdo rje'i gsung // rang sems rab tu 'bigs pa yis// zla ba rdo rje rnam par bsgom// rang bzhin gsum po gcig tu bsgom// 'di ni yid sbas chen po yin// 'di ni de nyid rgya chen mchog
251a7: rgyun du bsgom pa rnams byas te/ / gsum bsgoms pas ni 'grub par 'gyur// gzhan min rdo rje 'dzin gyis gsungs// sras gsum la sogs cho ga yis// phyag rgya thams cad rgyas btab ste// de bas nan tan thams cad kyis// rdzas
251a8: gsum rnam par sla bar bya/ / rdo rje mchog 'dzin chen po dang // gtso bo chen pos byin gyis rlob// blun po gang gis 'das byas na// rdo rje 'dzin pa skad cig 'jig/ sems dpa' che dang bral gyur na/ ngan song gsum du yang dang yang / ji

251b1: tsam nam mkha'i dkyil 'khor ba/ / shin du mi bzad smin par 'gyur// de nas dam tshig de dag kun// rdo rje 'dzin la mgu gyur te// 'jam po'i phyag gis gar mdzad cing // g.yon gyis phyag byas slar gsol ba// gar dbang rnam
251b2: gnon gar mdzad cing / / mtha' yas phyag ni bcu pa'i bsgyings pa yis// pad ma'i lo ma 'jam po brgyad dbye nas// gnyis min bde bar rdo rje 'jog mdzad de// sbas pa de nyid mi mnyams par gyur// rdo rje 'dam skyes zla ba
251b3: yang dga'adra/ / thabs dang shes rab dgyes pa bde byed sogs// bde gshegs rnams kyi sbas pa nyid kyis shod// sbyor dang sbyor ma yang dag sbyor// zhi ba'i thal mo mchog tu bde// 'dod pa lnga yi yon tan 'grub// sangs rgyas byang chub
251b4: rab bsgrubs pa'o/ / de nas bcom ldan dam tshig rgyal// rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba che// de nyid sbas pa bskul ba yis// sbas pa ma lus 'chang bar mdzad// rdo rje pa mo mnyam sbyor bas// cho gar ldan pas gang dbang bskur
251b5: bde bar 'dod pa'i slob dpon gyis/ / de nyid 'di ni de las bstan// 'di la khrus med nyes pa med// dka' thub med de dka' ba'ang med// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// de nyid sbyor bas 'grub par 'gyur// lus
251b6: rang ngag sems rdo rje yi/ / rdo rje sems dpa' nyid du 'gyur// rdo rje dbab pa skyes gyur na// ji tsam 'dod par nam mkha' 'phur// snying khar rdo rje khu tshur bcings// rdo rje lta bas rnam bltas te// dgyes pa'i tshul gyis bsnyen
251b7: byas na/ / rdo rje sems dpa' skad cig 'gyur// rnam sgeg dgyes pa'i rnam gnon pas// rab dgyes sar ni 'gro byed de// sangs rgyas bde ba chen po dang // grub pa yis kyang mchod byed cing // rdo rje sems dpa'i rgya che mchog
251b8: 'gying ba'i longs pas gar byed pas/ / bde byed zla ba'i 'od 'dra zhing // las kyi khyad par la sogs gnon// sbas pa'i gar gyis gar byas pas// sbas pa sbyor ba'i bdag nyid 'grub// sna tshogs dkyil 'khor gar byed cing //

252a1: lag pa mang po rnam bskur dang // phyir 'bying dbyibs su ldan pa dang // khro bar dri med lta ba yis// gdul dka' gnon pa 'jigs byed pa'i// 'jig rten gsum po nam rgyal 'gyur// me 'bar nyi ma'i dbus nyid du/
252a2: khro bo hUM mdzad bsgom byas na// myur du 'jig rten don bsgrub phyir// 'jig rten gsum po nam rgyal 'gyur// lha mo bzhi dang mnyam sbyor bas// su ra ta s+t+wa~M zhes smra zhing // har thig le tshul sbyar na// rab dgyes de ma thag tu
252a3: 'gyur/ / rab dgyes mchog tu btag pa yid// sa chen rnal 'byor 'gro 'gyur te// lha mo bzhi dang 'grogs pa yis// sems can rnams kyi don kun byed// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad bde ba chen
252a4: po la phyag bzhes nas gsol pa/ / thal mo yang dag sbyar byas te// phyag rgya de nyid nyid kyis shod// rdo rje mchog la gsol ba 'debs// bde ba'i bdag nyid mchod pa shod// gzugs dang sgra dang dri che dang // ro dang reg pa yid
252a5: 'ong ba/ / thugs rje chen pos bsgrubs pa yis// dpa' bo chen po nyid kyis shong // de nas bcom ldan par byed che// rdo rje sems dpa' bdag po che// phyag rgya bcing pa bde ba che// de nyid mchog ni bshad par mdzad// dang po chos kyi
252a6: phyag rgya ste/ / gnyis pa dam tshig phyag rgya yin// gsum la phyag rgya chen po ste// bzhi pa las kyi phyag rgyar bshad// de nas su gsung bugs do rje// ji ltar 'ching bzhin sgom bya ba// sna tshogs ye shes rjes su dag/ sna tshogs
252a7: chen pos 'chad par mdzad/ / rtag pa'i su ni ser po ste// mi bskyod rdo rje dkar po yin// nam mkha'i snying po mthing kaN// tshe dpag med pa pad modam pa// sgra tshogs kha dog rgya che mchog/ 'od zer phreng ba rmad byung ba la// gdon ma
252a8: zab rdo rjeH/ / don chen byed pa bsam par bya// nga rang rigs kyi gnas nyid du// myang dun ma mkha' 'ag byed cing // rigs kyi lha mo bzhi rnams kyis// rol pa dang ni mchod par byed// tshogs sbyor ba bdade che ba'i// lham pazhi

252b1: dang mnyam skor ba/ / rdo rje sbyor bdag bsgoms byas na// rdo rje sems dpa' bdag nyid 'gyur// rdo rje sems sogs sems dpa' mchog/ rdo rje la sogs gdan bzhugs pa pa/ rang gi 'khor lo mchog gis brgyan// rang gi
252b2: phyag rgyar gnas par bsam/ / pad mo'i gdan gyi tshul gyis ni// brtse dang ldan pas bsgom byas te// snying po sbas don gang byas pas// sbas pa che la bde byed na// 'gyeng ba'i bde bar ldan pa yi// rdo rje chen po de 'grub ste// sna
252b3: tshogs dkyil 'khor rab nye bar/ / sna tshogs chen po 'gro bar 'gyur// bde ba chen po thams cad 'grub pa'i sbyor ba chen po'i bde ba zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya rab tu rgyas pa'o// // de nas phyag rgya bcing bshad de// tag la sogs
252b4: pa'i de kho na/ / gang gis myur du bcings pa yis// sangs rgyas dngos grub bde cher 'gro// thabs ni g.yas kyi logs su bya// de bzhin shes rab g.yon par te// zhi ba'i thal mo gsum nyid kyis// sbyor ba'i tshul gyis bsdu
252b5: par bya/ / sor mo thams cad par bar du// mnyam du sbyor bas byed par sbyin// rdo rje yi ni thal mo 'dis// sangs rgyas thams cad nyid du bsgrub// 'di ni bcings pa tsam gyis kyang // nam mkha'i snying po'i gnas su 'gro// 'di nyid
252b6: shin du bcings pa yis/ / gsum du sbyor bas mchod par bya// de nyid las ni sor mo kun// kun du bskums te bcing par bya// rdo rje'i bcing ba bsdus pas ni// bcing ba ldan par rnam bsgyur te// de nyid sbom po rab bcug nas// khro mo'i rtsemo//
252b7: rab tu dgug/ 'di ni rdo rje rigs kyi bcing // rdo rje sems dpa' nyid 'grub byed// de bzhin bcing ba rnam bzhag ste// sbom po khro mo'i rtse mo sbyar// 'di ni bcing babacing ba che// nam mkhar 'gro ba nye bar sgrub// de nyid bcing babacing byas te// khro mo gnyis po
252b8: mtshan bzhin du/ / rtse mo sprad de dgug bya pa// bcing ba 'di yis pad mo bathub// bcing ba de nyid rab tu sbom// bde bar bcug nas bsdam byas te// las kyi bcing ba sbyor ba yis// don yod mchog gi rigs su 'gro// bcing ba de nyid bcing byas te//

253a1: sbom dang khro mo'i rtse mo sbyar// g.yas pa'i sbom po rdo rje yis// de yi dbu su bcug bya ba// nga 'di bcing ba chen po ste// rab dgyes ro ni sgrub byed pa// gang gis bcings pa tsam gyis ni// rab tu dgyes pa nyid 'thob bo// dngos
253a2: grub thams cad bde ba che/ / de yis 'di tshe 'thob 'gyur te// phyag brgya bcing ba'i cho ga yis// sangs rgyas thams cad rab tu gnas// phyag rgya bcing ba'i ye shes rnam par rgyas pa'o// bcing ba lnga yi cho ga yis// gcig gis rnal
253a3: 'byor bsgrub mi bya/ / drug ni sbyor bas sbyor byas na// de ma thag tu rab dgyes 'gyur// bcing ba lnga yi phyag rgya'o// de bzhin bcing ba gnyis byas te// g.yon gyi snying khar bcing bar bya// g.yas kyi rtse mo bsgred byas te// rdo rje'i tshul gcu
253a4: bar bya/ / phyag rgya 'di ni byang chub bde// sangs rgyas thams cad gcig tu bsgrub// gdon mi za bar tshe 'di la// rtag pa 'dra ba thob par byed// g.yon pa de nyid snying khar bzhag/ g.yas pa sa la reg byas pas/ sa la bde ba rol pa
253a5: yis/ / 'di yis mi zad 'thob par 'gyur// de bzhin snying khar g.yon pa bzhag/ lag pa g.yas par ba sbyin bya// 'di yis rin chen skal ldan sogs// nam mkha' nye bar 'grub par 'gyur// de bzhin g.yon pa snying khar gzhag/
253a6: g.yas kyang gzhag ste ting 'dzin gnas// 'di yis tshe dpag med pa nyid// tshe 'di nyid la 'thob par 'gyur// de bzhin g.yon pa snying khar sbyar// lag pa g.yas pa mi 'jigs sbyin// 'jigs pa ma lus rab sgrol ba// sdig pa gdug
253a7: pa'ajigs pa che/ / 'di yis thams cad 'phrog par byed// gdon mi za ba'i nges pa yi// / de ni chen po'i chen por 'gyur// de nyid bcing ba gnyis byas te// g.yon pa g.yon du sbyor bar bya// g.yas ni snying khar gzung byas te//
253a8: brjid pas rab tu bzhad cing gnas// bde ba chen po thabs gnas pas// 'di yis rab dgyes nyid 'gyur te// bde mchog nyid du bsgrub pa po// tshe 'di nyid la the tsom med// de bzhin bcing babacing byas te// sbyor dang ldan pas brtan

253b1: bar bya/ / sbom po'i rtse mo pad mo'i gnas// g.yon gyi khro mo'i rtse mor sbyar// g.yas pa yi ni sbom po yis// mngon sum rdo rjer byas pa yis// bcug nas bde ba spyod bya zhing // skad cig skad cig bsdam par bya// de 'di sangs rgyas thams cad
253b2: kyi/ / dgyes pa dgyes mchog sgrub pa po// 'di ni bcings pa tsam gyis kyang // yang dag rdo rje dgyes pa 'thob// rab dgyes pa de mchog longs spyod kyi// btsun mo dngos grub nyid du 'gyur// g.yas ni mtshan mas drang byas te// lcags kyu'i tshul du
253b3: gzhag par bya/ / rdo rje 'dod ma lugs kyu ste// rdo rje 'dod byed btsun mo yi// dang por 'dren pa de nyid gzhag/ tha mar ha ra thig ler bya// rdo rje dgyes pa bde 'thob byed// ming ni dbus su bri bar bya// 'di yis snying khar byas pa yis// de bzhin
253b4: gshegs pa bde mchog 'gro/ / phyag rgya bzhi dang 'grogs pa yis// lus 'dis tshe 'di 'grub par 'gyur// rab dgyes sbyor bar yang dag ldan// phyag rgya bzhi dang mnyam 'grogs shing // rdo rje 'gyid la sogs sprod pas// rnal 'byor 'di ni
253b5: bcings pa yis/ / rab dgyes la sogs ma lus pa// rab gyes rol bsgyings ma yis// skad cig nyid du 'dren par 'gyur// de bzhin sbom mo'i rtse mor sbyar// snying rje chen po der bzhag pa// skal pa chen po rdo rje sun// de nyid don kun ston byed/
253b6: ma// 'di ni yang dag bcings pa yis// rdo rje rtag pa'i spyan du 'gyur// yod dang med pa rnams spangs pa// dngos po thams cad mthong bar 'gyur// rdo rje'i bal mo brtan bya ste// khro mo rtse mo zlum po yi// mngon por mtshan dang 'dra byas te// blom
253b7: bor rdo rje btan pa che/ de 'di bcom ldan 'das ma mchog/ rdo rje pad mo'i bde 'thob byed// rnal 'byor 'di ni bcings pa yis// sbas pa chen po'i dgyes pa 'bog/ de nas lha mo chen mo dag/ spro ba chen pos gar mdzad ci// rdo rje bde byed bdag nyid la//
253b8: bdud dang bcas pas phyag byas te// chos kyi yi ge thabs gnas nas// de nyid chos kyi gsol ba 'debs// chos kyi phyag rgya bde ba che// rdo rje bcom ldan bshad du gsol// sgrub pa pos ni rab bsgrims na// gang gis lha ni 'grub par 'gyur// gang

254a1: gis myur dbyin pa rlabs pas/ / sangs rgyas kyang nabar ba bsgrub ste// bde byed gnyis kyis sgo cha ga/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gnas 'jug 'gyur// de nas bcom ldan 'das lha mo thams cad kyis gsol ba btabab mabyen
254a2: nas/ tid kyi su dang gsung dang zla smras pa las chos kyi phyag rgya chen pa'i tshig 'di byung // bcu gsum bdag nyid 'dren pa te// thig le lta ni yang dag ldan kha ma hang ga la gnas/ btud kyis pa rdo rje kyes/ rting bar phyag tu 'a
254a3: byas nas/ / dga' byed lhan cig rkyen byed cing // spyod dang mi spyod 'grub 'gyur te/ rnal 'byor bde ba chen por 'gro// de bzhin 'dren pa thog mar bya// rdo rje 'dod pa skyob mchog/ har thig le yang dag ldan// cha gnyis gsum pa sbyar byas pa// 'di ni
254a4: snying kar bzhag byas na/ / bde bar nam mkhar 'gro 'gyur te// bde ba shin du rtag pa yi// 'di yis mchog tu dngos grub po// 'dren pa de nyid thog mar gzhag/ ltos ltos zhes pa hUM dang ldan// skal pa chen po rdo rje spyan// dbus su bskul bas 'grub
254a5: par 'gyur/ / 'phrul gyi spyan lnga nor che ba// 'di yis rnal 'byor 'grub 'gyur te/ rdo rje byang chub gyes pa che// sangs rgyas thams cad mthong bar 'gyur// nga por 'dren pa de nyid gzhag/ tha mar har thig ler bya// rdo rje dgyes pa bde 'jol
254a6: byed/ / ming ni dbras su bri bar bya// 'di yis snying khar byas pa yis// de bzhin gshegs pa pa mchog 'gro// phyag rgya bzhi dang 'grogs pa yis// lus 'das 'di tshe 'grub par 'gyur// yang gyes sbyor bar yang dgazhon/ phyag rgya bzhi
254a7: dang mnyam 'grogs shing / / rdo rje 'gyid la sogs sprod pas// bcom ldan 'dod ma 'grub par 'gyur// chos kyi de kho na nyid kyi don gyi ye shes kyi phyag rgya'o// de nas bcom ldan sbyor ba che// thog ma tha ma med pa mchog/ gdug pa thams
254a8: cad gdul ba'i phyir/ / rdo rje khro bor de 'gyur ro// mdun du thog ma'i lha nyid du// rdo rje hU~M mdzad nyi ma 'bar// nyi ma bcu gnyis gzi brjid che// ma 'bar rab tu 'bar bar ldan// 'khor gyi 'khor lo da dag kun/ dung khrod kyi ni rgyan mchog

254b1: gis/ / brgyan ta gdug pa'i tshogs rnams la// de ni yang dag rol pa mdzad// khro chen mchog 'dral phyag rgya 'di// sngags ni rang gi snying khar bsgom// khro mo'i bu mos bdun du bskor// khro ma chen modas 'grub bo// 'di yis gdug pa thams
254b2: cad rnams/ / hUM byas myur du brgyal bar 'gyur// de dag gdug pa gdug pa che// 'jigs shing 'khrugs te rab tu 'jig/ skyobs shig skyobs shig ces smra zhing// rdo rje gcol dran par byed// phyag rgya 'di ni mnyam par gzhag/ 'gro ba thams
254b3: cad dba' bya ste/ / las mchog thams cad sgrub pa pos// dgra yi rnams ni gzhig par bya// sbyor dang ldan pas 'bum bzlas te// las rnams thams cad byed pa na// gdon me za bar kun 'gyur te/ rdo rje sems dpa 'ang bsgrub par nus/
254b4: zhes bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje sems dpa'as gsungs so// tho bo'i phyag rgya'i ye shes so// de nas sangs rgyas che de dag/ sangs rgyas nyid skyes thams cad mchog/ gzungs ma rnal 'byor ma thams cad// rang gi 'khor gyi 'khor la'i
254b5: tshogs/ / phan tshun bde ba ldan pa yi// dga' bas 'khor rnams 'phags 'gyur te// rang gi bde byed skyes par 'brel// skal pa chen mo tshon par byed// de nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje shin du dgyes pa chen pos rang gi 'khor gyi 'khor la'i tshigs rnams la yang
254b6: dang yang du gzigs te/ / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'dren pa'i rig ma'i snying po 'dis sdud pa mdzad do// oM badz+ra a~M kra sha du ru dra ru/ e h+ye hi kang d+ha bi kad b+h+ya/ sa dran par shad tsakras na tsal/ badz+ra e ku sha hUM phaT/ 'di yi phyag rgya rdo rje 'i/ tsang
254b7: bganyis ni dam byas te/ rdo rje khro mo dgrol bar bya// rdo rje khro bar basbyang ba/ rdo rje'i kyo bzhes bya'o// gro dang ri ba sems can rnamam// phyag rgya 'di yis kun bkrugs// 'dod pas 'byid pa'i med rngag rnams/ mi yi du mi smos ci dgos// rdo rje bcings pa
254b8: mnyam gzhag ste/ / g.yon gyi steng du de bzhin bzhag/ dbus su sbom mo bzhag par bya// rdo rje 'den pa gzi brjid che// rdo rje bcing ba bsdam byas te// rdo rje sbom mo rtse mo spang / bdag ni rdo rje zhes bsgom zhing / cing ba de ni dgrol bar bya// de nyid bcing ba dam

255a1: byas te/ / dbang dang chu ngu'i rtsa ba'i mtshams// rdo rje sbom po nub byas te// rab dgyes bdag nyid bskyod par bya// de las rdo rje mchog gnyis bskyed// mdung pa'i tshul du sbyar bar bya// gzhug pa dang ni
255a2: 'dren pa'i mchog/ 'di yis thams cad dngos grub pas// rnal 'byor phyag rgya 'di nyid kyis// drangs te bcu gnas bcings byas te// dbang du byas nas bsgrub par bya// de nas de dag thams cad drangs bcug bcings dga'/
255a3: ba skyes nas/ rang gi rab tu dgyes pa'i bde ba chen pos rang gis rgyal srid rjes su skyong zhing rdo rje chos la bka' stsal pa/ sangs rgyas kun gyi tshul chen po// dga' byed zla gsang thig le yi// rab dgyes bdag nyid gsang ba 'di/
255a4: sems dpa' chen po khyod kyis bzung // de nas gdan las myur bzhengs te// thal mo sbyar te phyag bzhes nas// chos kyi ngo bor tshig smras pa// bde ba chen po bdag gis blangs// rang bde longs spyod gar byas te// rdo rje che
255a5: yis 'di skad smras/ / rdo rje chos na sna tshogs che// sna tshogs pad mo gar rab byed// de nas pha rol phyin te kun// rab dgyes longs spyod gar byed cing // bde byed chen po'i bdag nyid rje// legs pazhes pa sbyin byed de/
255a6: legs so legs so bde ba che// legs so legs so ye shes che// legs so legs so sna tshogs che// legs so legs so dgyes pa che// bcom ldan 'das dgyes pa'i thugs kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/
255a7: pha rol phyin ma'i 'khor chen mo de dag mngon par dga' bar gyur to// zla gsang thig le zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po che po mo// gsang ba yongs su rdzogs s+ho// // zhus chen gyis lo ts+tsha ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos
255a8: sbyar cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ ye d+harmA he tu pra b+ha wa he tun+te ShAn+ta thA ga to h+ya bA data/ teSh+Thany+tsa yo ni ro d+ha e bam+b+ha dI ma hA shra ma NaH/ bkra shis 'bar gyur cig/ sems can mas
